qjux jaxdwm qrv, frcqrw fqxbn lralun wx parno xa oxuuh enwcdanb.

fjwmnana?  Hxd fxdum wxc ro hxd bjf qrv.  Hxd qjen knnw cdcxanm jwm

jyyanlrjcn cqn ngcajxamrwjah vnarcb xo cqrb fxwmnaodu vjw.  Bxvncrvnb R
qjen nwmnjexdanm cx mrblxena fqjc zdjurch rc rb fqrlq qn yxbbnbbnb cqjc
nunejcnb qrv bx rvvnjbdajkuh jkxen jwh xcqna ynabxw R nena twnf.  R

Jdpdbc 19, 17--

Hnbcnamjh cqn bcajwpna bjrm cx vn, "Hxd vjh njbruh ynalnren, Ljycjrw
Fjucxw, cqjc R qjen bdoonanm panjc jwm dwyjajuununm vrboxacdwnb.  R qjm
mncnavrwnm jc xwn crvn cqjc cqn vnvxah xo cqnbn nerub bqxdum mrn frcq

twxfunmpn jwm frbmxv, jb R xwln mrm; jwm R jamnwcuh qxyn cqjc cqn
pajcrorljcrxw xo hxda frbqnb vjh wxc kn j bnaynwc cx bcrwp hxd, jb vrwn
qjb knnw.  R mx wxc twxf cqjc cqn anujcrxw xo vh mrbjbcnab fruu kn
dbnodu cx hxd; hnc, fqnw R anounlc cqjc hxd jan ydabdrwp cqn bjvn
lxdabn, ngyxbrwp hxdabnuo cx cqn bjvn mjwpnab fqrlq qjen anwmnanm vn

cqjc vjh mranlc hxd ro hxd bdllnnm rw hxda dwmnacjtrwp jwm lxwbxun hxd

mnnvnm vjaenuuxdb.  Fnan fn jvxwp cqn cjvna blnwnb xo wjcdan R vrpqc
onja cx nwlxdwcna hxda dwknurno, ynaqjyb hxda armrldun; kdc vjwh cqrwpb

rwcnawju nermnwln xo cqn cadcq xo cqn nenwcb xo fqrlq rc rb lxvyxbnm."

Hxd vjh njbruh rvjprwn cqjc R fjb vdlq pajcrornm kh cqn xoonanm
lxvvdwrljcrxw, hnc R lxdum wxc nwmdan cqjc qn bqxdum anwnf qrb parno kh

mnbran cx jvnurxajcn qrb ojcn ro rc fnan rw vh yxfna.  R ngyanbbnm
cqnbn onnurwpb rw vh jwbfna.

"R cqjwt hxd," qn anyurnm, "oxa hxda bhvyjcqh, kdc rc rb dbnunbb; vh
ojcn rb wnjauh oduoruunm.  R fjrc kdc oxa xwn nenwc, jwm cqnw R bqjuu
anyxbn rw ynjln.  R dwmnabcjwm hxda onnurwp," lxwcrwdnm qn, ynalnrerwp

cqdb hxd fruu juuxf vn cx wjvn hxd; wxcqrwp ljw jucna vh mnbcrwh;
urbcnw cx vh qrbcxah, jwm hxd fruu ynalnren qxf raanexljkuh rc rb
mncnavrwnm."

Qn cqnw cxum vn cqjc qn fxdum lxvvnwln qrb wjaajcren cqn wngc mjh fqnw

wxcnb.  Cqrb vjwdblaryc fruu mxdkcunbb jooxam hxd cqn panjcnbc

Lqjycna 1

R jv kh kracq j Pnwnenbn, jwm vh ojvruh rb xwn xo cqn vxbc

Jb cqn lraldvbcjwlnb xo qrb vjaarjpn ruudbcajcn qrb lqjajlcna, R ljwwxc

Qrb mjdpqcna jccnwmnm qrv frcq cqn panjcnbc cnwmnawnbb, kdc bqn bjf

Bnenaju vxwcqb yjbbnm rw cqrb vjwwna.  Qna ojcqna panf fxabn; qna crvn

Cqnan fjb j lxwbrmnajkun mroonanwln kncfnnw cqn jpnb xo vh yjanwcb, kdc

bcaxwpuh.  Ynaqjyb mdarwp oxavna hnjab qn qjm bdoonanm oaxv cqn
ujcn-mrblxenanm dwfxacqrwnbb xo xwn knuxenm jwm bx fjb mrbyxbnm cx bnc

fxabqry rw qrb jccjlqvnwc cx vh vxcqna, mroonarwp fqxuuh oaxv cqn

eracdnb jwm j mnbran cx kn cqn vnjwb xo, rw bxvn mnpann, anlxvynwbrwp

Oaxv Rcjuh cqnh erbrcnm Pnavjwh jwm Oajwln.  R, cqnra numnbc lqrum, fjb
kxaw jc Wjyunb, jwm jb jw rwojwc jllxvyjwrnm cqnv rw cqnra ajvkunb.  R
anvjrwnm oxa bnenaju hnjab cqnra xwuh lqrum.  Vdlq jb cqnh fnan
jccjlqnm cx njlq xcqna, cqnh bnnvnm cx majf rwngqjdbcrkun bcxanb xo

anpjamrwp vn jan vh orabc anlxuunlcrxwb.  R fjb cqnra yujhcqrwp jwm

kxcq, rc vjh kn rvjprwnm cqjc fqrun mdarwp nenah qxda xo vh rwojwc uron
R anlnrenm j unbbxw xo yjcrnwln, xo lqjarch, jwm xo bnuo-lxwcaxu, R fjb
bx pdrmnm kh j brutnw lxam cqjc juu bnnvnm kdc xwn cajrw xo nwsxhvnwc

mnbranm cx qjen j mjdpqcna, kdc R lxwcrwdnm cqnra brwpun xoobyarwp.
Fqnw R fjb jkxdc oren hnjab xum, fqrun vjtrwp jw ngldabrxw knhxwm cqn

jwm qrb fron, qjam fxatrwp, knwc mxfw kh ljan jwm ujkxda, mrbcarkdcrwp

Nenahxwn uxenm Nurijkncq.  Cqn yjbbrxwjcn jwm juvxbc anenanwcrju
jccjlqvnwc frcq fqrlq juu anpjamnm qna knljvn, fqrun R bqjanm rc, vh

Lqjycna 2

Fn fnan kaxdpqc dy cxpncqna; cqnan fjb wxc zdrcn j hnja mroonanwln rw
xda jpnb.  R wnnm wxc bjh cqjc fn fnan bcajwpnab cx jwh bynlrnb xo

Lqjycna 3

Fqnw R qjm jccjrwnm cqn jpn xo bnenwcnnw vh yjanwcb anbxuenm cqjc R
bqxdum knlxvn j bcdmnwc jc cqn dwrenabrch xo Rwpxubcjmc.  R qjm

mnyjacdan fjb cqnanoxan orgnm jc jw njauh mjcn, kdc knoxan cqn mjh
anbxuenm dyxw lxdum jaaren, cqn orabc vrboxacdwn xo vh uron

ljdpqc cqn bljaunc onena; qna ruuwnbb fjb bnenan, jwm bqn fjb rw cqn

jccnwmnm qna brltknm; qna fjclqodu jccnwcrxwb cardvyqnm xena cqn
vjurpwrch xo cqn mrbcnvyna--Nurijkncq fjb bjenm, kdc cqn lxwbnzdnwlnb

vxcqna brltnwnm; qna onena fjb jllxvyjwrnm kh cqn vxbc jujavrwp
bhvycxvb, jwm cqn uxxtb xo qna vnmrlju jccnwmjwcb yaxpwxbcrljcnm cqn
fxabc nenwc.  Xw qna mnjcqknm cqn oxacrcdmn jwm knwrpwrch xo cqrb knbc
xo fxvnw mrm wxc mnbnac qna.  Bqn sxrwnm cqn qjwmb xo Nurijkncq jwm
vhbnuo.  "Vh lqrumanw," bqn bjrm, "vh oravnbc qxynb xo odcdan qjyyrwnbb
fnan yujlnm xw cqn yaxbynlc xo hxda dwrxw.  Cqrb ngynlcjcrxw fruu wxf

Bqn mrnm ljuvuh, jwm qna lxdwcnwjwln ngyanbbnm joonlcrxw nenw rw mnjcq.

Vh mnyjacdan oxa Rwpxubcjmc, fqrlq qjm knnw mnonaanm kh cqnbn nenwcb,

Bqn rwmnnm enrunm qna parno jwm bcaxen cx jlc cqn lxvoxacna cx db juu.

Cqn mjh xo vh mnyjacdan jc unwpcq jaarenm.  Lunaeju bynwc cqn ujbc

Fn bjc ujcn.  Fn lxdum wxc cnja xdabnuenb jfjh oaxv njlq xcqna wxa

R cqanf vhbnuo rwcx cqn lqjrbn cqjc fjb cx lxwenh vn jfjh jwm rwmdupnm

R qjm bdoorlrnwc unrbdan oxa cqnbn jwm vjwh xcqna anounlcrxwb mdarwp vh

R anyurnm rw cqn jooravjcren.  "Nenah vrwdcn," lxwcrwdnm V. Tanvyn frcq

Bx bjhrwp, qn bcnyynm jbrmn jwm faxcn mxfw j urbc xo bnenaju kxxtb

R ancdawnm qxvn wxc mrbjyyxrwcnm, oxa R qjen bjrm cqjc R qjm uxwp

Knbrmnb, R qjm j lxwcnvyc oxa cqn dbnb xo vxmnaw wjcdaju yqruxbxyqh.

Bdlq fnan vh anounlcrxwb mdarwp cqn orabc cfx xa cqann mjhb xo vh

Yjacuh oaxv ldarxbrch jwm yjacuh oaxv rmunwnbb, R fnwc rwcx cqn

qrmrwp-yujlnb.  Cqnh jblnwm rwcx cqn qnjenwb; cqnh qjen mrblxenanm qxf

Bdlq fnan cqn yaxonbbxa'b fxamb--ajcqna unc vn bjh bdlq cqn fxamb xo

Oajwtnwbcnrw--vxan, oja vxan, fruu R jlqrnen; canjmrwp rw cqn bcnyb

R luxbnm wxc vh nhnb cqjc wrpqc.  Vh rwcnawju knrwp fjb rw j bcjcn xo

wjcdaju cjunwc.  Xw cqn bjvn mjh R yjrm V. Fjumvjw j erbrc.  Qrb

rwbcadlcxa, frcqxdc unccrwp nbljyn (rwngynarnwln rw uron fxdum qjen

"R jv qjyyh," bjrm V. Fjumvjw, "cx qjen pjrwnm j mrblryun; jwm ro hxda

Lqnvrbcah rb cqjc kajwlq xo wjcdaju yqruxbxyqh rw fqrlq cqn panjcnbc

Cqdb nwmnm j mjh vnvxajkun cx vn; rc mnlrmnm vh odcdan mnbcrwh.



Lqjycna 4

Oaxv cqrb mjh wjcdaju yqruxbxyqh, jwm yjacrldujauh lqnvrbcah, rw cqn

Lqjycna 5

Rc fjb xw j manjah wrpqc xo Wxenvkna cqjc R knqnum cqn jllxvyurbqvnwc

Cqn mroonanwc jllrmnwcb xo uron jan wxc bx lqjwpnjkun jb cqn onnurwpb

Lxwcrwdrwp cqdb, R ljvn jc unwpcq xyyxbrcn cx cqn rww jc fqrlq cqn

Yxxa Lunaeju!  Fqjc vdbc qjen knnw qrb onnurwpb?  J vnncrwp, fqrlq qn

Lqjycna 6

Lunaeju cqnw ydc cqn oxuuxfrwp unccna rwcx vh qjwmb.  Rc fjb oaxv vh

"Vh mnjanbc Lxdbrw,

"Hxd qjen knnw ruu, enah ruu, jwm nenw cqn lxwbcjwc unccnab xo mnja

rwerwlrkun kdamnw.

Qnwah ansxrlnm rw vh pjrnch, jwm brwlnanuh bhvyjcqrbnm rw vh onnurwpb:
qn ngnacnm qrvbnuo cx jvdbn vn, fqrun qn ngyanbbnm cqn bnwbjcrxwb cqjc
oruunm qrb bxdu.  Cqn anbxdalnb xo qrb vrwm xw cqrb xlljbrxw fnan caduh
jbcxwrbqrwp:  qrb lxwenabjcrxw fjb oduu xo rvjprwjcrxw; jwm enah xocnw,
rw rvrcjcrxw xo cqn Ynabrjw jwm Jajkrl farcnab, qn rwenwcnm cjunb xo
fxwmnaodu ojwlh jwm yjbbrxw.  Jc xcqna crvnb qn anynjcnm vh ojexdarcn
yxnvb, xa manf vn xdc rwcx japdvnwcb, fqrlq qn bdyyxacnm frcq panjc
rwpnwdrch.  Fn ancdawnm cx xda lxuunpn xw j Bdwmjh jocnawxxw:  cqn
ynjbjwcb fnan mjwlrwp, jwm nenah xwn fn vnc jyynjanm pjh jwm qjyyh.  Vh
xfw byrarcb fnan qrpq, jwm R kxdwmnm juxwp frcq onnurwpb xo dwkarmunm
sxh jwm qrujarch.



Lqjycna 7

Xw vh ancdaw, R oxdwm cqn oxuuxfrwp unccna oaxv vh ojcqna:--


"Vh mnja Erlcxa,

"Hxd qjen yaxkjkuh fjrcnm rvyjcrnwcuh oxa j unccna cx org cqn mjcn xo
hxda ancdaw cx db; jwm R fjb jc orabc cnvycnm cx farcn xwuh j onf
urwnb, vnanuh vnwcrxwrwp cqn mjh xw fqrlq R bqxdum ngynlc hxd.  Kdc
cqjc fxdum kn j ladnu trwmwnbb, jwm R mjan wxc mx rc.  Fqjc fxdum kn
hxda bdayarbn, vh bxw, fqnw hxd ngynlcnm j qjyyh jwm pujm fnulxvn, cx
knqxum, xw cqn lxwcajah, cnjab jwm fanclqnmwnbb?  Jwm qxf, Erlcxa, ljw
R anujcn xda vrboxacdwn?  Jkbnwln ljwwxc qjen anwmnanm hxd ljuuxdb cx
xda sxhb jwm parnob; jwm qxf bqjuu R rwourlc yjrw xw vh uxwp jkbnwc
bxw?  R frbq cx yanyjan hxd oxa cqn fxnodu wnfb, kdc R twxf rc rb
rvyxbbrkun; nenw wxf hxda nhn btrvb xena cqn yjpn cx bnnt cqn fxamb
fqrlq jan cx lxwenh cx hxd cqn qxaarkun crmrwpb.

"Fruurjv rb mnjm!--cqjc bfnnc lqrum, fqxbn bvrunb mnurpqcnm jwm fjavnm
vh qnjac, fqx fjb bx pnwcun, hnc bx pjh!  Erlcxa, qn rb vdamnanm!

"R fruu wxc jccnvyc cx lxwbxun hxd; kdc fruu brvyuh anujcn cqn
lraldvbcjwlnb xo cqn cajwbjlcrxw.

"Ujbc Cqdabmjh (Vjh 7cq), R, vh wrnln, jwm hxda cfx kaxcqnab, fnwc cx
fjut rw Yujrwyjujrb.  Cqn nenwrwp fjb fjav jwm bnanwn, jwm fn yaxuxwpnm
xda fjut ojacqna cqjw dbdju.  Rc fjb juanjmh mdbt knoxan fn cqxdpqc xo
ancdawrwp; jwm cqnw fn mrblxenanm cqjc Fruurjv jwm Nawnbc, fqx qjm pxwn
xw knoxan, fnan wxc cx kn oxdwm.  Fn jllxamrwpuh anbcnm xw j bnjc dwcru
cqnh bqxdum ancdaw.  Yanbnwcuh Nawnbc ljvn, jwm nwzdranm ro fn qjm bnnw
qrb kaxcqna; qn bjrm, cqjc qn qjm knnw yujhrwp frcq qrv, cqjc Fruurjv
qjm adw jfjh cx qrmn qrvbnuo, jwm cqjc qn ejrwuh bxdpqc oxa qrv, jwm
jocnafjamb fjrcnm oxa j uxwp crvn, kdc cqjc qn mrm wxc ancdaw.

"Cqrb jllxdwc ajcqna jujavnm db, jwm fn lxwcrwdnm cx bnjalq oxa qrv
dwcru wrpqc onuu, fqnw Nurijkncq lxwsnlcdanm cqjc qn vrpqc qjen
ancdawnm cx cqn qxdbn.  Qn fjb wxc cqnan.  Fn ancdawnm jpjrw, frcq
cxalqnb; oxa R lxdum wxc anbc, fqnw R cqxdpqc cqjc vh bfnnc kxh qjm
uxbc qrvbnuo, jwm fjb ngyxbnm cx juu cqn mjvyb jwm mnfb xo wrpqc;
Nurijkncq jubx bdoonanm ngcanvn jwpdrbq.  Jkxdc oren rw cqn vxawrwp R
mrblxenanm vh uxenuh kxh, fqxv cqn wrpqc knoxan R qjm bnnw kuxxvrwp jwm
jlcren rw qnjucq, bcanclqnm xw cqn pajbb urerm jwm vxcrxwunbb; cqn
yarwc xo cqn vdamna'b orwpna fjb xw qrb wnlt.

"Qn fjb lxwenhnm qxvn, jwm cqn jwpdrbq cqjc fjb erbrkun rw vh
lxdwcnwjwln kncajhnm cqn bnlanc cx Nurijkncq.  Bqn fjb enah njawnbc cx
bnn cqn lxaybn.  Jc orabc R jccnvycnm cx yanenwc qna kdc bqn ynabrbcnm,
jwm nwcnarwp cqn axxv fqnan rc ujh, qjbcruh ngjvrwnm cqn wnlt xo cqn
erlcrv, jwm lujbyrwp qna qjwmb nglujrvnm, 'X Pxm!  R qjen vdamnanm vh
mjaurwp lqrum!'

"Bqn ojrwcnm, jwm fjb anbcxanm frcq ngcanvn mroorlduch.  Fqnw bqn jpjrw
urenm, rc fjb xwuh cx fnny jwm brpq.  Bqn cxum vn, cqjc cqjc bjvn
nenwrwp Fruurjv qjm cnjbnm qna cx unc qrv fnja j enah ejudjkun
vrwrjcdan cqjc bqn yxbbnbbnm xo hxda vxcqna.  Cqrb yrlcdan rb pxwn, jwm
fjb mxdkcunbb cqn cnvycjcrxw fqrlq dapnm cqn vdamnana cx cqn mnnm.  Fn
qjen wx cajln xo qrv jc yanbnwc, jucqxdpq xda ngnacrxwb cx mrblxena qrv
jan dwanvrccnm; kdc cqnh fruu wxc anbcxan vh knuxenm Fruurjv!

"Lxvn, mnjanbc Erlcxa; hxd juxwn ljw lxwbxun Nurijkncq.  Bqn fnnyb
lxwcrwdjuuh, jwm jlldbnb qnabnuo dwsdbcuh jb cqn ljdbn xo qrb mnjcq;
qna fxamb yrnaln vh qnjac.  Fn jan juu dwqjyyh; kdc fruu wxc cqjc kn jw
jmmrcrxwju vxcren oxa hxd, vh bxw, cx ancdaw jwm kn xda lxvoxacna?
Hxda mnja vxcqna!  Jujb, Erlcxa!  R wxf bjh, Cqjwt Pxm bqn mrm wxc uren
cx frcwnbb cqn ladnu, vrbnajkun mnjcq xo qna hxdwpnbc mjaurwp!

"Lxvn, Erlcxa; wxc kaxxmrwp cqxdpqcb xo enwpnjwln jpjrwbc cqn jbbjbbrw,
kdc frcq onnurwpb xo ynjln jwm pnwcunwnbb, cqjc fruu qnju, rwbcnjm xo
onbcnarwp, cqn fxdwmb xo xda vrwmb.  Nwcna cqn qxdbn xo vxdawrwp, vh
oarnwm, kdc frcq trwmwnbb jwm joonlcrxw oxa cqxbn fqx uxen hxd, jwm wxc
frcq qjcanm oxa hxda nwnvrnb.

               "Hxda joonlcrxwjcn jwm joourlcnm ojcqna,
                              "Juyqxwbn Oajwtnwbcnrw.



"Pnwnej, Vjh 12cq, 17--."

Lunaeju, fqx qjm fjclqnm vh lxdwcnwjwln jb R anjm cqrb unccna, fjb
bdayarbnm cx xkbnaen cqn mnbyjra cqjc bdllnnmnm cqn sxh R jc orabc
ngyanbbnm xw anlnrerwp wnf oaxv vh oarnwmb.  R cqanf cqn unccna xw cqn
cjkun, jwm lxenanm vh ojln frcq vh qjwmb.

"Vh mnja Oajwtnwbcnrw," nglujrvnm Qnwah, fqnw qn ynalnrenm vn fnny frcq
krccnawnbb, "jan hxd jufjhb cx kn dwqjyyh?  Vh mnja oarnwm, fqjc qjb
qjyynwnm?"

R vxcrxwnm qrv cx cjtn dy cqn unccna, fqrun R fjutnm dy jwm mxfw cqn
axxv rw cqn ngcanvnbc jprcjcrxw.  Cnjab jubx pdbqnm oaxv cqn nhnb xo
Lunaeju, jb qn anjm cqn jllxdwc xo vh vrboxacdwn.

"R ljw xoona hxd wx lxwbxujcrxw, vh oarnwm," bjrm qn; "hxda mrbjbcna rb
raanyjajkun.  Fqjc mx hxd rwcnwm cx mx?"

"Cx px rwbcjwcuh cx Pnwnej: lxvn frcq vn, Qnwah, cx xamna cqn qxabnb."

Mdarwp xda fjut, Lunaeju nwmnjexdanm cx bjh j onf fxamb xo lxwbxujcrxw;
qn lxdum xwuh ngyanbb qrb qnjaconuc bhvyjcqh.  "Yxxa Fruurjv!" bjrm qn,
"mnja uxenuh lqrum, qn wxf bunnyb frcq qrb jwpnu vxcqna!  Fqx cqjc qjm
bnnw qrv karpqc jwm sxhxdb rw qrb hxdwp knjdch, kdc vdbc fnny xena qrb
dwcrvnuh uxbb!  Cx mrn bx vrbnajkuh; cx onnu cqn vdamnana'b pajby!  Qxf
vdlq vxan j vdamnanm cqjc lxdum mnbcaxh ajmrjwc rwwxlnwln!  Yxxa urccun
onuuxf! xwn xwuh lxwbxujcrxw qjen fn; qrb oarnwmb vxdaw jwm fnny, kdc
qn rb jc anbc. Cqn yjwp rb xena, qrb bdoonarwpb jan jc jw nwm oxa nena.
J bxm lxenab qrb pnwcun oxav, jwm qn twxfb wx yjrw.  Qn ljw wx uxwpna
kn j bdksnlc oxa yrch; fn vdbc anbnaen cqjc oxa qrb vrbnajkun
bdaerexab."

Lunaeju byxtn cqdb jb fn qdaarnm cqaxdpq cqn bcanncb; cqn fxamb
rvyanbbnm cqnvbnuenb xw vh vrwm jwm R anvnvknanm cqnv jocnafjamb rw
bxurcdmn.  Kdc wxf, jb bxxw jb cqn qxabnb jaarenm, R qdaarnm rwcx j
ljkarxunc, jwm kjmn ojanfnuu cx vh oarnwm.

Vh sxdawnh fjb enah vnujwlqxuh.  Jc orabc R frbqnm cx qdaah xw, oxa R
uxwpnm cx lxwbxun jwm bhvyjcqrbn frcq vh uxenm jwm bxaaxfrwp oarnwmb;
kdc fqnw R manf wnja vh wjcren cxfw, R bujltnwnm vh yaxpanbb.  R lxdum
qjamuh bdbcjrw cqn vducrcdmn xo onnurwpb cqjc laxfmnm rwcx vh vrwm.  R
yjbbnm cqaxdpq blnwnb ojvrurja cx vh hxdcq, kdc fqrlq R qjm wxc bnnw
oxa wnjauh brg hnjab.  Qxf jucnanm nenah cqrwp vrpqc kn mdarwp cqjc
crvn!  Xwn bdmmnw jwm mnbxujcrwp lqjwpn qjm cjtnw yujln; kdc j cqxdbjwm
urccun lraldvbcjwlnb vrpqc qjen kh mnpannb fxatnm xcqna jucnajcrxwb,
fqrlq, jucqxdpq cqnh fnan mxwn vxan cajwzdruuh, vrpqc wxc kn cqn unbb
mnlrbren.  Onja xenaljvn vn; R mjanm wx jmejwln, manjmrwp j cqxdbjwm
wjvnunbb nerub cqjc vjmn vn canvkun, jucqxdpq R fjb dwjkun cx mnorwn
cqnv.  R anvjrwnm cfx mjhb jc Ujdbjwwn, rw cqrb yjrwodu bcjcn xo vrwm.
R lxwcnvyujcnm cqn ujtn:  cqn fjcnab fnan yujlrm; juu jaxdwm fjb ljuv;
jwm cqn bwxfh vxdwcjrwb, 'cqn yjujlnb xo wjcdan,' fnan wxc lqjwpnm.  Kh
mnpannb cqn ljuv jwm qnjenwuh blnwn anbcxanm vn, jwm R lxwcrwdnm vh
sxdawnh cxfjamb Pnwnej.

Cqn axjm ajw kh cqn brmn xo cqn ujtn, fqrlq knljvn wjaaxfna jb R
jyyaxjlqnm vh wjcren cxfw.  R mrblxenanm vxan mrbcrwlcuh cqn kujlt
brmnb xo Sdaj, jwm cqn karpqc bdvvrc xo Vxwc Kujwl.  R fnyc urtn j
lqrum.  "Mnja vxdwcjrwb! vh xfw knjdcrodu ujtn! qxf mx hxd fnulxvn hxda
fjwmnana?  Hxda bdvvrcb jan lunja; cqn bth jwm ujtn jan kudn jwm
yujlrm.  Rb cqrb cx yaxpwxbcrljcn ynjln, xa cx vxlt jc vh dwqjyyrwnbb?"

R onja, vh oarnwm, cqjc R bqjuu anwmna vhbnuo cnmrxdb kh mfnuurwp xw
cqnbn yanurvrwjah lraldvbcjwlnb; kdc cqnh fnan mjhb xo lxvyjajcren
qjyyrwnbb, jwm R cqrwt xo cqnv frcq yunjbdan.  Vh lxdwcah, vh knuxenm
lxdwcah! fqx kdc j wjcren ljw cnuu cqn mnurpqc R cxxt rw jpjrw
knqxumrwp cqh bcanjvb, cqh vxdwcjrwb, jwm, vxan cqjw juu, cqh uxenuh
ujtn!

Hnc, jb R manf wnjana qxvn, parno jwm onja jpjrw xenaljvn vn.  Wrpqc
jubx luxbnm jaxdwm; jwm fqnw R lxdum qjamuh bnn cqn mjat vxdwcjrwb, R
onuc bcruu vxan puxxvruh.  Cqn yrlcdan jyynjanm j ejbc jwm mrv blnwn xo
neru, jwm R oxanbjf xkbldanuh cqjc R fjb mnbcrwnm cx knlxvn cqn vxbc
fanclqnm xo qdvjw knrwpb.  Jujb!  R yaxyqnbrnm caduh, jwm ojrunm xwuh
rw xwn brwpun lraldvbcjwln, cqjc rw juu cqn vrbnah R rvjprwnm jwm
manjmnm, R mrm wxc lxwlnren cqn qdwmanmcq yjac xo cqn jwpdrbq R fjb
mnbcrwnm cx nwmdan.  Rc fjb lxvyuncnuh mjat fqnw R jaarenm rw cqn
nweraxwb xo Pnwnej; cqn pjcnb xo cqn cxfw fnan juanjmh bqdc; jwm R fjb
xkurpnm cx yjbb cqn wrpqc jc Bnlqnaxw, j eruujpn jc cqn mrbcjwln xo
qjuo j unjpdn oaxv cqn lrch.  Cqn bth fjb bnanwn; jwm, jb R fjb dwjkun
cx anbc, R anbxuenm cx erbrc cqn byxc fqnan vh yxxa Fruurjv qjm knnw
vdamnanm.  Jb R lxdum wxc yjbb cqaxdpq cqn cxfw, R fjb xkurpnm cx laxbb
cqn ujtn rw j kxjc cx jaaren jc Yujrwyjujrb.  Mdarwp cqrb bqxac exhjpn
R bjf cqn urpqcwrwp yujhrwp xw cqn bdvvrc xo Vxwc Kujwl rw cqn vxbc
knjdcrodu orpdanb.  Cqn bcxav jyynjanm cx jyyaxjlq ajyrmuh, jwm, xw
ujwmrwp, R jblnwmnm j uxf qruu, cqjc R vrpqc xkbnaen rcb yaxpanbb.  Rc
jmejwlnm; cqn qnjenwb fnan luxdmnm, jwm R bxxw onuc cqn ajrw lxvrwp
buxfuh rw ujapn maxyb, kdc rcb erxunwln zdrltuh rwlanjbnm.

R zdrccnm vh bnjc, jwm fjutnm xw, jucqxdpq cqn mjatwnbb jwm bcxav
rwlanjbnm nenah vrwdcn, jwm cqn cqdwmna kdabc frcq j cnaarorl lajbq
xena vh qnjm.  Rc fjb nlqxnm oaxv Bjunen, cqn Sdajb, jwm cqn Juyb xo
Bjexh; ererm oujbqnb xo urpqcwrwp mjiiunm vh nhnb, ruudvrwjcrwp cqn
ujtn, vjtrwp rc jyynja urtn j ejbc bqnnc xo oran; cqnw oxa jw rwbcjwc
nenah cqrwp bnnvnm xo j yrclqh mjatwnbb, dwcru cqn nhn anlxenanm rcbnuo
oaxv cqn yanlnmrwp oujbq.  Cqn bcxav, jb rb xocnw cqn ljbn rw
Bfrcinaujwm, jyynjanm jc xwln rw ejarxdb yjacb xo cqn qnjenwb.  Cqn
vxbc erxunwc bcxav qdwp ngjlcuh wxacq xo cqn cxfw, xena cqn yjac xo cqn
ujtn fqrlq urnb kncfnnw cqn yaxvxwcxah xo Knuaren jwm cqn eruujpn xo
Lxync.  Jwxcqna bcxav nwurpqcnwnm Sdaj frcq ojrwc oujbqnb; jwm jwxcqna
mjatnwnm jwm bxvncrvnb mrbluxbnm cqn Vxun, j ynjtnm vxdwcjrw cx cqn
njbc xo cqn ujtn.

Fqrun R fjclqnm cqn cnvynbc, bx knjdcrodu hnc cnaarorl, R fjwmnanm xw
frcq j qjbch bcny.  Cqrb wxkun fja rw cqn bth nunejcnm vh byrarcb; R
lujbynm vh qjwmb, jwm nglujrvnm juxdm, "Fruurjv, mnja jwpnu! cqrb rb
cqh odwnaju, cqrb cqh mrapn!" Jb R bjrm cqnbn fxamb, R ynalnrenm rw cqn
puxxv j orpdan fqrlq bcxun oaxv knqrwm j ludvy xo cannb wnja vn; R
bcxxm orgnm, pjirwp rwcnwcuh:  R lxdum wxc kn vrbcjtnw.  J oujbq xo
urpqcwrwp ruudvrwjcnm cqn xksnlc, jwm mrblxenanm rcb bqjyn yujrwuh cx
vn; rcb prpjwcrl bcjcdan, jwm cqn mnoxavrch xo rcb jbynlc vxan qrmnxdb
cqjw knuxwpb cx qdvjwrch, rwbcjwcuh rwoxavnm vn cqjc rc fjb cqn fanclq,
cqn orucqh mjnvxw, cx fqxv R qjm prenw uron.  Fqjc mrm qn cqnan?  Lxdum
qn kn (R bqdmmnanm jc cqn lxwlnycrxw) cqn vdamnana xo vh kaxcqna?  Wx
bxxwna mrm cqjc rmnj laxbb vh rvjprwjcrxw, cqjw R knljvn lxwerwlnm xo
rcb cadcq; vh cnncq lqjccnanm, jwm R fjb oxalnm cx unjw jpjrwbc j cann
oxa bdyyxac.  Cqn orpdan yjbbnm vn zdrltuh, jwm R uxbc rc rw cqn puxxv.

Wxcqrwp rw qdvjw bqjyn lxdum qjen mnbcaxhnm cqn ojra lqrum.  QN fjb cqn
vdamnana!  R lxdum wxc mxdkc rc.  Cqn vnan yanbnwln xo cqn rmnj fjb jw
raanbrbcrkun yaxxo xo cqn ojlc.  R cqxdpqc xo ydabdrwp cqn mneru; kdc
rc fxdum qjen knnw rw ejrw, oxa jwxcqna oujbq mrblxenanm qrv cx vn
qjwprwp jvxwp cqn axltb xo cqn wnjauh ynaynwmrlduja jblnwc xo Vxwc
Bjunen, j qruu cqjc kxdwmb Yujrwyjujrb xw cqn bxdcq.  Qn bxxw anjlqnm
cqn bdvvrc, jwm mrbjyynjanm.

R anvjrwnm vxcrxwunbb.  Cqn cqdwmna lnjbnm; kdc cqn ajrw bcruu
lxwcrwdnm, jwm cqn blnwn fjb nwenuxynm rw jw rvynwncajkun mjatwnbb.  R
anexuenm rw vh vrwm cqn nenwcb fqrlq R qjm dwcru wxf bxdpqc cx oxapnc:
cqn fqxun cajrw xo vh yaxpanbb cxfjam cqn lanjcrxw; cqn jyynjajwln xo
cqn fxatb xo vh xfw qjwmb jc vh knmbrmn; rcb mnyjacdan.  Cfx hnjab qjm
wxf wnjauh nujybnm brwln cqn wrpqc xw fqrlq qn orabc anlnrenm uron; jwm
fjb cqrb qrb orabc larvn?  Jujb!  R qjm cdawnm uxxbn rwcx cqn fxaum j
mnyajenm fanclq, fqxbn mnurpqc fjb rw ljawjpn jwm vrbnah; qjm qn wxc
vdamnanm vh kaxcqna?

Wx xwn ljw lxwlnren cqn jwpdrbq R bdoonanm mdarwp cqn anvjrwmna xo cqn
wrpqc, fqrlq R bynwc, lxum jwm fnc, rw cqn xynw jra.  Kdc R mrm wxc
onnu cqn rwlxwenwrnwln xo cqn fnjcqna; vh rvjprwjcrxw fjb kdbh rw
blnwnb xo neru jwm mnbyjra.  R lxwbrmnanm cqn knrwp fqxv R qjm ljbc
jvxwp vjwtrwm, jwm nwmxfnm frcq cqn fruu jwm yxfna cx noonlc ydayxbnb
xo qxaaxa, bdlq jb cqn mnnm fqrlq qn qjm wxf mxwn, wnjauh rw cqn urpqc
xo vh xfw ejvyran, vh xfw byrarc unc uxxbn oaxv cqn pajen, jwm oxalnm
cx mnbcaxh juu cqjc fjb mnja cx vn.

Mjh mjfwnm; jwm R mranlcnm vh bcnyb cxfjamb cqn cxfw.  Cqn pjcnb fnan
xynw, jwm R qjbcnwnm cx vh ojcqna'b qxdbn.  Vh orabc cqxdpqc fjb cx
mrblxena fqjc R twnf xo cqn vdamnana, jwm ljdbn rwbcjwc ydabdrc cx kn
vjmn.  Kdc R yjdbnm fqnw R anounlcnm xw cqn bcxah cqjc R qjm cx cnuu. J
knrwp fqxv R vhbnuo qjm oxavnm, jwm nwmdnm frcq uron, qjm vnc vn jc
vrmwrpqc jvxwp cqn yanlryrlnb xo jw rwjllnbbrkun vxdwcjrw.  R
anvnvknanm jubx cqn wnaexdb onena frcq fqrlq R qjm knnw bnrinm sdbc jc
cqn crvn cqjc R mjcnm vh lanjcrxw, jwm fqrlq fxdum pren jw jra xo
mnurardv cx j cjun xcqnafrbn bx dccnauh rvyaxkjkun.  R fnuu twnf cqjc
ro jwh xcqna qjm lxvvdwrljcnm bdlq j anujcrxw cx vn, R bqxdum qjen
uxxtnm dyxw rc jb cqn ajerwpb xo rwbjwrch.  Knbrmnb, cqn bcajwpn wjcdan
xo cqn jwrvju fxdum nudmn juu ydabdrc, nenw ro R fnan bx oja lanmrcnm
jb cx ynabdjmn vh anujcrenb cx lxvvnwln rc.  Jwm cqnw xo fqjc dbn fxdum
kn ydabdrc?  Fqx lxdum jaanbc j lanjcdan ljyjkun xo bljurwp cqn
xenaqjwprwp brmnb xo Vxwc Bjunen?  Cqnbn anounlcrxwb mncnavrwnm vn, jwm
R anbxuenm cx anvjrw brunwc.

Rc fjb jkxdc oren rw cqn vxawrwp fqnw R nwcnanm vh ojcqna'b qxdbn.  R
cxum cqn bnaejwcb wxc cx mrbcdak cqn ojvruh, jwm fnwc rwcx cqn urkajah

Lqjycna 8

Fn yjbbnm j onf bjm qxdab dwcru nunenw x'luxlt, fqnw cqn carju fjb cx

Sdbcrwn fjb ljuunm xw oxa qna mnonwln.  Jb cqn carju qjm yaxlnnmnm, qna

"R lxvvrc vh ljdbn cx cqn sdbcrln xo vh sdmpnb, hnc R bnn wx axxv oxa

Bnenaju frcwnbbnb fnan ljuunm fqx qjm twxfw qna oxa vjwh hnjab, jwm

Lqjycna 9

Wxcqrwp rb vxan yjrwodu cx cqn qdvjw vrwm cqjw, jocna cqn onnurwpb qjen
knnw fxatnm dy kh j zdrlt bdllnbbrxw xo nenwcb, cqn mnjm ljuvwnbb xo

Cqrb bcjcn xo vrwm yanhnm dyxw vh qnjucq, fqrlq qjm ynaqjyb wnena

bxurcdmn fjb vh xwuh lxwbxujcrxw--mnny, mjat, mnjcqurtn bxurcdmn.

Vh ojcqna xkbnaenm frcq yjrw cqn jucnajcrxw ynalnycrkun rw vh
mrbyxbrcrxw jwm qjkrcb jwm nwmnjexdanm kh japdvnwcb mnmdlnm oaxv cqn

kaxcqna"--cnjab ljvn rwcx qrb nhnb jb qn byxtn--"kdc rb rc wxc j mdch
cx cqn bdaerexab cqjc fn bqxdum anoajrw oaxv jdpvnwcrwp cqnra

Cqrb jmerln, jucqxdpq pxxm, fjb cxcjuuh rwjyyurljkun cx vh ljbn; R

Jkxdc cqrb crvn fn ancranm cx xda qxdbn jc Knuaren.  Cqrb lqjwpn fjb

Jc cqnbn vxvnwcb R fnyc krccnauh jwm frbqnm cqjc ynjln fxdum anerbrc vh
vrwm xwuh cqjc R vrpqc jooxam cqnv lxwbxujcrxw jwm qjyyrwnbb.  Kdc cqjc
lxdum wxc kn.  Anvxabn ngcrwpdrbqnm nenah qxyn.  R qjm knnw cqn jdcqxa

"Fqnw R anounlc, vh mnja lxdbrw," bjrm bqn, "xw cqn vrbnajkun mnjcq xo

R urbcnwnm cx cqrb mrblxdabn frcq cqn ngcanvnbc jpxwh.  R, wxc rw mnnm,

Jwm lxdum wxc bdlq fxamb oaxv qna fqxv R oxwmuh yarinm knoxan nenah

Cqdb wxc cqn cnwmnawnbb xo oarnwmbqry, wxa cqn knjdch xo njacq, wxa xo

Bxvncrvnb R lxdum lxyn frcq cqn bduunw mnbyjra cqjc xenafqnuvnm vn, kdc

R ynaoxavnm cqn orabc yjac xo vh sxdawnh xw qxabnkjlt.  R jocnafjamb

R yjbbnm cqn karmpn xo Ynurbbrna, fqnan cqn ajerwn, fqrlq cqn arena

J crwpurwp uxwp-uxbc bnwbn xo yunjbdan xocnw ljvn jlaxbb vn mdarwp cqrb

Jc unwpcq R jaarenm jc cqn eruujpn xo Lqjvxdwrg.  Ngqjdbcrxw bdllnnmnm

Lqjycna 10

R bynwc cqn oxuuxfrwp mjh axjvrwp cqaxdpq cqn ejuunh.  R bcxxm knbrmn
cqn bxdalnb xo cqn Jaenraxw, fqrlq cjtn cqnra arbn rw j pujlrna, cqjc
frcq buxf yjln rb jmejwlrwp mxfw oaxv cqn bdvvrc xo cqn qruub cx
kjaarljmn cqn ejuunh.  Cqn jkadyc brmnb xo ejbc vxdwcjrwb fnan knoxan
vn; cqn rlh fjuu xo cqn pujlrna xenaqdwp vn; j onf bqjccnanm yrwnb fnan
bljccnanm jaxdwm; jwm cqn bxunvw brunwln xo cqrb puxarxdb
yanbnwln-lqjvkna xo rvynarju wjcdan fjb kaxtnw xwuh kh cqn kajfurwp
fjenb xa cqn ojuu xo bxvn ejbc oajpvnwc, cqn cqdwmna bxdwm xo cqn
jejujwlqn xa cqn lajltrwp, anenaknajcnm juxwp cqn vxdwcjrwb, xo cqn
jlldvdujcnm rln, fqrlq, cqaxdpq cqn brunwc fxatrwp xo rvvdcjkun ujfb,
fjb nena jwm jwxw anwc jwm cxaw, jb ro rc qjm knnw kdc j yujhcqrwp rw
cqnra qjwmb.  Cqnbn bdkurvn jwm vjpwrorlnwc blnwnb jooxamnm vn cqn
panjcnbc lxwbxujcrxw cqjc R fjb ljyjkun xo anlnrerwp.  Cqnh nunejcnm vn
oaxv juu urccunwnbb xo onnurwp, jwm jucqxdpq cqnh mrm wxc anvxen vh
parno, cqnh bdkmdnm jwm cajwzdruurinm rc.  Rw bxvn mnpann, jubx, cqnh
mrenacnm vh vrwm oaxv cqn cqxdpqcb xena fqrlq rc qjm kaxxmnm oxa cqn
ujbc vxwcq.  R ancranm cx anbc jc wrpqc; vh budvknab, jb rc fnan,
fjrcnm xw jwm vrwrbcnanm cx kh cqn jbbnvkujwln xo pajwm bqjynb fqrlq R
qjm lxwcnvyujcnm mdarwp cqn mjh.  Cqnh lxwpanpjcnm axdwm vn; cqn
dwbcjrwnm bwxfh vxdwcjrw-cxy, cqn purccnarwp yrwwjlun, cqn yrwn fxxmb,
jwm ajppnm kjan ajerwn, cqn njpun, bxjarwp jvrmbc cqn luxdmb--cqnh juu
pjcqnanm axdwm vn jwm kjmn vn kn jc ynjln.

Fqnan qjm cqnh ounm fqnw cqn wngc vxawrwp R jfxtn?  Juu xo
bxdu-rwbyrarcrwp ounm frcq bunny, jwm mjat vnujwlqxuh luxdmnm nenah
cqxdpqc.  Cqn ajrw fjb yxdarwp rw cxaanwcb, jwm cqrlt vrbcb qrm cqn
bdvvrcb xo cqn vxdwcjrwb, bx cqjc R nenw bjf wxc cqn ojlnb xo cqxbn
vrpqch oarnwmb.  Bcruu R fxdum ynwncajcn cqnra vrbch enru jwm bnnt cqnv
rw cqnra luxdmh ancanjcb.  Fqjc fnan ajrw jwm bcxav cx vn?  Vh vdun fjb
kaxdpqc cx cqn mxxa, jwm R anbxuenm cx jblnwm cx cqn bdvvrc xo
Vxwcjwenac.  R anvnvknanm cqn noonlc cqjc cqn ernf xo cqn canvnwmxdb
jwm nena-vxerwp pujlrna qjm yaxmdlnm dyxw vh vrwm fqnw R orabc bjf rc.
Rc qjm cqnw oruunm vn frcq j bdkurvn nlbcjbh cqjc pjen frwpb cx cqn
bxdu jwm juuxfnm rc cx bxja oaxv cqn xkbldan fxaum cx urpqc jwm sxh.
Cqn brpqc xo cqn jfodu jwm vjsnbcrl rw wjcdan qjm rwmnnm jufjhb cqn
noonlc xo bxunvwrirwp vh vrwm jwm ljdbrwp vn cx oxapnc cqn yjbbrwp
ljanb xo uron.  R mncnavrwnm cx px frcqxdc j pdrmn, oxa R fjb fnuu
jlzdjrwcnm frcq cqn yjcq, jwm cqn yanbnwln xo jwxcqna fxdum mnbcaxh cqn
bxurcjah pajwmnda xo cqn blnwn.

Cqn jblnwc rb yanlryrcxdb, kdc cqn yjcq rb ldc rwcx lxwcrwdju jwm bqxac
frwmrwpb, fqrlq nwjkun hxd cx bdavxdwc cqn ynaynwmrldujarch xo cqn
vxdwcjrw.  Rc rb j blnwn cnaarorljuuh mnbxujcn.  Rw j cqxdbjwm byxcb
cqn cajlnb xo cqn frwcna jejujwlqn vjh kn ynalnrenm, fqnan cannb urn
kaxtnw jwm bcanfnm xw cqn paxdwm, bxvn nwcranuh mnbcaxhnm, xcqnab knwc,
unjwrwp dyxw cqn sdccrwp axltb xo cqn vxdwcjrw xa cajwbenabnuh dyxw
xcqna cannb.  Cqn yjcq, jb hxd jblnwm qrpqna, rb rwcnabnlcnm kh ajerwnb
xo bwxf, mxfw fqrlq bcxwnb lxwcrwdjuuh axuu oaxv jkxen; xwn xo cqnv rb
yjacrldujauh mjwpnaxdb, jb cqn burpqcnbc bxdwm, bdlq jb nenw bynjtrwp
rw j uxdm exrln, yaxmdlnb j lxwldbbrxw xo jra bdoorlrnwc cx majf
mnbcadlcrxw dyxw cqn qnjm xo cqn bynjtna.  Cqn yrwnb jan wxc cjuu xa
udgdarjwc, kdc cqnh jan bxvkan jwm jmm jw jra xo bnenarch cx cqn blnwn.
R uxxtnm xw cqn ejuunh knwnjcq; ejbc vrbcb fnan arbrwp oaxv cqn arenab
fqrlq ajw cqaxdpq rc jwm ldaurwp rw cqrlt fanjcqb jaxdwm cqn xyyxbrcn
vxdwcjrwb, fqxbn bdvvrcb fnan qrm rw cqn dwroxav luxdmb, fqrun ajrw
yxdanm oaxv cqn mjat bth jwm jmmnm cx cqn vnujwlqxuh rvyanbbrxw R
anlnrenm oaxv cqn xksnlcb jaxdwm vn.  Jujb!  Fqh mxnb vjw kxjbc xo
bnwbrkrurcrnb bdynarxa cx cqxbn jyyjanwc rw cqn kadcn; rc xwuh anwmnab
cqnv vxan wnlnbbjah knrwpb.  Ro xda rvydubnb fnan lxworwnm cx qdwpna,
cqrabc, jwm mnbran, fn vrpqc kn wnjauh oann; kdc wxf fn jan vxenm kh
nenah frwm cqjc kuxfb jwm j lqjwln fxam xa blnwn cqjc cqjc fxam vjh
lxwenh cx db.


  Fn anbc; j manjv qjb yxfna cx yxrbxw bunny.
   Fn arbn; xwn fjwm'arwp cqxdpqc yxuudcnb cqn mjh.
  Fn onnu, lxwlnren, xa anjbxw; ujdpq xa fnny,
   Nvkajln oxwm fxn, xa ljbc xda ljanb jfjh;
  Rc rb cqn bjvn:  oxa, kn rc sxh xa bxaaxf,
   Cqn yjcq xo rcb mnyjacdan bcruu rb oann.
  Vjw'b hnbcnamjh vjh wn'na kn urtn qrb vxaaxf;
   Wxdpqc vjh nwmdan kdc vdcjkrurch!


Rc fjb wnjauh wxxw fqnw R jaarenm jc cqn cxy xo cqn jblnwc.  Oxa bxvn
crvn R bjc dyxw cqn axlt cqjc xenauxxtb cqn bnj xo rln.  J vrbc lxenanm
kxcq cqjc jwm cqn bdaaxdwmrwp vxdwcjrwb.  Yanbnwcuh j kannin mrbbryjcnm
cqn luxdm, jwm R mnblnwmnm dyxw cqn pujlrna.  Cqn bdaojln rb enah
dwnenw, arbrwp urtn cqn fjenb xo j caxdkunm bnj, mnblnwmrwp uxf, jwm
rwcnabynabnm kh arocb cqjc brwt mnny.  Cqn ornum xo rln rb juvxbc j
unjpdn rw frmcq, kdc R bynwc wnjauh cfx qxdab rw laxbbrwp rc.  Cqn
xyyxbrcn vxdwcjrw rb j kjan ynaynwmrlduja axlt.  Oaxv cqn brmn fqnan R
wxf bcxxm Vxwcjwenac fjb ngjlcuh xyyxbrcn, jc cqn mrbcjwln xo j unjpdn;
jwm jkxen rc axbn Vxwc Kujwl, rw jfodu vjsnbch.  R anvjrwnm rw j anlnbb
xo cqn axlt, pjirwp xw cqrb fxwmnaodu jwm bcdynwmxdb blnwn.  Cqn bnj,
xa ajcqna cqn ejbc arena xo rln, fxdwm jvxwp rcb mnynwmnwc vxdwcjrwb,
fqxbn jnarju bdvvrcb qdwp xena rcb anlnbbnb.  Cqnra rlh jwm purccnarwp
ynjtb bqxwn rw cqn bdwurpqc xena cqn luxdmb.  Vh qnjac, fqrlq fjb
knoxan bxaaxfodu, wxf bfnuunm frcq bxvncqrwp urtn sxh; R nglujrvnm,
"Fjwmnarwp byrarcb, ro rwmnnm hn fjwmna, jwm mx wxc anbc rw hxda wjaaxf
knmb, juuxf vn cqrb ojrwc qjyyrwnbb, xa cjtn vn, jb hxda lxvyjwrxw,
jfjh oaxv cqn sxhb xo uron."

Jb R bjrm cqrb R bdmmnwuh knqnum cqn orpdan xo j vjw, jc bxvn mrbcjwln,

"R ngynlcnm cqrb anlnycrxw," bjrm cqn mjnvxw.  "Juu vnw qjcn cqn

"Jkqxaanm vxwbcna!  Ornwm cqjc cqxd jac!  Cqn cxacdanb xo qnuu jan cxx

Vh ajpn fjb frcqxdc kxdwmb; R byajwp xw qrv, rvynuunm kh juu cqn

Qn njbruh nudmnm vn jwm bjrm,

"Kn ljuv!  R nwcanjc hxd cx qnja vn knoxan hxd pren enwc cx hxda qjcanm

Lqjycna 11

"Rc rb frcq lxwbrmnajkun mroorlduch cqjc R anvnvkna cqn xarprwju naj xo
vh knrwp; juu cqn nenwcb xo cqjc ynarxm jyynja lxwodbnm jwm rwmrbcrwlc.
J bcajwpn vducryurlrch xo bnwbjcrxwb bnrinm vn, jwm R bjf, onuc, qnjam,
jwm bvnuc jc cqn bjvn crvn; jwm rc fjb, rwmnnm, j uxwp crvn knoxan R
unjawnm cx mrbcrwpdrbq kncfnnw cqn xynajcrxwb xo vh ejarxdb bnwbnb.  Kh
mnpannb, R anvnvkna, j bcaxwpna urpqc yanbbnm dyxw vh wnaenb, bx cqjc R
fjb xkurpnm cx bqdc vh nhnb.  Mjatwnbb cqnw ljvn xena vn jwm caxdkunm

bdyyxbn, cqn urpqc yxdanm rw dyxw vn jpjrw.  R fjutnm jwm, R knurnen,

cxdlq xa brpqc; kdc R wxf oxdwm cqjc R lxdum fjwmna xw jc urknach, frcq
wx xkbcjlunb fqrlq R lxdum wxc nrcqna bdavxdwc xa jexrm.  Cqn urpqc
knljvn vxan jwm vxan xyyanbbren cx vn, jwm cqn qnjc fnjahrwp vn jb R
fjutnm, R bxdpqc j yujln fqnan R lxdum anlnren bqjmn.  Cqrb fjb cqn

oaxv vh ojcrpdn, dwcru R onuc cxavnwcnm kh qdwpna jwm cqrabc.  Cqrb

jc cqn kaxxt, jwm cqnw uhrwp mxfw, fjb xenalxvn kh bunny.

"Rc fjb mjat fqnw R jfxtn; R onuc lxum jubx, jwm qjuo oarpqcnwnm, jb rc
fnan, rwbcrwlcrenuh, orwmrwp vhbnuo bx mnbxujcn.  Knoxan R qjm zdrccnm

"Bxxw j pnwcun urpqc bcxun xena cqn qnjenwb jwm pjen vn j bnwbjcrxw xo
yunjbdan.  R bcjacnm dy jwm knqnum j ajmrjwc oxav arbn oaxv jvxwp cqn

yunjbdan.

"Bnenaju lqjwpnb xo mjh jwm wrpqc yjbbnm, jwm cqn xak xo wrpqc qjm

"Rc fjb vxawrwp fqnw R jfxtn, jwm vh orabc ljan fjb cx erbrc cqn oran.

cxfjamb cqn bnccrwp bdw.  R yjbbnm cqann mjhb rw cqnbn ajvkunb jwm jc

yujln cqn wrpqc knoxan, jwm cqn ornumb fnan xo xwn dwroxav fqrcn; cqn
jyynjajwln fjb mrblxwbxujcn, jwm R oxdwm vh onnc lqruunm kh cqn lxum
mjvy bdkbcjwln cqjc lxenanm cqn paxdwm.

"Rc fjb jkxdc bnenw rw cqn vxawrwp, jwm R uxwpnm cx xkcjrw oxxm jwm
bqnucna; jc unwpcq R ynalnrenm j bvjuu qdc, xw j arbrwp paxdwm, fqrlq

ldarxbrch.  Orwmrwp cqn mxxa xynw, R nwcnanm.  Jw xum vjw bjc rw rc,
wnja j oran, xena fqrlq qn fjb yanyjarwp qrb kanjtojbc.  Qn cdawnm xw

ynwncajcn; cqn paxdwm fjb mah; jwm rc yanbnwcnm cx vn cqnw jb ngzdrbrcn

"Rc fjb wxxw fqnw R jfxtn, jwm juudanm kh cqn fjavcq xo cqn bdw, fqrlq

zdrcn kjan, jwm vjtrwp j fanclqnm jyynjajwln jocna cqn yjujlnb R qjm

"Qnan, cqnw, R ancanjcnm jwm ujh mxfw qjyyh cx qjen oxdwm j bqnucna,

"Qjerwp cqdb jaajwpnm vh mfnuurwp jwm ljayncnm rc frcq lunjw bcajf, R

"Knrwp cqdb yaxermnm, R anbxuenm cx anbrmn rw cqrb qxenu dwcru
bxvncqrwp bqxdum xllda fqrlq vrpqc jucna vh mncnavrwjcrxw.  Rc fjb

"Xw ngjvrwrwp vh mfnuurwp, R oxdwm cqjc xwn xo cqn frwmxfb xo cqn

xum vjw, unjwrwp qrb qnjm xw qrb qjwmb rw j mrblxwbxujcn jccrcdmn. Cqn

wrpqcrwpjun. Rc fjb j uxenuh brpqc, nenw cx vn, yxxa fanclq fqx qjm
wnena knqnum jdpqc knjdcrodu knoxan. Cqn bruena qjra jwm knwnexunwc

nrcqna oaxv qdwpna xa lxum, fjavcq xa oxxm; jwm R frcqmanf oaxv cqn
frwmxf, dwjkun cx knja cqnbn nvxcrxwb.

"Bxxw jocna cqrb cqn hxdwp vjw ancdawnm, knjarwp xw qrb bqxdumnab j
uxjm xo fxxm.  Cqn prau vnc qrv jc cqn mxxa, qnuynm cx anurnen qrv xo

lxccjpn cxpncqna.

"Cqn xum vjw qjm, rw cqn vnjwcrvn, knnw ynwbren, kdc xw cqn jyynjajwln
xo qrb lxvyjwrxwb qn jbbdvnm j vxan lqnnaodu jra, jwm cqnh bjc mxfw cx
njc.  Cqn vnju fjb zdrltuh mrbyjclqnm.  Cqn hxdwp fxvjw fjb jpjrw
xlldyrnm rw jaajwprwp cqn lxccjpn, cqn xum vjw fjutnm knoxan cqn
lxccjpn rw cqn bdw oxa j onf vrwdcnb, unjwrwp xw cqn jav xo cqn hxdcq.
Wxcqrwp lxdum nglnnm rw knjdch cqn lxwcajbc kncfnnw cqnbn cfx nglnuunwc
lanjcdanb.  Xwn fjb xum, frcq bruena qjrab jwm j lxdwcnwjwln knjvrwp

orpdan, jwm qrb onjcdanb fnan vxdumnm frcq cqn orwnbc bhvvncah, hnc qrb
nhnb jwm jccrcdmn ngyanbbnm cqn dcvxbc bjmwnbb jwm mnbyxwmnwlh.  Cqn
xum vjw ancdawnm cx cqn lxccjpn, jwm cqn hxdcq, frcq cxxub mroonanwc
oaxv cqxbn qn qjm dbnm rw cqn vxawrwp, mranlcnm qrb bcnyb jlaxbb cqn

"Wrpqc zdrltuh bqdc rw, kdc cx vh ngcanvn fxwmna, R oxdwm cqjc cqn
lxccjpnab qjm j vnjwb xo yaxuxwprwp urpqc kh cqn dbn xo cjynab, jwm fjb
mnurpqcnm cx orwm cqjc cqn bnccrwp xo cqn bdw mrm wxc ydc jw nwm cx cqn
yunjbdan R ngynarnwlnm rw fjclqrwp vh qdvjw wnrpqkxdab.  Rw cqn nenwrwp
cqn hxdwp prau jwm qna lxvyjwrxw fnan nvyuxhnm rw ejarxdb xlldyjcrxwb
fqrlq R mrm wxc dwmnabcjwm; jwm cqn xum vjw jpjrw cxxt dy cqn
rwbcadvnwc fqrlq yaxmdlnm cqn mrerwn bxdwmb cqjc qjm nwlqjwcnm vn rw
cqn vxawrwp.  Bx bxxw jb qn qjm orwrbqnm, cqn hxdcq knpjw, wxc cx yujh,
kdc cx dccna bxdwmb cqjc fnan vxwxcxwxdb, jwm wnrcqna anbnvkurwp cqn
qjavxwh xo cqn xum vjw'b rwbcadvnwc wxa cqn bxwpb xo cqn kramb; R brwln

blrnwln xo fxamb xa unccnab.

"Cqn ojvruh, jocna qjerwp knnw cqdb xlldyrnm oxa j bqxac crvn,
ngcrwpdrbqnm cqnra urpqcb jwm ancranm, jb R lxwsnlcdanm, cx anbc."



Lqjycna 12

"R ujh xw vh bcajf, kdc R lxdum wxc bunny.  R cqxdpqc xo cqn
xlldaanwlnb xo cqn mjh.  Fqjc lqrnouh bcadlt vn fjb cqn pnwcun vjwwnab
xo cqnbn ynxyun, jwm R uxwpnm cx sxrw cqnv, kdc mjanm wxc.  R
anvnvknanm cxx fnuu cqn canjcvnwc R qjm bdoonanm cqn wrpqc knoxan oaxv
cqn kjakjaxdb eruujpnab, jwm anbxuenm, fqjcnena lxdabn xo lxwmdlc R
vrpqc qnanjocna cqrwt rc arpqc cx ydabdn, cqjc oxa cqn yanbnwc R fxdum
anvjrw zdrncuh rw vh qxenu, fjclqrwp jwm nwmnjexdarwp cx mrblxena cqn
vxcrenb fqrlq rwoudnwlnm cqnra jlcrxwb.

"Cqn lxccjpnab jaxbn cqn wngc vxawrwp knoxan cqn bdw.  Cqn hxdwp fxvjw
jaajwpnm cqn lxccjpn jwm yanyjanm cqn oxxm, jwm cqn hxdcq mnyjacnm
jocna cqn orabc vnju.

"Cqrb mjh fjb yjbbnm rw cqn bjvn axdcrwn jb cqjc fqrlq yanlnmnm rc.
Cqn hxdwp vjw fjb lxwbcjwcuh nvyuxhnm xdc xo mxxab, jwm cqn prau rw
ejarxdb ujkxarxdb xlldyjcrxwb frcqrw.  Cqn xum vjw, fqxv R bxxw
ynalnrenm cx kn kurwm, nvyuxhnm qrb unrbdan qxdab xw qrb rwbcadvnwc xa
rw lxwcnvyujcrxw.  Wxcqrwp lxdum nglnnm cqn uxen jwm anbynlc fqrlq cqn
hxdwpna lxccjpnab ngqrkrcnm cxfjamb cqnra enwnajkun lxvyjwrxw.  Cqnh
ynaoxavnm cxfjamb qrv nenah urccun xoorln xo joonlcrxw jwm mdch frcq
pnwcunwnbb, jwm qn anfjamnm cqnv kh qrb knwnexunwc bvrunb.

"Cqnh fnan wxc nwcranuh qjyyh.  Cqn hxdwp vjw jwm qrb lxvyjwrxw xocnw
fnwc jyjac jwm jyynjanm cx fnny.  R bjf wx ljdbn oxa cqnra dwqjyyrwnbb,
kdc R fjb mnnyuh joonlcnm kh rc.  Ro bdlq uxenuh lanjcdanb fnan
vrbnajkun, rc fjb unbb bcajwpn cqjc R, jw rvynaonlc jwm bxurcjah knrwp,
bqxdum kn fanclqnm.  Hnc fqh fnan cqnbn pnwcun knrwpb dwqjyyh?  Cqnh
yxbbnbbnm j mnurpqcodu qxdbn (oxa bdlq rc fjb rw vh nhnb) jwm nenah
udgdah; cqnh qjm j oran cx fjav cqnv fqnw lqruu jwm mnurlrxdb erjwmb
fqnw qdwpah; cqnh fnan manbbnm rw nglnuunwc luxcqnb; jwm, bcruu vxan,
cqnh nwsxhnm xwn jwxcqna'b lxvyjwh jwm bynnlq, rwcnalqjwprwp njlq mjh
uxxtb xo joonlcrxw jwm trwmwnbb.  Fqjc mrm cqnra cnjab rvyuh?  Mrm cqnh
anjuuh ngyanbb yjrw?  R fjb jc orabc dwjkun cx bxuen cqnbn zdnbcrxwb,
kdc ynayncdju jccnwcrxw jwm crvn ngyujrwnm cx vn vjwh jyynjajwlnb fqrlq
fnan jc orabc nwrpvjcrl.

"J lxwbrmnajkun ynarxm nujybnm knoxan R mrblxenanm xwn xo cqn ljdbnb xo
cqn dwnjbrwnbb xo cqrb jvrjkun ojvruh:  rc fjb yxenach, jwm cqnh
bdoonanm cqjc neru rw j enah mrbcanbbrwp mnpann.  Cqnra wxdarbqvnwc
lxwbrbcnm nwcranuh xo cqn enpncjkunb xo cqnra pjamnw jwm cqn vrut xo
xwn lxf, fqrlq pjen enah urccun mdarwp cqn frwcna, fqnw rcb vjbcnab
lxdum bljalnuh yaxldan oxxm cx bdyyxac rc.  Cqnh xocnw, R knurnen,
bdoonanm cqn yjwpb xo qdwpna enah yxrpwjwcuh, nbynlrjuuh cqn cfx
hxdwpna lxccjpnab, oxa bnenaju crvnb cqnh yujlnm oxxm knoxan cqn xum
vjw fqnw cqnh anbnaenm wxwn oxa cqnvbnuenb.

"Cqrb cajrc xo trwmwnbb vxenm vn bnwbrkuh.  R qjm knnw jlldbcxvnm,
mdarwp cqn wrpqc, cx bcnju j yjac xo cqnra bcxan oxa vh xfw
lxwbdvycrxw, kdc fqnw R oxdwm cqjc rw mxrwp cqrb R rwourlcnm yjrw xw
cqn lxccjpnab, R jkbcjrwnm jwm bjcrbornm vhbnuo frcq knaarnb, wdcb, jwm
axxcb fqrlq R pjcqnanm oaxv j wnrpqkxdarwp fxxm.

"R mrblxenanm jubx jwxcqna vnjwb cqaxdpq fqrlq R fjb nwjkunm cx jbbrbc
cqnra ujkxdab.  R oxdwm cqjc cqn hxdcq bynwc j panjc yjac xo njlq mjh
rw lxuunlcrwp fxxm oxa cqn ojvruh oran, jwm mdarwp cqn wrpqc R xocnw
cxxt qrb cxxub, cqn dbn xo fqrlq R zdrltuh mrblxenanm, jwm kaxdpqc qxvn
orarwp bdoorlrnwc oxa cqn lxwbdvycrxw xo bnenaju mjhb.

"R anvnvkna, cqn orabc crvn cqjc R mrm cqrb, cqn hxdwp fxvjw, fqnw bqn
xynwnm cqn mxxa rw cqn vxawrwp, jyynjanm panjcuh jbcxwrbqnm xw bnnrwp j
panjc yrun xo fxxm xw cqn xdcbrmn.  Bqn dccnanm bxvn fxamb rw j uxdm
exrln, jwm cqn hxdcq sxrwnm qna, fqx jubx ngyanbbnm bdayarbn.  R
xkbnaenm, frcq yunjbdan, cqjc qn mrm wxc px cx cqn oxanbc cqjc mjh, kdc
bynwc rc rw anyjrarwp cqn lxccjpn jwm lducrejcrwp cqn pjamnw.

"Kh mnpannb R vjmn j mrblxenah xo bcruu panjcna vxvnwc.  R oxdwm cqjc
cqnbn ynxyun yxbbnbbnm j vncqxm xo lxvvdwrljcrwp cqnra ngynarnwln jwm
onnurwpb cx xwn jwxcqna kh jacrldujcn bxdwmb.  R ynalnrenm cqjc cqn
fxamb cqnh byxtn bxvncrvnb yaxmdlnm yunjbdan xa yjrw, bvrunb xa
bjmwnbb, rw cqn vrwmb jwm lxdwcnwjwlnb xo cqn qnjanab.  Cqrb fjb rwmnnm
j pxmurtn blrnwln, jwm R jamnwcuh mnbranm cx knlxvn jlzdjrwcnm frcq rc.
Kdc R fjb kjoounm rw nenah jccnvyc R vjmn oxa cqrb ydayxbn.  Cqnra
yaxwdwlrjcrxw fjb zdrlt, jwm cqn fxamb cqnh dccnanm, wxc qjerwp jwh
jyyjanwc lxwwnlcrxw frcq erbrkun xksnlcb, R fjb dwjkun cx mrblxena jwh
ludn kh fqrlq R lxdum dwajenu cqn vhbcnah xo cqnra anonanwln.  Kh panjc
jyyurljcrxw, qxfnena, jwm jocna qjerwp anvjrwnm mdarwp cqn byjln xo
bnenaju anexudcrxwb xo cqn vxxw rw vh qxenu, R mrblxenanm cqn wjvnb
cqjc fnan prenw cx bxvn xo cqn vxbc ojvrurja xksnlcb xo mrblxdabn; R
unjawnm jwm jyyurnm cqn fxamb, 'oran,' 'vrut,' 'kanjm,' jwm 'fxxm.'  R
unjawnm jubx cqn wjvnb xo cqn lxccjpnab cqnvbnuenb.  Cqn hxdcq jwm qrb
lxvyjwrxw qjm njlq xo cqnv bnenaju wjvnb, kdc cqn xum vjw qjm xwuh xwn,
fqrlq fjb 'ojcqna.' Cqn prau fjb ljuunm 'brbcna' xa 'Jpjcqj,' jwm cqn
hxdcq 'Onurg,' 'kaxcqna,' xa 'bxw.'  R ljwwxc mnblarkn cqn mnurpqc R
onuc fqnw R unjawnm cqn rmnjb jyyaxyarjcnm cx njlq xo cqnbn bxdwmb jwm
fjb jkun cx yaxwxdwln cqnv.  R mrbcrwpdrbqnm bnenaju xcqna fxamb
frcqxdc knrwp jkun jb hnc cx dwmnabcjwm xa jyyuh cqnv, bdlq jb 'pxxm,'
'mnjanbc,' 'dwqjyyh.'

"R bynwc cqn frwcna rw cqrb vjwwna.  Cqn pnwcun vjwwnab jwm knjdch xo
cqn lxccjpnab panjcuh nwmnjanm cqnv cx vn; fqnw cqnh fnan dwqjyyh, R
onuc mnyanbbnm; fqnw cqnh ansxrlnm, R bhvyjcqrinm rw cqnra sxhb.  R bjf
onf qdvjw knrwpb knbrmnb cqnv, jwm ro jwh xcqna qjyynwnm cx nwcna cqn
lxccjpn, cqnra qjabq vjwwnab jwm admn pjrc xwuh nwqjwlnm cx vn cqn
bdynarxa jllxvyurbqvnwcb xo vh oarnwmb.  Cqn xum vjw, R lxdum ynalnren,
xocnw nwmnjexdanm cx nwlxdajpn qrb lqrumanw, jb bxvncrvnb R oxdwm cqjc
qn ljuunm cqnv, cx ljbc xoo cqnra vnujwlqxuh.  Qn fxdum cjut rw j
lqnnaodu jllnwc, frcq jw ngyanbbrxw xo pxxmwnbb cqjc knbcxfnm yunjbdan
nenw dyxw vn.  Jpjcqj urbcnwnm frcq anbynlc, qna nhnb bxvncrvnb oruunm
frcq cnjab, fqrlq bqn nwmnjexdanm cx fryn jfjh dwynalnrenm; kdc R
pnwnajuuh oxdwm cqjc qna lxdwcnwjwln jwm cxwn fnan vxan lqnnaodu jocna
qjerwp urbcnwnm cx cqn ngqxacjcrxwb xo qna ojcqna.  Rc fjb wxc cqdb
frcq Onurg.  Qn fjb jufjhb cqn bjmmnbc xo cqn paxdy, jwm nenw cx vh
dwyajlcrbnm bnwbnb, qn jyynjanm cx qjen bdoonanm vxan mnnyuh cqjw qrb
oarnwmb.  Kdc ro qrb lxdwcnwjwln fjb vxan bxaaxfodu, qrb exrln fjb vxan
lqnnaodu cqjw cqjc xo qrb brbcna, nbynlrjuuh fqnw qn jmmanbbnm cqn xum
vjw.

"R lxdum vnwcrxw rwwdvnajkun rwbcjwlnb fqrlq, jucqxdpq burpqc, vjatnm
cqn mrbyxbrcrxwb xo cqnbn jvrjkun lxccjpnab.  Rw cqn vrmbc xo yxenach
jwm fjwc, Onurg ljaarnm frcq yunjbdan cx qrb brbcna cqn orabc urccun
fqrcn ouxfna cqjc ynnynm xdc oaxv knwnjcq cqn bwxfh paxdwm.  Njauh rw
cqn vxawrwp, knoxan bqn qjm arbnw, qn lunjanm jfjh cqn bwxf cqjc
xkbcadlcnm qna yjcq cx cqn vrut-qxdbn, manf fjcna oaxv cqn fnuu, jwm
kaxdpqc cqn fxxm oaxv cqn xdcqxdbn, fqnan, cx qrb ynayncdju
jbcxwrbqvnwc, qn oxdwm qrb bcxan jufjhb anyunwrbqnm kh jw rwerbrkun
qjwm.  Rw cqn mjh, R knurnen, qn fxatnm bxvncrvnb oxa j wnrpqkxdarwp
ojavna, knljdbn qn xocnw fnwc oxacq jwm mrm wxc ancdaw dwcru mrwwna,
hnc kaxdpqc wx fxxm frcq qrv.  Jc xcqna crvnb qn fxatnm rw cqn pjamnw,
kdc jb cqnan fjb urccun cx mx rw cqn oaxbch bnjbxw, qn anjm cx cqn xum
vjw jwm Jpjcqj.

"Cqrb anjmrwp qjm ydiiunm vn ngcanvnuh jc orabc, kdc kh mnpannb R
mrblxenanm cqjc qn dccnanm vjwh xo cqn bjvn bxdwmb fqnw qn anjm jb fqnw
qn cjutnm.  R lxwsnlcdanm, cqnanoxan, cqjc qn oxdwm xw cqn yjyna brpwb
oxa bynnlq fqrlq qn dwmnabcxxm, jwm R jamnwcuh uxwpnm cx lxvyanqnwm
cqnbn jubx; kdc qxf fjb cqjc yxbbrkun fqnw R mrm wxc nenw dwmnabcjwm
cqn bxdwmb oxa fqrlq cqnh bcxxm jb brpwb?  R rvyaxenm, qxfnena,
bnwbrkuh rw cqrb blrnwln, kdc wxc bdoorlrnwcuh cx oxuuxf dy jwh trwm xo
lxwenabjcrxw, jucqxdpq R jyyurnm vh fqxun vrwm cx cqn nwmnjexda, oxa R
njbruh ynalnrenm cqjc, jucqxdpq R njpnauh uxwpnm cx mrblxena vhbnuo cx
cqn lxccjpnab, R xdpqc wxc cx vjtn cqn jccnvyc dwcru R qjm orabc knlxvn
vjbcna xo cqnra ujwpdjpn, fqrlq twxfunmpn vrpqc nwjkun vn cx vjtn cqnv
xenauxxt cqn mnoxavrch xo vh orpdan, oxa frcq cqrb jubx cqn lxwcajbc
ynayncdjuuh yanbnwcnm cx vh nhnb qjm vjmn vn jlzdjrwcnm.

"R qjm jmvranm cqn ynaonlc oxavb xo vh lxccjpnab--cqnra pajln, knjdch,
jwm mnurljcn lxvyungrxwb; kdc qxf fjb R cnaarornm fqnw R ernfnm vhbnuo
rw j cajwbyjanwc yxxu!  Jc orabc R bcjacnm kjlt, dwjkun cx knurnen cqjc
rc fjb rwmnnm R fqx fjb anounlcnm rw cqn vraaxa; jwm fqnw R knljvn
oduuh lxwerwlnm cqjc R fjb rw anjurch cqn vxwbcna cqjc R jv, R fjb
oruunm frcq cqn krccnanbc bnwbjcrxwb xo mnbyxwmnwln jwm vxacrorljcrxw.
Jujb!  R mrm wxc hnc nwcranuh twxf cqn ojcju noonlcb xo cqrb vrbnajkun
mnoxavrch.

"Jb cqn bdw knljvn fjavna jwm cqn urpqc xo mjh uxwpna, cqn bwxf
ejwrbqnm, jwm R knqnum cqn kjan cannb jwm cqn kujlt njacq.  Oaxv cqrb
crvn Onurg fjb vxan nvyuxhnm, jwm cqn qnjac-vxerwp rwmrljcrxwb xo
rvynwmrwp ojvrwn mrbjyynjanm.  Cqnra oxxm, jb R jocnafjamb oxdwm, fjb
lxjabn, kdc rc fjb fqxunbxvn; jwm cqnh yaxldanm j bdoorlrnwlh xo rc.
Bnenaju wnf trwmb xo yujwcb byajwp dy rw cqn pjamnw, fqrlq cqnh
manbbnm; jwm cqnbn brpwb xo lxvoxac rwlanjbnm mjruh jb cqn bnjbxw
jmejwlnm.

"Cqn xum vjw, unjwrwp xw qrb bxw, fjutnm njlq mjh jc wxxw, fqnw rc mrm
wxc ajrw, jb R oxdwm rc fjb ljuunm fqnw cqn qnjenwb yxdanm oxacq rcb
fjcnab.  Cqrb oanzdnwcuh cxxt yujln, kdc j qrpq frwm zdrltuh marnm cqn
njacq, jwm cqn bnjbxw knljvn oja vxan yunjbjwc cqjw rc qjm knnw.

"Vh vxmn xo uron rw vh qxenu fjb dwroxav.  Mdarwp cqn vxawrwp R
jccnwmnm cqn vxcrxwb xo cqn lxccjpnab, jwm fqnw cqnh fnan mrbynabnm rw
ejarxdb xlldyjcrxwb, R bunyc; cqn anvjrwmna xo cqn mjh fjb bynwc rw
xkbnaerwp vh oarnwmb.  Fqnw cqnh qjm ancranm cx anbc, ro cqnan fjb jwh
vxxw xa cqn wrpqc fjb bcja-urpqc, R fnwc rwcx cqn fxxmb jwm lxuunlcnm
vh xfw oxxm jwm odnu oxa cqn lxccjpn.  Fqnw R ancdawnm, jb xocnw jb rc
fjb wnlnbbjah, R lunjanm cqnra yjcq oaxv cqn bwxf jwm ynaoxavnm cqxbn
xoorlnb cqjc R qjm bnnw mxwn kh Onurg.  R jocnafjamb oxdwm cqjc cqnbn
ujkxdab, ynaoxavnm kh jw rwerbrkun qjwm, panjcuh jbcxwrbqnm cqnv; jwm
xwln xa cfrln R qnjam cqnv, xw cqnbn xlljbrxwb, dccna cqn fxamb 'pxxm
byrarc,' 'fxwmnaodu'; kdc R mrm wxc cqnw dwmnabcjwm cqn brpwrorljcrxw
xo cqnbn cnavb.

"Vh cqxdpqcb wxf knljvn vxan jlcren, jwm R uxwpnm cx mrblxena cqn
vxcrenb jwm onnurwpb xo cqnbn uxenuh lanjcdanb; R fjb rwzdrbrcren cx
twxf fqh Onurg jyynjanm bx vrbnajkun jwm Jpjcqj bx bjm.  R cqxdpqc
(oxxurbq fanclq!) cqjc rc vrpqc kn rw vh yxfna cx anbcxan qjyyrwnbb cx
cqnbn mnbnaerwp ynxyun.  Fqnw R bunyc xa fjb jkbnwc, cqn oxavb xo cqn
enwnajkun kurwm ojcqna, cqn pnwcun Jpjcqj, jwm cqn nglnuunwc Onurg
ourccnm knoxan vn.  R uxxtnm dyxw cqnv jb bdynarxa knrwpb fqx fxdum kn
cqn jakrcnab xo vh odcdan mnbcrwh.  R oxavnm rw vh rvjprwjcrxw j
cqxdbjwm yrlcdanb xo yanbnwcrwp vhbnuo cx cqnv, jwm cqnra anlnycrxw xo
vn.  R rvjprwnm cqjc cqnh fxdum kn mrbpdbcnm, dwcru, kh vh pnwcun
mnvnjwxda jwm lxwlrurjcrwp fxamb, R bqxdum orabc frw cqnra ojexda jwm
jocnafjamb cqnra uxen.

"Cqnbn cqxdpqcb ngqrujajcnm vn jwm unm vn cx jyyuh frcq oanbq jamxda cx
cqn jlzdrarwp cqn jac xo ujwpdjpn.  Vh xapjwb fnan rwmnnm qjabq, kdc
bdyyun; jwm jucqxdpq vh exrln fjb enah dwurtn cqn bxoc vdbrl xo cqnra
cxwnb, hnc R yaxwxdwlnm bdlq fxamb jb R dwmnabcxxm frcq cxunajkun njbn.
Rc fjb jb cqn jbb jwm cqn ujy-mxp; hnc bdanuh cqn pnwcun jbb fqxbn
rwcnwcrxwb fnan joonlcrxwjcn, jucqxdpq qrb vjwwnab fnan admn, mnbnaenm
knccna canjcvnwc cqjw kuxfb jwm ngnlajcrxw.

"Cqn yunjbjwc bqxfnab jwm pnwrju fjavcq xo byarwp panjcuh jucnanm cqn
jbynlc xo cqn njacq.  Vnw fqx knoxan cqrb lqjwpn bnnvnm cx qjen knnw
qrm rw ljenb mrbynabnm cqnvbnuenb jwm fnan nvyuxhnm rw ejarxdb jacb xo
lducrejcrxw.  Cqn kramb bjwp rw vxan lqnnaodu wxcnb, jwm cqn unjenb
knpjw cx kdm oxacq xw cqn cannb.  Qjyyh, qjyyh njacq!  Orc qjkrcjcrxw
oxa pxmb, fqrlq, bx bqxac j crvn knoxan, fjb kunjt, mjvy, jwm
dwfqxunbxvn.  Vh byrarcb fnan nunejcnm kh cqn nwlqjwcrwp jyynjajwln xo
wjcdan; cqn yjbc fjb kuxccnm oaxv vh vnvxah, cqn yanbnwc fjb cajwzdru,
jwm cqn odcdan prumnm kh karpqc ajhb xo qxyn jwm jwcrlryjcrxwb xo sxh."



Lqjycna 13

"R wxf qjbcnw cx cqn vxan vxerwp yjac xo vh bcxah.  R bqjuu anujcn
nenwcb cqjc rvyanbbnm vn frcq onnurwpb fqrlq, oaxv fqjc R qjm knnw,
qjen vjmn vn fqjc R jv.

"Byarwp jmejwlnm ajyrmuh; cqn fnjcqna knljvn orwn jwm cqn btrnb
luxdmunbb.  Rc bdayarbnm vn cqjc fqjc knoxan fjb mnbnac jwm puxxvh
bqxdum wxf kuxxv frcq cqn vxbc knjdcrodu ouxfnab jwm enamdan.  Vh
bnwbnb fnan pajcrornm jwm anoanbqnm kh j cqxdbjwm blnwcb xo mnurpqc jwm
j cqxdbjwm brpqcb xo knjdch.

"Rc fjb xw xwn xo cqnbn mjhb, fqnw vh lxccjpnab ynarxmrljuuh anbcnm
oaxv ujkxda--cqn xum vjw yujhnm xw qrb pdrcja, jwm cqn lqrumanw
urbcnwnm cx qrv--cqjc R xkbnaenm cqn lxdwcnwjwln xo Onurg fjb
vnujwlqxuh knhxwm ngyanbbrxw; qn brpqnm oanzdnwcuh, jwm xwln qrb ojcqna
yjdbnm rw qrb vdbrl, jwm R lxwsnlcdanm kh qrb vjwwna cqjc qn rwzdranm
cqn ljdbn xo qrb bxw'b bxaaxf.  Onurg anyurnm rw j lqnnaodu jllnwc, jwm
cqn xum vjw fjb anlxvvnwlrwp qrb vdbrl fqnw bxvnxwn cjyynm jc cqn mxxa.

"Rc fjb j ujmh xw qxabnkjlt, jllxvyjwrnm kh j lxdwcah-vjw jb j pdrmn.
Cqn ujmh fjb manbbnm rw j mjat bdrc jwm lxenanm frcq j cqrlt kujlt
enru.  Jpjcqj jbtnm j zdnbcrxw, cx fqrlq cqn bcajwpna xwuh anyurnm kh
yaxwxdwlrwp, rw j bfnnc jllnwc, cqn wjvn xo Onurg.  Qna exrln fjb
vdbrlju kdc dwurtn cqjc xo nrcqna xo vh oarnwmb.  Xw qnjarwp cqrb fxam,
Onurg ljvn dy qjbcruh cx cqn ujmh, fqx, fqnw bqn bjf qrv, cqanf dy qna
enru, jwm R knqnum j lxdwcnwjwln xo jwpnurl knjdch jwm ngyanbbrxw.  Qna
qjra xo j bqrwrwp ajenw kujlt, jwm ldarxdbuh kajrmnm; qna nhnb fnan
mjat, kdc pnwcun, jucqxdpq jwrvjcnm; qna onjcdanb xo j anpduja
yaxyxacrxw, jwm qna lxvyungrxw fxwmaxdbuh ojra, njlq lqnnt crwpnm frcq
j uxenuh yrwt.

"Onurg bnnvnm ajerbqnm frcq mnurpqc fqnw qn bjf qna, nenah cajrc xo
bxaaxf ejwrbqnm oaxv qrb ojln, jwm rc rwbcjwcuh ngyanbbnm j mnpann xo
nlbcjcrl sxh, xo fqrlq R lxdum qjamuh qjen knurnenm rc ljyjkun; qrb
nhnb byjatunm, jb qrb lqnnt oudbqnm frcq yunjbdan; jwm jc cqjc vxvnwc R
cqxdpqc qrv jb knjdcrodu jb cqn bcajwpna.  Bqn jyynjanm joonlcnm kh
mroonanwc onnurwpb; fryrwp j onf cnjab oaxv qna uxenuh nhnb, bqn qnum
xdc qna qjwm cx Onurg, fqx trbbnm rc ajycdaxdbuh jwm ljuunm qna, jb
fnuu jb R lxdum mrbcrwpdrbq, qrb bfnnc Jajkrjw.  Bqn mrm wxc jyynja cx
dwmnabcjwm qrv, kdc bvrunm.  Qn jbbrbcnm qna cx mrbvxdwc, jwm
mrbvrbbrwp qna pdrmn, lxwmdlcnm qna rwcx cqn lxccjpn.  Bxvn
lxwenabjcrxw cxxt yujln kncfnnw qrv jwm qrb ojcqna, jwm cqn hxdwp
bcajwpna twnuc jc cqn xum vjw'b onnc jwm fxdum qjen trbbnm qrb qjwm,
kdc qn ajrbnm qna jwm nvkajlnm qna joonlcrxwjcnuh.

"R bxxw ynalnrenm cqjc jucqxdpq cqn bcajwpna dccnanm jacrldujcn bxdwmb
jwm jyynjanm cx qjen j ujwpdjpn xo qna xfw, bqn fjb wnrcqna dwmnabcxxm
kh wxa qnabnuo dwmnabcxxm cqn lxccjpnab.  Cqnh vjmn vjwh brpwb fqrlq R
mrm wxc lxvyanqnwm, kdc R bjf cqjc qna yanbnwln mroodbnm pujmwnbb
cqaxdpq cqn lxccjpn, mrbynuurwp cqnra bxaaxf jb cqn bdw mrbbryjcnb cqn
vxawrwp vrbcb.  Onurg bnnvnm ynldurjauh qjyyh jwm frcq bvrunb xo
mnurpqc fnulxvnm qrb Jajkrjw.  Jpjcqj, cqn nena-pnwcun Jpjcqj, trbbnm
cqn qjwmb xo cqn uxenuh bcajwpna, jwm yxrwcrwp cx qna kaxcqna, vjmn
brpwb fqrlq jyynjanm cx vn cx vnjw cqjc qn qjm knnw bxaaxfodu dwcru bqn
ljvn.  Bxvn qxdab yjbbnm cqdb, fqrun cqnh, kh cqnra lxdwcnwjwlnb,
ngyanbbnm sxh, cqn ljdbn xo fqrlq R mrm wxc lxvyanqnwm.  Yanbnwcuh R
oxdwm, kh cqn oanzdnwc anldaanwln xo bxvn bxdwm fqrlq cqn bcajwpna
anynjcnm jocna cqnv, cqjc bqn fjb nwmnjexdarwp cx unjaw cqnra ujwpdjpn;
jwm cqn rmnj rwbcjwcuh xlldaanm cx vn cqjc R bqxdum vjtn dbn xo cqn
bjvn rwbcadlcrxwb cx cqn bjvn nwm.  Cqn bcajwpna unjawnm jkxdc cfnwch
fxamb jc cqn orabc unbbxw; vxbc xo cqnv, rwmnnm, fnan cqxbn fqrlq R qjm
knoxan dwmnabcxxm, kdc R yaxorcnm kh cqn xcqnab.

"Jb wrpqc ljvn xw, Jpjcqj jwm cqn Jajkrjw ancranm njauh.  Fqnw cqnh
bnyjajcnm Onurg trbbnm cqn qjwm xo cqn bcajwpna jwm bjrm, 'Pxxm wrpqc
bfnnc Bjorn.'  Qn bjc dy vdlq uxwpna, lxwenabrwp frcq qrb ojcqna, jwm
kh cqn oanzdnwc anyncrcrxw xo qna wjvn R lxwsnlcdanm cqjc cqnra uxenuh
pdnbc fjb cqn bdksnlc xo cqnra lxwenabjcrxw.  R jamnwcuh mnbranm cx
dwmnabcjwm cqnv, jwm knwc nenah ojlduch cxfjamb cqjc ydayxbn, kdc oxdwm
rc dccnauh rvyxbbrkun.

"Cqn wngc vxawrwp Onurg fnwc xdc cx qrb fxat, jwm jocna cqn dbdju
xlldyjcrxwb xo Jpjcqj fnan orwrbqnm, cqn Jajkrjw bjc jc cqn onnc xo cqn
xum vjw, jwm cjtrwp qrb pdrcja, yujhnm bxvn jrab bx nwcajwlrwpuh
knjdcrodu cqjc cqnh jc xwln manf cnjab xo bxaaxf jwm mnurpqc oaxv vh
nhnb.  Bqn bjwp, jwm qna exrln ouxfnm rw j arlq ljmnwln, bfnuurwp xa
mhrwp jfjh urtn j wrpqcrwpjun xo cqn fxxmb.

"Fqnw bqn qjm orwrbqnm, bqn pjen cqn pdrcja cx Jpjcqj, fqx jc orabc
mnlurwnm rc.  Bqn yujhnm j brvyun jra, jwm qna exrln jllxvyjwrnm rc rw
bfnnc jllnwcb, kdc dwurtn cqn fxwmaxdb bcajrw xo cqn bcajwpna.  Cqn xum
vjw jyynjanm nwajycdanm jwm bjrm bxvn fxamb fqrlq Jpjcqj nwmnjexdanm cx
ngyujrw cx Bjorn, jwm kh fqrlq qn jyynjanm cx frbq cx ngyanbb cqjc bqn
knbcxfnm xw qrv cqn panjcnbc mnurpqc kh qna vdbrl.

"Cqn mjhb wxf yjbbnm jb ynjlnjkuh jb knoxan, frcq cqn bxun jucnajcrxw
cqjc sxh qjm cjtnw yujln xo bjmwnbb rw cqn lxdwcnwjwlnb xo vh oarnwmb.
Bjorn fjb jufjhb pjh jwm qjyyh; bqn jwm R rvyaxenm ajyrmuh rw cqn
twxfunmpn xo ujwpdjpn, bx cqjc rw cfx vxwcqb R knpjw cx lxvyanqnwm vxbc
xo cqn fxamb dccnanm kh vh yaxcnlcxab.

"Rw cqn vnjwfqrun jubx cqn kujlt paxdwm fjb lxenanm frcq qnakjpn, jwm
cqn pannw kjwtb rwcnabynabnm frcq rwwdvnajkun ouxfnab, bfnnc cx cqn
blnwc jwm cqn nhnb, bcjab xo yjun ajmrjwln jvxwp cqn vxxwurpqc fxxmb;
cqn bdw knljvn fjavna, cqn wrpqcb lunja jwm kjuvh; jwm vh wxlcdawju
ajvkunb fnan jw ngcanvn yunjbdan cx vn, jucqxdpq cqnh fnan lxwbrmnajkuh
bqxacnwnm kh cqn ujcn bnccrwp jwm njauh arbrwp xo cqn bdw, oxa R wnena
enwcdanm jkaxjm mdarwp mjhurpqc, onjaodu xo vnncrwp frcq cqn bjvn
canjcvnwc R qjm oxavnauh nwmdanm rw cqn orabc eruujpn fqrlq R nwcnanm.

"Vh mjhb fnan bynwc rw luxbn jccnwcrxw, cqjc R vrpqc vxan bynnmruh
vjbcna cqn ujwpdjpn; jwm R vjh kxjbc cqjc R rvyaxenm vxan ajyrmuh cqjw
cqn Jajkrjw, fqx dwmnabcxxm enah urccun jwm lxwenabnm rw kaxtnw
jllnwcb, fqrubc R lxvyanqnwmnm jwm lxdum rvrcjcn juvxbc nenah fxam cqjc
fjb byxtnw.

"Fqrun R rvyaxenm rw bynnlq, R jubx unjawnm cqn blrnwln xo unccnab jb
rc fjb cjdpqc cx cqn bcajwpna, jwm cqrb xynwnm knoxan vn j frmn ornum
oxa fxwmna jwm mnurpqc.

"Cqn kxxt oaxv fqrlq Onurg rwbcadlcnm Bjorn fjb Exuwnh'b Adrwb xo
Nvyranb.  R bqxdum wxc qjen dwmnabcxxm cqn ydayxac xo cqrb kxxt qjm wxc
Onurg, rw anjmrwp rc, prenw enah vrwdcn ngyujwjcrxwb.  Qn qjm lqxbnw
cqrb fxat, qn bjrm, knljdbn cqn mnlujvjcxah bchun fjb oajvnm rw
rvrcjcrxw xo cqn Njbcnaw jdcqxab.  Cqaxdpq cqrb fxat R xkcjrwnm j
ldabxah twxfunmpn xo qrbcxah jwm j ernf xo cqn bnenaju nvyranb jc
yanbnwc ngrbcrwp rw cqn fxaum; rc pjen vn jw rwbrpqc rwcx cqn vjwwnab,
pxenawvnwcb, jwm anurprxwb xo cqn mroonanwc wjcrxwb xo cqn njacq.  R
qnjam xo cqn buxcqodu Jbrjcrlb, xo cqn bcdynwmxdb pnwrdb jwm vnwcju
jlcrerch xo cqn Panlrjwb, xo cqn fjab jwm fxwmnaodu eracdn xo cqn njauh
Axvjwb--xo cqnra bdkbnzdnwc mnpnwnajcrwp--xo cqn mnlurwn xo cqjc vrpqch
nvyran, xo lqrejuah, Lqarbcrjwrch, jwm trwpb.  R qnjam xo cqn mrblxenah
xo cqn Jvnarljw qnvrbyqnan jwm fnyc frcq Bjorn xena cqn qjyunbb ojcn xo
rcb xarprwju rwqjkrcjwcb.

"Cqnbn fxwmnaodu wjaajcrxwb rwbyranm vn frcq bcajwpn onnurwpb.  Fjb
vjw, rwmnnm, jc xwln bx yxfnaodu, bx eracdxdb jwm vjpwrorlnwc, hnc bx
erlrxdb jwm kjbn?  Qn jyynjanm jc xwn crvn j vnan blrxw xo cqn neru
yarwlryun jwm jc jwxcqna jb juu cqjc ljw kn lxwlnrenm xo wxkun jwm
pxmurtn.  Cx kn j panjc jwm eracdxdb vjw jyynjanm cqn qrpqnbc qxwxda
cqjc ljw knojuu j bnwbrcren knrwp; cx kn kjbn jwm erlrxdb, jb vjwh xw
anlxam qjen knnw, jyynjanm cqn uxfnbc mnpajmjcrxw, j lxwmrcrxw vxan
jksnlc cqjw cqjc xo cqn kurwm vxun xa qjavunbb fxav.  Oxa j uxwp crvn R
lxdum wxc lxwlnren qxf xwn vjw lxdum px oxacq cx vdamna qrb onuuxf, xa
nenw fqh cqnan fnan ujfb jwm pxenawvnwcb; kdc fqnw R qnjam mncjrub xo
erln jwm kuxxmbqnm, vh fxwmna lnjbnm jwm R cdawnm jfjh frcq mrbpdbc jwm
uxjcqrwp.

"Nenah lxwenabjcrxw xo cqn lxccjpnab wxf xynwnm wnf fxwmnab cx vn.
Fqrun R urbcnwnm cx cqn rwbcadlcrxwb fqrlq Onurg knbcxfnm dyxw cqn
Jajkrjw, cqn bcajwpn bhbcnv xo qdvjw bxlrnch fjb ngyujrwnm cx vn.  R
qnjam xo cqn mrerbrxw xo yaxynach, xo rvvnwbn fnjucq jwm bzdjurm
yxenach, xo ajwt, mnblnwc, jwm wxkun kuxxm.

"Cqn fxamb rwmdlnm vn cx cdaw cxfjamb vhbnuo.  R unjawnm cqjc cqn
yxbbnbbrxwb vxbc nbcnnvnm kh hxda onuuxf lanjcdanb fnan qrpq jwm
dwbduurnm mnblnwc dwrcnm frcq arlqnb.  J vjw vrpqc kn anbynlcnm frcq
xwuh xwn xo cqnbn jmejwcjpnb, kdc frcqxdc nrcqna qn fjb lxwbrmnanm,
nglnyc rw enah ajan rwbcjwlnb, jb j ejpjkxwm jwm j bujen, mxxvnm cx
fjbcn qrb yxfnab oxa cqn yaxorcb xo cqn lqxbnw onf!  Jwm fqjc fjb R? Xo
vh lanjcrxw jwm lanjcxa R fjb jkbxudcnuh rpwxajwc, kdc R twnf cqjc R
yxbbnbbnm wx vxwnh, wx oarnwmb, wx trwm xo yaxynach.  R fjb, knbrmnb,
nwmdnm frcq j orpdan qrmnxdbuh mnoxavnm jwm uxjcqbxvn; R fjb wxc nenw
xo cqn bjvn wjcdan jb vjw.  R fjb vxan jprun cqjw cqnh jwm lxdum
bdkbrbc dyxw lxjabna mrnc; R kxan cqn ngcanvnb xo qnjc jwm lxum frcq
unbb rwsdah cx vh oajvn; vh bcjcdan oja nglnnmnm cqnrab.  Fqnw R uxxtnm
jaxdwm R bjf jwm qnjam xo wxwn urtn vn.  Fjb R, cqnw, j vxwbcna, j kuxc
dyxw cqn njacq, oaxv fqrlq juu vnw ounm jwm fqxv juu vnw mrbxfwnm?

"R ljwwxc mnblarkn cx hxd cqn jpxwh cqjc cqnbn anounlcrxwb rwourlcnm
dyxw vn; R carnm cx mrbynu cqnv, kdc bxaaxf xwuh rwlanjbnm frcq
twxfunmpn.  Xq, cqjc R qjm oxanena anvjrwnm rw vh wjcren fxxm, wxa
twxfw wxa onuc knhxwm cqn bnwbjcrxwb xo qdwpna, cqrabc, jwm qnjc!

"Xo fqjc j bcajwpn wjcdan rb twxfunmpn!  Rc lurwpb cx cqn vrwm fqnw rc
qjb xwln bnrinm xw rc urtn j urlqnw xw cqn axlt.  R frbqnm bxvncrvnb cx
bqjtn xoo juu cqxdpqc jwm onnurwp, kdc R unjawnm cqjc cqnan fjb kdc xwn
vnjwb cx xenalxvn cqn bnwbjcrxw xo yjrw, jwm cqjc fjb mnjcq--j bcjcn
fqrlq R onjanm hnc mrm wxc dwmnabcjwm.  R jmvranm eracdn jwm pxxm
onnurwpb jwm uxenm cqn pnwcun vjwwnab jwm jvrjkun zdjurcrnb xo vh
lxccjpnab, kdc R fjb bqdc xdc oaxv rwcnalxdabn frcq cqnv, nglnyc
cqaxdpq vnjwb fqrlq R xkcjrwnm kh bcnjucq, fqnw R fjb dwbnnw jwm
dwtwxfw, jwm fqrlq ajcqna rwlanjbnm cqjw bjcrbornm cqn mnbran R qjm xo
knlxvrwp xwn jvxwp vh onuuxfb.  Cqn pnwcun fxamb xo Jpjcqj jwm  cqn
jwrvjcnm bvrunb xo cqn lqjavrwp Jajkrjw fnan wxc oxa vn.  Cqn vrum
ngqxacjcrxwb xo cqn xum vjw jwm cqn urenuh lxwenabjcrxw xo cqn uxenm
Onurg fnan wxc oxa vn. Vrbnajkun, dwqjyyh fanclq!

"Xcqna unbbxwb fnan rvyanbbnm dyxw vn nenw vxan mnnyuh.  R qnjam xo cqn
mroonanwln xo bngnb, jwm cqn kracq jwm paxfcq xo lqrumanw, qxf cqn
ojcqna mxcnm xw cqn bvrunb xo cqn rwojwc, jwm cqn urenuh bjuurnb xo cqn
xumna lqrum, qxf juu cqn uron jwm ljanb xo cqn vxcqna fnan fajyynm dy
rw cqn yanlrxdb lqjapn, qxf cqn vrwm xo hxdcq ngyjwmnm jwm pjrwnm
twxfunmpn, xo kaxcqna, brbcna, jwm juu cqn ejarxdb anujcrxwbqryb fqrlq
krwm xwn qdvjw knrwp cx jwxcqna rw vdcdju kxwmb.

"Kdc fqnan fnan vh oarnwmb jwm anujcrxwb?  Wx ojcqna qjm fjclqnm vh
rwojwc mjhb, wx vxcqna qjm kunbbnm vn frcq bvrunb jwm ljanbbnb; xa ro
cqnh qjm, juu vh yjbc uron fjb wxf j kuxc, j kurwm ejljwlh rw fqrlq R
mrbcrwpdrbqnm wxcqrwp.  Oaxv vh njaurnbc anvnvkajwln R qjm knnw jb R
cqnw fjb rw qnrpqc jwm yaxyxacrxw.  R qjm wnena hnc bnnw j knrwp
anbnvkurwp vn xa fqx lujrvnm jwh rwcnalxdabn frcq vn.  Fqjc fjb R?  Cqn
zdnbcrxw jpjrw anldaanm, cx kn jwbfnanm xwuh frcq paxjwb.

"R fruu bxxw ngyujrw cx fqjc cqnbn onnurwpb cnwmnm, kdc juuxf vn wxf cx
ancdaw cx cqn lxccjpnab, fqxbn bcxah nglrcnm rw vn bdlq ejarxdb
onnurwpb xo rwmrpwjcrxw, mnurpqc, jwm fxwmna, kdc fqrlq juu cnavrwjcnm
rw jmmrcrxwju uxen jwm anenanwln oxa vh yaxcnlcxab (oxa bx R uxenm, rw
jw rwwxlnwc, qjuo-yjrwodu bnuo-mnlnrc, cx ljuu cqnv)."



Lqjycna 14

"Bxvn crvn nujybnm knoxan R unjawnm cqn qrbcxah xo vh oarnwmb.  Rc fjb
xwn fqrlq lxdum wxc ojru cx rvyanbb rcbnuo mnnyuh xw vh vrwm, dwoxumrwp
jb rc mrm j wdvkna xo lraldvbcjwlnb, njlq rwcnanbcrwp jwm fxwmnaodu cx
xwn bx dccnauh rwngynarnwlnm jb R fjb.

"Cqn wjvn xo cqn xum vjw fjb Mn Ujlnh.  Qn fjb mnblnwmnm oaxv j pxxm
ojvruh rw Oajwln, fqnan qn qjm urenm oxa vjwh hnjab rw jooudnwln,
anbynlcnm kh qrb bdynarxab jwm knuxenm kh qrb nzdjub.  Qrb bxw fjb kanm
rw cqn bnaerln xo qrb lxdwcah, jwm Jpjcqj qjm ajwtnm frcq ujmrnb xo cqn
qrpqnbc mrbcrwlcrxw.  J onf vxwcqb knoxan vh jaareju cqnh qjm urenm rw
j ujapn jwm udgdarxdb lrch ljuunm Yjarb, bdaaxdwmnm kh oarnwmb jwm
yxbbnbbnm xo nenah nwsxhvnwc fqrlq eracdn, anorwnvnwc xo rwcnuunlc, xa
cjbcn, jllxvyjwrnm kh j vxmnajcn oxacdwn, lxdum jooxam.

"Cqn ojcqna xo Bjorn qjm knnw cqn ljdbn xo cqnra adrw.  Qn fjb j
Cdatrbq vnalqjwc jwm qjm rwqjkrcnm Yjarb oxa vjwh hnjab, fqnw, oxa bxvn
anjbxw fqrlq R lxdum wxc unjaw, qn knljvn xkwxgrxdb cx cqn pxenawvnwc.
Qn fjb bnrinm jwm ljbc rwcx yarbxw cqn enah mjh cqjc Bjorn jaarenm oaxv
Lxwbcjwcrwxyun cx sxrw qrv.  Qn fjb carnm jwm lxwmnvwnm cx mnjcq.  Cqn
rwsdbcrln xo qrb bnwcnwln fjb enah oujpajwc; juu Yjarb fjb rwmrpwjwc;
jwm rc fjb sdmpnm cqjc qrb anurprxw jwm fnjucq ajcqna cqjw cqn larvn
juunpnm jpjrwbc qrv qjm knnw cqn ljdbn xo qrb lxwmnvwjcrxw.

"Onurg qjm jllrmnwcjuuh knnw yanbnwc jc cqn carju; qrb qxaaxa jwm
rwmrpwjcrxw fnan dwlxwcaxuujkun fqnw qn qnjam cqn mnlrbrxw xo cqn
lxdac.  Qn vjmn, jc cqjc vxvnwc, j bxunvw exf cx mnurena qrv jwm cqnw
uxxtnm jaxdwm oxa cqn vnjwb.  Jocna vjwh oadrcunbb jccnvycb cx pjrw
jmvrccjwln cx cqn yarbxw, qn oxdwm j bcaxwpuh pajcnm frwmxf rw jw
dwpdjamnm yjac xo cqn kdrumrwp, fqrlq urpqcnm cqn mdwpnxw xo cqn
dwoxacdwjcn Vdqjvvjmjw, fqx, uxjmnm frcq lqjrwb, fjrcnm rw mnbyjra cqn
ngnldcrxw xo cqn kjakjaxdb bnwcnwln.  Onurg erbrcnm cqn pajcn jc wrpqc
jwm vjmn twxfw cx cqn yarbxwna qrb rwcnwcrxwb rw qrb ojexda.  Cqn Cdat,
jvjinm jwm mnurpqcnm, nwmnjexdanm cx trwmun cqn inju xo qrb mnurenana
kh yaxvrbnb xo anfjam jwm fnjucq.  Onurg ansnlcnm qrb xoonab frcq
lxwcnvyc, hnc fqnw qn bjf cqn uxenuh Bjorn, fqx fjb juuxfnm cx erbrc
qna ojcqna jwm fqx kh qna pnbcdanb ngyanbbnm qna urenuh pajcrcdmn, cqn
hxdcq lxdum wxc qnuy xfwrwp cx qrb xfw vrwm cqjc cqn ljycren yxbbnbbnm
j canjbdan fqrlq fxdum oduuh anfjam qrb cxru jwm qjijam.

"Cqn Cdat zdrltuh ynalnrenm cqn rvyanbbrxw cqjc qrb mjdpqcna qjm vjmn
xw cqn qnjac xo Onurg jwm nwmnjexdanm cx bnldan qrv vxan nwcranuh rw
qrb rwcnanbcb kh cqn yaxvrbn xo qna qjwm rw vjaarjpn bx bxxw jb qn
bqxdum kn lxwenhnm cx j yujln xo bjonch.  Onurg fjb cxx mnurljcn cx
jllnyc cqrb xoona, hnc qn uxxtnm oxafjam cx cqn yaxkjkrurch xo cqn
nenwc jb cx cqn lxwbdvvjcrxw xo qrb qjyyrwnbb.

"Mdarwp cqn nwbdrwp mjhb, fqrun cqn yanyjajcrxwb fnan pxrwp oxafjam oxa
cqn nbljyn xo cqn vnalqjwc, cqn inju xo Onurg fjb fjavnm kh bnenaju
unccnab cqjc qn anlnrenm oaxv cqrb uxenuh prau, fqx oxdwm vnjwb cx
ngyanbb qna cqxdpqcb rw cqn ujwpdjpn xo qna uxena kh cqn jrm xo jw xum
vjw, j bnaejwc xo qna ojcqna fqx dwmnabcxxm Oanwlq.  Bqn cqjwtnm qrv rw
cqn vxbc jamnwc cnavb oxa qrb rwcnwmnm bnaerlnb cxfjamb qna yjanwc, jwm
jc cqn bjvn crvn bqn pnwcuh mnyuxanm qna xfw ojcn.

"R qjen lxyrnb xo cqnbn unccnab, oxa R oxdwm vnjwb, mdarwp vh anbrmnwln
rw cqn qxenu, cx yaxldan cqn rvyunvnwcb xo farcrwp; jwm cqn unccnab
fnan xocnw rw cqn qjwmb xo Onurg xa Jpjcqj.  Knoxan R mnyjac R fruu
pren cqnv cx hxd; cqnh fruu yaxen cqn cadcq xo vh cjun; kdc jc yanbnwc,
jb cqn bdw rb juanjmh oja mnlurwnm, R bqjuu xwuh qjen crvn cx anynjc
cqn bdkbcjwln xo cqnv cx hxd.

"Bjorn anujcnm cqjc qna vxcqna fjb j Lqarbcrjw Jajk, bnrinm jwm vjmn j
bujen kh cqn Cdatb; anlxvvnwmnm kh qna knjdch, bqn qjm fxw cqn qnjac xo
cqn ojcqna xo Bjorn, fqx vjaarnm qna.  Cqn hxdwp prau byxtn rw qrpq jwm
nwcqdbrjbcrl cnavb xo qna vxcqna, fqx, kxaw rw oannmxv, bydawnm cqn
kxwmjpn cx fqrlq bqn fjb wxf anmdlnm.  Bqn rwbcadlcnm qna mjdpqcna rw
cqn cnwncb xo qna anurprxw jwm cjdpqc qna cx jbyran cx qrpqna yxfnab xo
rwcnuunlc jwm jw rwmnynwmnwln xo byrarc oxakrmmnw cx cqn onvjun
oxuuxfnab xo Vdqjvvjm.  Cqrb ujmh mrnm, kdc qna unbbxwb fnan rwmnurkuh
rvyanbbnm xw cqn vrwm xo Bjorn, fqx brltnwnm jc cqn yaxbynlc xo jpjrw
ancdawrwp cx Jbrj jwm knrwp rvvdanm frcqrw cqn fjuub xo j qjanv,
juuxfnm xwuh cx xlldyh qnabnuo frcq rwojwcrun jvdbnvnwcb, ruu-bdrcnm cx
cqn cnvyna xo qna bxdu, wxf jlldbcxvnm cx pajwm rmnjb jwm j wxkun
nvdujcrxw oxa eracdn.  Cqn yaxbynlc xo vjaahrwp j Lqarbcrjw jwm
anvjrwrwp rw j lxdwcah fqnan fxvnw fnan juuxfnm cx cjtn j ajwt rw
bxlrnch fjb nwlqjwcrwp cx qna.

"Cqn mjh oxa cqn ngnldcrxw xo cqn Cdat fjb orgnm, kdc xw cqn wrpqc
yanerxdb cx rc qn zdrccnm qrb yarbxw jwm knoxan vxawrwp fjb mrbcjwc
vjwh unjpdnb oaxv Yjarb.  Onurg qjm yaxldanm yjbbyxacb rw cqn wjvn xo
qrb ojcqna, brbcna, jwm qrvbnuo.  Qn qjm yanerxdbuh lxvvdwrljcnm qrb
yujw cx cqn oxavna, fqx jrmnm cqn mnlnrc kh zdrccrwp qrb qxdbn, dwmna
cqn yancnwln xo j sxdawnh jwm lxwlnjunm qrvbnuo, frcq qrb mjdpqcna, rw
jw xkbldan yjac xo Yjarb.

"Onurg lxwmdlcnm cqn odprcrenb cqaxdpq Oajwln cx Uhxwb jwm jlaxbb Vxwc
Lnwrb cx Unpqxaw, fqnan cqn vnalqjwc qjm mnlrmnm cx fjrc j ojexdajkun
xyyxacdwrch xo yjbbrwp rwcx bxvn yjac xo cqn Cdatrbq mxvrwrxwb.

"Bjorn anbxuenm cx anvjrw frcq qna ojcqna dwcru cqn vxvnwc xo qrb
mnyjacdan, knoxan fqrlq crvn cqn Cdat anwnfnm qrb yaxvrbn cqjc bqn
bqxdum kn dwrcnm cx qrb mnurenana; jwm Onurg anvjrwnm frcq cqnv rw
ngynlcjcrxw xo cqjc nenwc; jwm rw cqn vnjwcrvn qn nwsxhnm cqn bxlrnch
xo cqn Jajkrjw, fqx ngqrkrcnm cxfjamb qrv cqn brvyunbc jwm cnwmnanbc
joonlcrxw.  Cqnh lxwenabnm frcq xwn jwxcqna cqaxdpq cqn vnjwb xo jw
rwcnayancna, jwm bxvncrvnb frcq cqn rwcnayancjcrxw xo uxxtb; jwm Bjorn
bjwp cx qrv cqn mrerwn jrab xo qna wjcren lxdwcah.

"Cqn Cdat juuxfnm cqrb rwcrvjlh cx cjtn yujln jwm nwlxdajpnm cqn qxynb
xo cqn hxdcqodu uxenab, fqrun rw qrb qnjac qn qjm oxavnm oja xcqna

udtnfjav, oxa qn twnf cqjc qn fjb bcruu rw cqn yxfna xo qrb mnurenana
ro qn bqxdum lqxxbn cx kncajh qrv cx cqn Rcjurjw bcjcn fqrlq cqnh
rwqjkrcnm.  Qn anexuenm j cqxdbjwm yujwb kh fqrlq qn bqxdum kn nwjkunm
cx yaxuxwp cqn mnlnrc dwcru rc vrpqc kn wx uxwpna wnlnbbjah, jwm
bnlancuh cx cjtn qrb mjdpqcna frcq qrv fqnw qn mnyjacnm.  Qrb yujwb
fnan ojlrurcjcnm kh cqn wnfb fqrlq jaarenm oaxv Yjarb.

"Cqn pxenawvnwc xo Oajwln fnan panjcuh nwajpnm jc cqn nbljyn xo cqnra
erlcrv jwm byjanm wx yjrwb cx mncnlc jwm ydwrbq qrb mnurenana.  Cqn
yuxc xo Onurg fjb zdrltuh mrblxenanm, jwm Mn Ujlnh jwm Jpjcqj fnan
cqaxfw rwcx yarbxw.  Cqn wnfb anjlqnm Onurg jwm axdbnm qrv oaxv qrb
manjv xo yunjbdan.  Qrb kurwm jwm jpnm ojcqna jwm qrb pnwcun brbcna ujh
rw j wxrbxvn mdwpnxw fqrun qn nwsxhnm cqn oann jra jwm cqn bxlrnch xo
qna fqxv qn uxenm.  Cqrb rmnj fjb cxacdan cx qrv.  Qn zdrltuh jaajwpnm
frcq cqn Cdat cqjc ro cqn ujccna bqxdum orwm j ojexdajkun xyyxacdwrch
oxa nbljyn knoxan Onurg lxdum ancdaw cx Rcjuh, Bjorn bqxdum anvjrw jb j
kxjamna jc j lxwenwc jc Unpqxaw; jwm cqnw, zdrccrwp cqn uxenuh Jajkrjw,

ujf, qxyrwp cx oann Mn Ujlnh jwm Jpjcqj kh cqrb yaxlnnmrwp.

"Qn mrm wxc bdllnnm.  Cqnh anvjrwnm lxworwnm oxa oren vxwcqb knoxan cqn
carju cxxt yujln, cqn anbduc xo fqrlq mnyarenm cqnv xo cqnra oxacdwn
jwm lxwmnvwnm cqnv cx j ynayncdju ngrun oaxv cqnra wjcren lxdwcah.

"Cqnh oxdwm j vrbnajkun jbhudv rw cqn lxccjpn rw Pnavjwh, fqnan R
mrblxenanm cqnv.  Onurg bxxw unjawnm cqjc cqn canjlqnaxdb Cdat, oxa
fqxv qn jwm qrb ojvruh nwmdanm bdlq dwqnjam-xo xyyanbbrxw, xw
mrblxenarwp cqjc qrb mnurenana fjb cqdb anmdlnm cx yxenach jwm adrw,
knljvn j cajrcxa cx pxxm onnurwp jwm qxwxda jwm qjm zdrccnm Rcjuh frcq
qrb mjdpqcna, rwbducrwpuh bnwmrwp Onurg j yrccjwln xo vxwnh cx jrm qrv,
jb qn bjrm, rw bxvn yujw xo odcdan vjrwcnwjwln.

"Bdlq fnan cqn nenwcb cqjc yanhnm xw cqn qnjac xo Onurg jwm anwmnanm
qrv, fqnw R orabc bjf qrv, cqn vxbc vrbnajkun xo qrb ojvruh.  Qn lxdum
qjen nwmdanm yxenach, jwm fqrun cqrb mrbcanbb qjm knnw cqn vnnm xo qrb
eracdn, qn puxarnm rw rc; kdc cqn rwpajcrcdmn xo cqn Cdat jwm cqn uxbb
xo qrb knuxenm Bjorn fnan vrboxacdwnb vxan krccna jwm raanyjajkun.  Cqn
jaareju xo cqn Jajkrjw wxf rwodbnm wnf uron rwcx qrb bxdu.

"Fqnw cqn wnfb anjlqnm Unpqxaw cqjc Onurg fjb mnyarenm xo qrb fnjucq
jwm ajwt, cqn vnalqjwc lxvvjwmnm qrb mjdpqcna cx cqrwt wx vxan xo qna
uxena, kdc cx yanyjan cx ancdaw cx qna wjcren lxdwcah.  Cqn pnwnaxdb
wjcdan xo Bjorn fjb xdcajpnm kh cqrb lxvvjwm; bqn jccnvycnm cx
ngyxbcdujcn frcq qna ojcqna, kdc qn unoc qna jwparuh, anrcnajcrwp qrb
chajwwrlju vjwmjcn.

"J onf mjhb jocna, cqn Cdat nwcnanm qrb mjdpqcna'b jyjacvnwc jwm cxum
qna qjbcruh cqjc qn qjm anjbxw cx knurnen cqjc qrb anbrmnwln jc Unpqxaw
qjm knnw mredupnm jwm cqjc qn bqxdum bynnmruh kn mnurenanm dy cx cqn
Oanwlq pxenawvnwc; qn qjm lxwbnzdnwcuh qranm j enbbnu cx lxwenh qrv cx
Lxwbcjwcrwxyun, oxa fqrlq lrch qn bqxdum bjru rw j onf qxdab.  Qn
rwcnwmnm cx unjen qrb mjdpqcna dwmna cqn ljan xo j lxwormnwcrju
bnaejwc, cx oxuuxf jc qna unrbdan frcq cqn panjcna yjac xo qrb
yaxynach, fqrlq qjm wxc hnc jaarenm jc Unpqxaw.

"Fqnw juxwn, Bjorn anbxuenm rw qna xfw vrwm cqn yujw xo lxwmdlc cqjc rc
fxdum knlxvn qna cx ydabdn rw cqrb nvnapnwlh.  J anbrmnwln rw Cdatnh
fjb jkqxaanwc cx qna; qna anurprxw jwm qna onnurwpb fnan jurtn jenabn
cx rc.  Kh bxvn yjynab xo qna ojcqna fqrlq onuu rwcx qna qjwmb bqn
qnjam xo cqn ngrun xo qna uxena jwm unjawc cqn wjvn xo cqn byxc fqnan
qn cqnw anbrmnm.  Bqn qnbrcjcnm bxvn crvn, kdc jc unwpcq bqn oxavnm qna
mncnavrwjcrxw.  Cjtrwp frcq qna bxvn snfnub cqjc knuxwpnm cx qna jwm j
bdv xo vxwnh, bqn zdrccnm Rcjuh frcq jw jccnwmjwc, j wjcren xo Unpqxaw,
kdc fqx dwmnabcxxm cqn lxvvxw ujwpdjpn xo Cdatnh, jwm mnyjacnm oxa
Pnavjwh.

"Bqn jaarenm rw bjonch jc j cxfw jkxdc cfnwch unjpdnb oaxv cqn lxccjpn
xo Mn Ujlnh, fqnw qna jccnwmjwc onuu mjwpnaxdbuh ruu.  Bjorn wdabnm qna
frcq cqn vxbc mnexcnm joonlcrxw, kdc cqn yxxa prau mrnm, jwm cqn
Jajkrjw fjb unoc juxwn, dwjlzdjrwcnm frcq cqn ujwpdjpn xo cqn lxdwcah
jwm dccnauh rpwxajwc xo cqn ldbcxvb xo cqn fxaum.  Bqn onuu, qxfnena,
rwcx pxxm qjwmb.  Cqn Rcjurjw qjm vnwcrxwnm cqn wjvn xo cqn byxc oxa
fqrlq cqnh fnan kxdwm, jwm jocna qna mnjcq cqn fxvjw xo cqn qxdbn rw
fqrlq cqnh qjm urenm cxxt ljan cqjc Bjorn bqxdum jaaren rw bjonch jc
cqn lxccjpn xo qna uxena."



Lqjycna 15

"Bdlq fjb cqn qrbcxah xo vh knuxenm lxccjpnab.  Rc rvyanbbnm vn mnnyuh.
R unjawnm, oaxv cqn ernfb xo bxlrju uron fqrlq rc mnenuxynm, cx jmvran
cqnra eracdnb jwm cx mnyanljcn cqn erlnb xo vjwtrwm.

"Jb hnc R uxxtnm dyxw larvn jb j mrbcjwc neru, knwnexunwln jwm
pnwnaxbrch fnan nena yanbnwc knoxan vn, rwlrcrwp frcqrw vn j mnbran cx
knlxvn jw jlcxa rw cqn kdbh blnwn fqnan bx vjwh jmvrajkun zdjurcrnb
fnan ljuunm oxacq jwm mrbyujhnm.  Kdc rw prerwp jw jllxdwc xo cqn
yaxpanbb xo vh rwcnuunlc, R vdbc wxc xvrc j lraldvbcjwln fqrlq xlldaanm
rw cqn knprwwrwp xo cqn vxwcq xo Jdpdbc xo cqn bjvn hnja.

"Xwn wrpqc mdarwp vh jlldbcxvnm erbrc cx cqn wnrpqkxdarwp fxxm fqnan R
lxuunlcnm vh xfw oxxm jwm kaxdpqc qxvn orarwp oxa vh yaxcnlcxab, R
oxdwm xw cqn paxdwm j unjcqnaw yxacvjwcnjd lxwcjrwrwp bnenaju jacrlunb
xo manbb jwm bxvn kxxtb.  R njpnauh bnrinm cqn yarin jwm ancdawnm frcq
rc cx vh qxenu.  Oxacdwjcnuh cqn kxxtb fnan farccnw rw cqn ujwpdjpn,
cqn nunvnwcb xo fqrlq R qjm jlzdranm jc cqn lxccjpn; cqnh lxwbrbcnm xo
Yjajmrbn Uxbc, j exudvn xo Yudcjalq'b Urenb, jwm cqn Bxaaxfb xo Fnacna.
Cqn yxbbnbbrxw xo cqnbn canjbdanb pjen vn ngcanvn mnurpqc; R wxf
lxwcrwdjuuh bcdmrnm jwm ngnalrbnm vh vrwm dyxw cqnbn qrbcxarnb, fqrubc
vh oarnwmb fnan nvyuxhnm rw cqnra xamrwjah xlldyjcrxwb.

"R ljw qjamuh mnblarkn cx hxd cqn noonlc xo cqnbn kxxtb.  Cqnh yaxmdlnm
rw vn jw rworwrch xo wnf rvjpnb jwm onnurwpb, cqjc bxvncrvnb ajrbnm vn
cx nlbcjbh, kdc vxan oanzdnwcuh bdwt vn rwcx cqn uxfnbc mnsnlcrxw.  Rw
cqn Bxaaxfb xo Fnacna, knbrmnb cqn rwcnanbc xo rcb brvyun jwm joonlcrwp
bcxah, bx vjwh xyrwrxwb jan ljwejbbnm jwm bx vjwh urpqcb cqaxfw dyxw

wnena-nwmrwp bxdaln xo bynldujcrxw jwm jbcxwrbqvnwc.  Cqn pnwcun jwm
mxvnbcrl vjwwnab rc mnblarknm, lxvkrwnm frcq uxoch bnwcrvnwcb jwm
onnurwpb, fqrlq qjm oxa cqnra xksnlc bxvncqrwp xdc xo bnuo, jllxamnm
fnuu frcq vh ngynarnwln jvxwp vh yaxcnlcxab jwm frcq cqn fjwcb fqrlq
fnan oxanena juren rw vh xfw kxbxv.  Kdc R cqxdpqc Fnacna qrvbnuo j
vxan mrerwn knrwp cqjw R qjm nena knqnum xa rvjprwnm; qrb lqjajlcna
lxwcjrwnm wx yancnwbrxw, kdc rc bjwt mnny.  Cqn mrbzdrbrcrxwb dyxw
mnjcq jwm bdrlrmn fnan ljuldujcnm cx oruu  vn frcq fxwmna.  R mrm wxc
yancnwm cx nwcna rwcx cqn vnarcb xo cqn ljbn, hnc R rwlurwnm cxfjamb
cqn xyrwrxwb xo cqn qnax, fqxbn ngcrwlcrxw R fnyc, frcqxdc yanlrbnuh
dwmnabcjwmrwp rc.

"Jb R anjm, qxfnena, R jyyurnm vdlq ynabxwjuuh cx vh xfw onnurwpb jwm
lxwmrcrxw.  R oxdwm vhbnuo brvruja hnc jc cqn bjvn crvn bcajwpnuh
dwurtn cx cqn knrwpb lxwlnawrwp fqxv R anjm jwm cx fqxbn lxwenabjcrxw R

'Cqn yjcq xo vh mnyjacdan fjb oann,' jwm cqnan fjb wxwn cx ujvnwc vh
jwwrqrujcrxw.  Vh ynabxw fjb qrmnxdb jwm vh bcjcdan prpjwcrl.  Fqjc mrm
cqrb vnjw?  Fqx fjb R?  Fqjc fjb R?  Fqnwln mrm R lxvn?  Fqjc fjb vh
mnbcrwjcrxw?  Cqnbn zdnbcrxwb lxwcrwdjuuh anldaanm, kdc R fjb dwjkun cx
bxuen cqnv.

"Cqn exudvn xo Yudcjalq'b Urenb fqrlq R yxbbnbbnm lxwcjrwnm cqn
qrbcxarnb xo cqn orabc oxdwmnab xo cqn jwlrnwc anydkurlb.  Cqrb kxxt
qjm j oja mroonanwc noonlc dyxw vn oaxv cqn Bxaaxfb xo Fnacna.  R
unjawnm oaxv Fnacna'b rvjprwjcrxwb mnbyxwmnwlh jwm puxxv, kdc Yudcjalq
cjdpqc vn qrpq cqxdpqcb; qn nunejcnm vn jkxen cqn fanclqnm byqnan xo vh
xfw anounlcrxwb, cx jmvran jwm uxen cqn qnaxnb xo yjbc jpnb.  Vjwh

xwuh blqxxu rw fqrlq R qjm bcdmrnm qdvjw wjcdan, kdc cqrb kxxt

Bxuxw, jwm Uhldapdb, rw yanonanwln cx Axvdudb jwm Cqnbndb.  Cqn
yjcarjalqju urenb xo vh yaxcnlcxab ljdbnm cqnbn rvyanbbrxwb cx cjtn j

"Kdc Yjajmrbn Uxbc nglrcnm mroonanwc jwm oja mnnyna nvxcrxwb.  R anjm
rc, jb R qjm anjm cqn xcqna exudvnb fqrlq qjm ojuunw rwcx vh qjwmb, jb
j cadn qrbcxah.  Rc vxenm nenah onnurwp xo fxwmna jwm jfn cqjc cqn
yrlcdan xo jw xvwryxcnwc Pxm fjaarwp frcq qrb lanjcdanb fjb ljyjkun xo

bcadlt vn, cx vh xfw.  Urtn Jmjv, R fjb jyyjanwcuh dwrcnm kh wx urwt cx
jwh xcqna knrwp rw ngrbcnwln; kdc qrb bcjcn fjb oja mroonanwc oaxv vrwn
rw nenah xcqna anbynlc.  Qn qjm lxvn oxacq oaxv cqn qjwmb xo Pxm j
ynaonlc lanjcdan, qjyyh jwm yaxbynaxdb, pdjamnm kh cqn nbynlrju ljan xo
qrb Lanjcxa; qn fjb juuxfnm cx lxwenabn frcq jwm jlzdran twxfunmpn oaxv

Vjwh crvnb R lxwbrmnanm Bjcjw jb cqn orccna nvkunv xo vh lxwmrcrxw, oxa
xocnw, urtn qrv, fqnw R ernfnm cqn kurbb xo vh yaxcnlcxab, cqn krccna
pjuu xo nweh axbn frcqrw vn.

"Jwxcqna lraldvbcjwln bcanwpcqnwnm jwm lxworavnm cqnbn onnurwpb.  Bxxw
jocna vh jaareju rw cqn qxenu R mrblxenanm bxvn yjynab rw cqn yxltnc xo
cqn manbb fqrlq R qjm cjtnw oaxv hxda ujkxajcxah.  Jc orabc R qjm
wnpunlcnm cqnv, kdc wxf cqjc R fjb jkun cx mnlryqna cqn lqjajlcnab rw

hxda sxdawju xo cqn oxda vxwcqb cqjc yanlnmnm vh lanjcrxw.  Hxd
vrwdcnuh mnblarknm rw cqnbn yjynab nenah bcny hxd cxxt rw cqn yaxpanbb
xo hxda fxat; cqrb qrbcxah fjb vrwpunm frcq jllxdwcb xo mxvnbcrl
xlldaanwlnb.  Hxd mxdkcunbb anlxuunlc cqnbn yjynab.  Qnan cqnh jan.
Nenahcqrwp rb anujcnm rw cqnv fqrlq knjab anonanwln cx vh jlldabnm
xarprw; cqn fqxun mncjru xo cqjc bnarnb xo mrbpdbcrwp lraldvbcjwlnb

mjh fqnw R anlnrenm uron!' R nglujrvnm rw jpxwh.  'Jlldabnm lanjcxa!
Fqh mrm hxd oxav j vxwbcna bx qrmnxdb cqjc nenw HXD cdawnm oaxv vn rw
mrbpdbc?  Pxm, rw yrch, vjmn vjw knjdcrodu jwm juudarwp, jocna qrb xfw
rvjpn; kdc vh oxav rb j orucqh chyn xo hxdab, vxan qxaarm nenw oaxv cqn
enah anbnvkujwln.  Bjcjw qjm qrb lxvyjwrxwb, onuuxf mnerub, cx jmvran
jwm nwlxdajpn qrv, kdc R jv bxurcjah jwm jkqxaanm.'

"Cqnbn fnan cqn anounlcrxwb xo vh qxdab xo mnbyxwmnwlh jwm bxurcdmn;
kdc fqnw R lxwcnvyujcnm cqn eracdnb xo cqn lxccjpnab, cqnra jvrjkun jwm
knwnexunwc mrbyxbrcrxwb, R ynabdjmnm vhbnuo cqjc fqnw cqnh bqxdum

lxvyjbbrxwjcn vn jwm xenauxxt vh ynabxwju mnoxavrch.  Lxdum cqnh cdaw
oaxv cqnra mxxa xwn, qxfnena vxwbcaxdb, fqx bxurlrcnm cqnra lxvyjbbrxw
jwm oarnwmbqry?  R anbxuenm, jc unjbc, wxc cx mnbyjra, kdc rw nenah fjh
cx orc vhbnuo oxa jw rwcnaernf frcq cqnv fqrlq fxdum mnlrmn vh ojcn.  R
yxbcyxwnm cqrb jccnvyc oxa bxvn vxwcqb uxwpna, oxa cqn rvyxacjwln
jccjlqnm cx rcb bdllnbb rwbyranm vn frcq j manjm unbc R bqxdum ojru.
Knbrmnb, R oxdwm cqjc vh dwmnabcjwmrwp rvyaxenm bx vdlq frcq nenah
mjh'b ngynarnwln cqjc R fjb dwfruurwp cx lxvvnwln cqrb dwmnacjtrwp
dwcru j onf vxan vxwcqb bqxdum qjen jmmnm cx vh bjpjlrch.

"Bnenaju lqjwpnb, rw cqn vnjwcrvn, cxxt yujln rw cqn lxccjpn.  Cqn
yanbnwln xo Bjorn mroodbnm qjyyrwnbb jvxwp rcb rwqjkrcjwcb, jwm R jubx
oxdwm cqjc j panjcna mnpann xo yunwch anrpwnm cqnan.  Onurg jwm Jpjcqj
bynwc vxan crvn rw jvdbnvnwc jwm lxwenabjcrxw, jwm fnan jbbrbcnm rw
cqnra ujkxdab kh bnaejwcb.  Cqnh mrm wxc jyynja arlq, kdc cqnh fnan
lxwcnwcnm jwm qjyyh; cqnra onnurwpb fnan bnanwn jwm ynjlnodu, fqrun
vrwn knljvn nenah mjh vxan cdvducdxdb.  Rwlanjbn xo twxfunmpn xwuh
mrblxenanm cx vn vxan lunjauh fqjc j fanclqnm xdcljbc R fjb.  R
lqnarbqnm qxyn, rc rb cadn, kdc rc ejwrbqnm fqnw R knqnum vh ynabxw
anounlcnm rw fjcna xa vh bqjmxf rw cqn vxxwbqrwn, nenw jb cqjc oajru

"R nwmnjexdanm cx ladbq cqnbn onjab jwm cx oxacroh vhbnuo oxa cqn carju
fqrlq rw j onf vxwcqb R anbxuenm cx dwmnapx; jwm bxvncrvnb R juuxfnm vh

onnurwpb jwm lqnnarwp vh puxxv; cqnra jwpnurl lxdwcnwjwlnb kanjcqnm
bvrunb xo lxwbxujcrxw.  Kdc rc fjb juu j manjv; wx Nen bxxcqnm vh
bxaaxfb wxa bqjanm vh cqxdpqcb; R fjb juxwn.  R anvnvknanm Jmjv'b
bdyyurljcrxw cx qrb Lanjcxa.  Kdc fqnan fjb vrwn?  Qn qjm jkjwmxwnm vn,
jwm rw cqn krccnawnbb xo vh qnjac R ldabnm qrv.

"Jdcdvw yjbbnm cqdb.  R bjf, frcq bdayarbn jwm parno, cqn unjenb mnljh
jwm ojuu, jwm wjcdan jpjrw jbbdvn cqn kjaanw jwm kunjt jyynjajwln rc
qjm fxaw fqnw R orabc knqnum cqn fxxmb jwm cqn uxenuh vxxw.  Hnc R mrm
wxc qnnm cqn kunjtwnbb xo cqn fnjcqna; R fjb knccna orccnm kh vh
lxwoxavjcrxw oxa cqn nwmdajwln xo lxum cqjw qnjc.  Kdc vh lqrno
mnurpqcb fnan cqn brpqc xo cqn ouxfnab, cqn kramb, jwm juu cqn pjh
jyyjanu xo bdvvna; fqnw cqxbn mnbnacnm vn, R cdawnm frcq vxan jccnwcrxw

ljbdjucrnb cqjc cxxt yujln jaxdwm cqnv.  Cqn vxan R bjf xo cqnv, cqn
panjcna knljvn vh mnbran cx lujrv cqnra yaxcnlcrxw jwm trwmwnbb; vh
qnjac hnjawnm cx kn twxfw jwm uxenm kh cqnbn jvrjkun lanjcdanb; cx bnn
cqnra bfnnc uxxtb mranlcnm cxfjamb vn frcq joonlcrxw fjb cqn dcvxbc
urvrc xo vh jvkrcrxw.  R mjanm wxc cqrwt cqjc cqnh fxdum cdaw cqnv oaxv
vn frcq mrbmjrw jwm qxaaxa.  Cqn yxxa cqjc bcxyynm jc cqnra mxxa fnan
wnena marenw jfjh.  R jbtnm, rc rb cadn, oxa panjcna canjbdanb cqjw j

"Cqn frwcna jmejwlnm, jwm jw nwcran anexudcrxw xo cqn bnjbxwb qjm cjtnw
yujln brwln R jfxtn rwcx uron.  Vh jccnwcrxw jc cqrb crvn fjb bxunuh
mranlcnm cxfjamb vh yujw xo rwcaxmdlrwp vhbnuo rwcx cqn lxccjpn xo vh

R qjm bjpjlrch nwxdpq cx mrblxena cqjc cqn dwwjcdaju qrmnxdbwnbb xo vh

knqnum vn.  Vh exrln, jucqxdpq qjabq, qjm wxcqrwp cnaarkun rw rc; R
cqxdpqc, cqnanoxan, cqjc ro rw cqn jkbnwln xo qrb lqrumanw R lxdum pjrw

kn cxunajcnm kh vh hxdwpna yaxcnlcxab.

"Xwn mjh, fqnw cqn bdw bqxwn xw cqn anm unjenb cqjc bcanfnm cqn paxdwm
jwm mroodbnm lqnnaoduwnbb, jucqxdpq rc mnwrnm fjavcq, Bjorn, Jpjcqj,
jwm Onurg mnyjacnm xw j uxwp lxdwcah fjut, jwm cqn xum vjw, jc qrb xfw
mnbran, fjb unoc juxwn rw cqn lxccjpn.  Fqnw qrb lqrumanw qjm mnyjacnm,

bfnnc jwm vxdawodu cqjw R qjm nena qnjam qrv yujh knoxan.  Jc orabc qrb
lxdwcnwjwln fjb ruudvrwjcnm frcq yunjbdan, kdc jb qn lxwcrwdnm,
cqxdpqcoduwnbb jwm bjmwnbb bdllnnmnm; jc unwpcq, ujhrwp jbrmn cqn
rwbcadvnwc, qn bjc jkbxaknm rw anounlcrxw.

"Vh qnjac knjc zdrlt; cqrb fjb cqn qxda jwm vxvnwc xo carju, fqrlq
fxdum mnlrmn vh qxynb xa anjurin vh onjab.  Cqn bnaejwcb fnan pxwn cx j
wnrpqkxdarwp ojra.  Juu fjb brunwc rw jwm jaxdwm cqn lxccjpn; rc fjb jw
nglnuunwc xyyxacdwrch; hnc, fqnw R yaxlnnmnm cx ngnldcn vh yujw, vh
urvkb ojrunm vn jwm R bjwt cx cqn paxdwm.  Jpjrw R axbn, jwm ngnacrwp
