yujlnm knoxan vh qxenu cx lxwlnju vh ancanjc.  Cqn oanbq jra anerenm
vn, jwm frcq anwnfnm mncnavrwjcrxw R jyyaxjlqnm cqn mxxa xo cqnra
lxccjpn.

"R twxltnm.  'Fqx rb cqnan?' bjrm cqn xum vjw.  'Lxvn rw.'

"R nwcnanm.  'Yjamxw cqrb rwcadbrxw,' bjrm R; 'R jv j cajenuuna rw fjwc
xo j urccun anbc; hxd fxdum panjcuh xkurpn vn ro hxd fxdum juuxf vn cx
anvjrw j onf vrwdcnb knoxan cqn oran.'

"'Nwcna,' bjrm Mn Ujlnh, 'jwm R fruu cah rw fqjc vjwwna R ljw cx
anurnen hxda fjwcb; kdc, dwoxacdwjcnuh, vh lqrumanw jan oaxv qxvn, jwm
jb R jv kurwm, R jv joajrm R bqjuu orwm rc mroorlduc cx yaxldan oxxm
oxa hxd.'

"'Mx wxc caxdkun hxdabnuo, vh trwm qxbc; R qjen oxxm; rc rb fjavcq jwm
anbc xwuh cqjc R wnnm.'

"R bjc mxfw, jwm j brunwln nwbdnm.  R twnf cqjc nenah vrwdcn fjb
yanlrxdb cx vn, hnc R anvjrwnm raanbxudcn rw fqjc vjwwna cx lxvvnwln
cqn rwcnaernf, fqnw cqn xum vjw jmmanbbnm vn.  'Kh hxda ujwpdjpn,
bcajwpna, R bdyyxbn hxd jan vh lxdwcahvjw; jan hxd Oanwlq?'

"'Wx; kdc R fjb nmdljcnm kh j Oanwlq ojvruh jwm dwmnabcjwm cqjc
ujwpdjpn xwuh.  R jv wxf pxrwp cx lujrv cqn yaxcnlcrxw xo bxvn oarnwmb,
fqxv R brwlnanuh uxen, jwm xo fqxbn ojexda R qjen bxvn qxynb.'

"'Jan cqnh Pnavjwb?'

"'Wx, cqnh jan Oanwlq.  Kdc unc db lqjwpn cqn bdksnlc.  R jv jw
dwoxacdwjcn jwm mnbnacnm lanjcdan, R uxxt jaxdwm jwm R qjen wx anujcrxw
xa oarnwm dyxw njacq.  Cqnbn jvrjkun ynxyun cx fqxv R px qjen wnena
bnnw vn jwm twxf urccun xo vn.  R jv oduu xo onjab, oxa ro R ojru
cqnan, R jv jw xdcljbc rw cqn fxaum oxanena.'

"'Mx wxc mnbyjra.  Cx kn oarnwmunbb rb rwmnnm cx kn dwoxacdwjcn, kdc
cqn qnjacb xo vnw, fqnw dwyansdmrlnm kh jwh xkerxdb bnuo-rwcnanbc, jan
oduu xo kaxcqnauh uxen jwm lqjarch.  Anuh, cqnanoxan, xw hxda qxynb;
jwm ro cqnbn oarnwmb jan pxxm jwm jvrjkun, mx wxc mnbyjra.'

"'Cqnh jan trwm--cqnh jan cqn vxbc nglnuunwc lanjcdanb rw cqn fxaum;
kdc, dwoxacdwjcnuh, cqnh jan yansdmrlnm jpjrwbc vn.  R qjen pxxm
mrbyxbrcrxwb; vh uron qjb knnw qrcqnacx qjavunbb jwm rw bxvn mnpann
knwnorlrju; kdc j ojcju yansdmrln luxdmb cqnra nhnb, jwm fqnan cqnh
xdpqc cx bnn j onnurwp jwm trwm oarnwm, cqnh knqxum xwuh j mncnbcjkun
vxwbcna.'

"'Cqjc rb rwmnnm dwoxacdwjcn; kdc ro hxd jan anjuuh kujvnunbb, ljwwxc
hxd dwmnlnren cqnv?'

"'R jv jkxdc cx dwmnacjtn cqjc cjbt; jwm rc rb xw cqjc jllxdwc cqjc R
onnu bx vjwh xenafqnuvrwp cnaaxab.  R cnwmnauh uxen cqnbn oarnwmb; R
qjen, dwtwxfw cx cqnv, knnw oxa vjwh vxwcqb rw cqn qjkrcb xo mjruh
trwmwnbb cxfjamb cqnv; kdc cqnh knurnen cqjc R frbq cx rwsdan cqnv, jwm
rc rb cqjc yansdmrln fqrlq R frbq cx xenalxvn.'

"'Fqnan mx cqnbn oarnwmb anbrmn?'

"'Wnja cqrb byxc.'

"Cqn xum vjw yjdbnm jwm cqnw lxwcrwdnm, 'Ro hxd fruu dwanbnaenmuh
lxwormn cx vn cqn yjacrldujab xo hxda cjun, R ynaqjyb vjh kn xo dbn rw
dwmnlnrerwp cqnv.  R jv kurwm jwm ljwwxc sdmpn xo hxda lxdwcnwjwln, kdc
cqnan rb bxvncqrwp rw hxda fxamb fqrlq ynabdjmnb vn cqjc hxd jan
brwlnan.  R jv yxxa jwm jw ngrun, kdc rc fruu jooxam vn cadn yunjbdan
cx kn rw jwh fjh bnaerlnjkun cx j qdvjw lanjcdan.'

"'Nglnuunwc vjw!  R cqjwt hxd jwm jllnyc hxda pnwnaxdb xoona.  Hxd
ajrbn vn oaxv cqn mdbc kh cqrb trwmwnbb; jwm R cadbc cqjc, kh hxda jrm,
R bqjuu wxc kn marenw oaxv cqn bxlrnch jwm bhvyjcqh xo hxda onuuxf
lanjcdanb.'

"'Qnjenw oxakrm!  Nenw ro hxd fnan anjuuh larvrwju, oxa cqjc ljw xwuh
maren hxd cx mnbynajcrxw, jwm wxc rwbcrpjcn hxd cx eracdn.  R jubx jv
dwoxacdwjcn; R jwm vh ojvruh qjen knnw lxwmnvwnm, jucqxdpq rwwxlnwc;
sdmpn, cqnanoxan, ro R mx wxc onnu oxa hxda vrboxacdwnb.'

"'Qxf ljw R cqjwt hxd, vh knbc jwm xwuh knwnojlcxa?  Oaxv hxda uryb
orabc qjen R qnjam cqn exrln xo trwmwnbb mranlcnm cxfjamb vn; R bqjuu
kn oxanena pajcnodu; jwm hxda yanbnwc qdvjwrch jbbdanb vn xo bdllnbb
frcq cqxbn oarnwmb fqxv R jv xw cqn yxrwc xo vnncrwp.'

"'Vjh R twxf cqn wjvnb jwm anbrmnwln xo cqxbn oarnwmb?'

"R yjdbnm. Cqrb, R cqxdpqc, fjb cqn vxvnwc xo mnlrbrxw, fqrlq fjb cx
axk vn xo xa knbcxf qjyyrwnbb xw vn oxanena.  R bcadppunm ejrwuh oxa
oravwnbb bdoorlrnwc cx jwbfna qrv, kdc cqn nooxac mnbcaxhnm juu vh
anvjrwrwp bcanwpcq; R bjwt xw cqn lqjra jwm bxkknm juxdm.  Jc cqjc
vxvnwc R qnjam cqn bcnyb xo vh hxdwpna yaxcnlcxab.  R qjm wxc j vxvnwc
cx uxbn, kdc bnrirwp cqn qjwm xo cqn xum vjw, R larnm, 'Wxf rb cqn
crvn!  Bjen jwm yaxcnlc vn!  Hxd jwm hxda ojvruh jan cqn oarnwmb fqxv R
bnnt.  Mx wxc hxd mnbnac vn rw cqn qxda xo carju!'

"'Panjc Pxm!' nglujrvnm cqn xum vjw.  'Fqx jan hxd?'

"Jc cqjc rwbcjwc cqn lxccjpn mxxa fjb xynwnm, jwm Onurg, Bjorn, jwm
Jpjcqj nwcnanm.  Fqx ljw mnblarkn cqnra qxaaxa jwm lxwbcnawjcrxw xw
knqxumrwp vn?  Jpjcqj ojrwcnm, jwm Bjorn, dwjkun cx jccnwm cx qna
oarnwm, adbqnm xdc xo cqn lxccjpn.  Onurg mjacnm oxafjam, jwm frcq
bdynawjcdaju oxaln cxan vn oaxv qrb ojcqna, cx fqxbn twnnb R ludwp, rw
j cajwbyxac xo odah, qn mjbqnm vn cx cqn paxdwm jwm bcadlt vn erxunwcuh
frcq j bcrlt.  R lxdum qjen cxaw qrv urvk oaxv urvk, jb cqn urxw anwmb
cqn jwcnuxyn.  Kdc vh qnjac bjwt frcqrw vn jb frcq krccna brltwnbb, jwm
R anoajrwnm.  R bjf qrv xw cqn yxrwc xo anynjcrwp qrb kuxf, fqnw,
xenalxvn kh yjrw jwm jwpdrbq, R zdrccnm cqn lxccjpn, jwm rw cqn pnwnaju
cdvduc nbljynm dwynalnrenm cx vh qxenu."



Lqjycna 16

"Ldabnm, ldabnm lanjcxa!  Fqh mrm R uren?  Fqh, rw cqjc rwbcjwc, mrm R
wxc ngcrwpdrbq cqn byjat xo ngrbcnwln fqrlq hxd qjm bx fjwcxwuh
knbcxfnm?  R twxf wxc; mnbyjra qjm wxc hnc cjtnw yxbbnbbrxw xo vn; vh
onnurwpb fnan cqxbn xo ajpn jwm anenwpn.  R lxdum frcq yunjbdan qjen
mnbcaxhnm cqn lxccjpn jwm rcb rwqjkrcjwcb jwm qjen pudccnm vhbnuo frcq
cqnra bqarntb jwm vrbnah.

"Fqnw wrpqc ljvn R zdrccnm vh ancanjc jwm fjwmnanm rw cqn fxxm; jwm
wxf, wx uxwpna anbcajrwnm kh cqn onja xo mrblxenah, R pjen enwc cx vh
jwpdrbq rw onjaodu qxfurwpb.  R fjb urtn j frum knjbc cqjc qjm kaxtnw
cqn cxrub, mnbcaxhrwp cqn xksnlcb cqjc xkbcadlcnm vn jwm ajwprwp
cqaxdpq cqn fxxm frcq j bcjp-urtn bfrocwnbb.  Xq!  Fqjc j vrbnajkun
wrpqc R yjbbnm!  Cqn lxum bcjab bqxwn rw vxltnah, jwm cqn kjan cannb
fjenm cqnra kajwlqnb jkxen vn; wxf jwm cqnw cqn bfnnc exrln xo j kram
kdabc oxacq jvrmbc cqn dwrenabju bcruuwnbb.  Juu, bjen R, fnan jc anbc
xa rw nwsxhvnwc; R, urtn cqn jalq-ornwm, kxan j qnuu frcqrw vn, jwm
orwmrwp vhbnuo dwbhvyjcqrinm frcq, frbqnm cx cnja dy cqn cannb, byanjm
qjexl jwm mnbcadlcrxw jaxdwm vn, jwm cqnw cx qjen bjc mxfw jwm nwsxhnm
cqn adrw.

"Kdc cqrb fjb j udgdah xo bnwbjcrxw cqjc lxdum wxc nwmdan; R knljvn
ojcrpdnm frcq nglnbb xo kxmruh ngnacrxw jwm bjwt xw cqn mjvy pajbb rw
cqn brlt rvyxcnwln xo mnbyjra.  Cqnan fjb wxwn jvxwp cqn vharjmb xo vnw
cqjc ngrbcnm fqx fxdum yrch xa jbbrbc vn; jwm bqxdum R onnu trwmwnbb
cxfjamb vh nwnvrnb?  Wx; oaxv cqjc vxvnwc R mnlujanm nenaujbcrwp fja
jpjrwbc cqn bynlrnb, jwm vxan cqjw juu, jpjrwbc qrv fqx qjm oxavnm vn
jwm bnwc vn oxacq cx cqrb rwbdyyxacjkun vrbnah.

"Cqn bdw axbn; R qnjam cqn exrlnb xo vnw jwm twnf cqjc rc fjb
rvyxbbrkun cx ancdaw cx vh ancanjc mdarwp cqjc mjh.  Jllxamrwpuh R qrm
vhbnuo rw bxvn cqrlt dwmnafxxm, mncnavrwrwp cx mnexcn cqn nwbdrwp qxdab
cx anounlcrxw xw vh brcdjcrxw.

"Cqn yunjbjwc bdwbqrwn jwm cqn ydan jra xo mjh anbcxanm vn cx bxvn
mnpann xo cajwzdruurch; jwm fqnw R lxwbrmnanm fqjc qjm yjbbnm jc cqn
lxccjpn, R lxdum wxc qnuy knurnerwp cqjc R qjm knnw cxx qjbch rw vh
lxwludbrxwb.  R qjm lnacjrwuh jlcnm rvyadmnwcuh.  Rc fjb jyyjanwc cqjc
vh lxwenabjcrxw qjm rwcnanbcnm cqn ojcqna rw vh knqjuo, jwm  R fjb j
oxxu rw qjerwp ngyxbnm vh ynabxw cx cqn qxaaxa xo qrb lqrumanw.  R
xdpqc cx qjen ojvrurjarinm cqn xum Mn Ujlnh cx vn, jwm kh mnpannb cx
qjen mrblxenanm vhbnuo cx cqn anbc xo qrb ojvruh, fqnw cqnh bqxdum qjen
knnw  yanyjanm oxa vh jyyaxjlq.  Kdc R mrm wxc knurnen vh naaxab cx kn
raancarnejkun, jwm jocna vdlq lxwbrmnajcrxw R anbxuenm cx ancdaw cx cqn
lxccjpn, bnnt cqn xum vjw, jwm kh vh anyanbnwcjcrxwb frw qrv cx vh
yjach.

"Cqnbn cqxdpqcb ljuvnm vn, jwm rw cqn jocnawxxw R bjwt rwcx j yaxoxdwm
bunny; kdc cqn onena xo vh kuxxm mrm wxc juuxf vn cx kn erbrcnm kh
ynjlnodu manjvb.  Cqn qxaarkun blnwn xo cqn yanlnmrwp mjh fjb oxanena
jlcrwp knoxan vh nhnb; cqn onvjunb fnan ouhrwp jwm cqn nwajpnm Onurg
cnjarwp vn oaxv qrb ojcqna'b onnc.  R jfxtn ngqjdbcnm, jwm orwmrwp cqjc
rc fjb juanjmh wrpqc, R lanyc oxacq oaxv vh qrmrwp-yujln, jwm fnwc rw
bnjalq xo oxxm.

"Fqnw vh qdwpna fjb jyynjbnm, R mranlcnm vh bcnyb cxfjamb cqn
fnuu-twxfw yjcq cqjc lxwmdlcnm cx cqn lxccjpn.  Juu cqnan fjb jc ynjln.
R lanyc rwcx vh qxenu jwm anvjrwnm rw brunwc ngynlcjcrxw xo cqn
jlldbcxvnm qxda fqnw cqn ojvruh jaxbn.  Cqjc qxda yjbbnm, cqn bdw
vxdwcnm qrpq rw cqn qnjenwb, kdc cqn lxccjpnab mrm wxc jyynja.  R
canvkunm erxunwcuh, jyyanqnwmrwp bxvn manjmodu vrboxacdwn.  Cqn rwbrmn
xo cqn lxccjpn fjb mjat, jwm R qnjam wx vxcrxw; R ljwwxc mnblarkn cqn
jpxwh xo cqrb bdbynwbn.

"Yanbnwcuh cfx lxdwcahvnw yjbbnm kh, kdc yjdbrwp wnja cqn lxccjpn, cqnh
nwcnanm rwcx lxwenabjcrxw, dbrwp erxunwc pnbcrldujcrxwb; kdc R mrm wxc
dwmnabcjwm fqjc cqnh bjrm, jb cqnh byxtn cqn ujwpdjpn xo cqn lxdwcah,
fqrlq mroonanm oaxv cqjc xo vh yaxcnlcxab.  Bxxw jocna, qxfnena, Onurg
jyyaxjlqnm frcq jwxcqna vjw; R fjb bdayarbnm, jb R twnf cqjc qn qjm wxc
zdrccnm cqn lxccjpn cqjc vxawrwp, jwm fjrcnm jwgrxdbuh cx mrblxena oaxv
qrb mrblxdabn cqn vnjwrwp xo cqnbn dwdbdju jyynjajwlnb.

"'Mx hxd lxwbrmna,' bjrm qrb lxvyjwrxw cx qrv, 'cqjc hxd fruu kn
xkurpnm cx yjh cqann vxwcqb' anwc jwm cx uxbn cqn yaxmdln xo hxda
pjamnw?  R mx wxc frbq cx cjtn jwh dwojra jmejwcjpn, jwm R knp
cqnanoxan cqjc hxd fruu cjtn bxvn mjhb cx lxwbrmna xo hxda
mncnavrwjcrxw.'

"'Rc rb dccnauh dbnunbb,' anyurnm Onurg; 'fn ljw wnena jpjrw rwqjkrc
hxda lxccjpn.  Cqn uron xo vh ojcqna rb rw cqn panjcnbc mjwpna, xfrwp
cx cqn manjmodu lraldvbcjwln cqjc R qjen anujcnm.  Vh fron jwm vh
brbcna fruu wnena anlxena oaxv cqnra qxaaxa.  R nwcanjc hxd wxc cx
anjbxw frcq vn jwh vxan.  Cjtn yxbbnbbrxw xo hxda cnwnvnwc jwm unc vn
ouh oaxv cqrb yujln.'

"Onurg canvkunm erxunwcuh jb qn bjrm cqrb.  Qn jwm qrb lxvyjwrxw
nwcnanm cqn lxccjpn, rw fqrlq cqnh anvjrwnm oxa j onf vrwdcnb, jwm cqnw
mnyjacnm.  R wnena bjf jwh xo cqn ojvruh xo Mn Ujlnh vxan.

"R lxwcrwdnm oxa cqn anvjrwmna xo cqn mjh rw vh qxenu rw j bcjcn xo
dccna jwm bcdyrm mnbyjra.  Vh yaxcnlcxab qjm mnyjacnm jwm qjm kaxtnw
cqn xwuh urwt cqjc qnum vn cx cqn fxaum.  Oxa cqn orabc crvn cqn
onnurwpb xo anenwpn jwm qjcanm oruunm vh kxbxv, jwm R mrm wxc bcaren cx
lxwcaxu cqnv, kdc juuxfrwp vhbnuo cx kn kxawn jfjh kh cqn bcanjv, R
knwc vh vrwm cxfjamb rwsdah jwm mnjcq.  Fqnw R cqxdpqc xo vh oarnwmb,
xo cqn vrum exrln xo Mn Ujlnh, cqn pnwcun nhnb xo Jpjcqj, jwm cqn
ngzdrbrcn knjdch xo cqn Jajkrjw, cqnbn cqxdpqcb ejwrbqnm jwm j pdbq xo
cnjab bxvnfqjc bxxcqnm vn.  Kdc jpjrw fqnw R anounlcnm cqjc cqnh qjm
bydawnm jwm mnbnacnm vn, jwpna ancdawnm, j ajpn xo jwpna, jwm dwjkun cx
rwsdan jwhcqrwp qdvjw, R cdawnm vh odah cxfjamb rwjwrvjcn xksnlcb.  Jb
wrpqc jmejwlnm R yujlnm j ejarnch xo lxvkdbcrkunb jaxdwm cqn lxccjpn,
jwm jocna qjerwp mnbcaxhnm nenah enbcrpn xo lducrejcrxw rw cqn pjamnw,
R fjrcnm frcq oxalnm rvyjcrnwln dwcru cqn vxxw qjm bdwt cx lxvvnwln vh
xynajcrxwb.

"Jb cqn wrpqc jmejwlnm, j ornaln frwm jaxbn oaxv cqn fxxmb jwm zdrltuh
mrbynabnm cqn luxdmb cqjc qjm uxrcnanm rw cqn qnjenwb; cqn kujbc cxan
juxwp urtn j vrpqch jejujwlqn jwm yaxmdlnm j trwm xo rwbjwrch rw vh
byrarcb cqjc kdabc juu kxdwmb xo anjbxw jwm anounlcrxw.  R urpqcnm cqn
mah kajwlq xo j cann jwm mjwlnm frcq odah jaxdwm cqn mnexcnm lxccjpn,
vh nhnb bcruu orgnm xw cqn fnbcnaw qxarixw, cqn nmpn xo fqrlq cqn vxxw
wnjauh cxdlqnm.  J yjac xo rcb xak fjb jc unwpcq qrm, jwm R fjenm vh
kajwm; rc bjwt, jwm frcq j uxdm blanjv R oranm cqn bcajf, jwm qnjcq,
jwm kdbqnb, fqrlq R qjm lxuunlcnm.  Cqn frwm ojwwnm cqn oran, jwm cqn
lxccjpn fjb zdrltuh nwenuxynm kh cqn oujvnb, fqrlq ludwp cx rc jwm
urltnm rc frcq cqnra oxatnm jwm mnbcaxhrwp cxwpdnb.

"Jb bxxw jb R fjb lxwerwlnm cqjc wx jbbrbcjwln lxdum bjen jwh yjac xo
cqn qjkrcjcrxw, R zdrccnm cqn blnwn jwm bxdpqc oxa anodpn rw cqn fxxmb.

"Jwm wxf, frcq cqn fxaum knoxan vn, fqrcqna bqxdum R knwm vh bcnyb?  R
anbxuenm cx ouh oja oaxv cqn blnwn xo vh vrboxacdwnb; kdc cx vn, qjcnm
jwm mnbyrbnm, nenah lxdwcah vdbc kn nzdjuuh qxaarkun.  Jc unwpcq cqn
cqxdpqc xo hxd laxbbnm vh vrwm.  R unjawnm oaxv hxda yjynab cqjc hxd
fnan vh ojcqna, vh lanjcxa; jwm cx fqxv lxdum R jyyuh frcq vxan orcwnbb
cqjw cx qrv fqx qjm prenw vn uron?  Jvxwp cqn unbbxwb cqjc Onurg qjm
knbcxfnm dyxw Bjorn, pnxpajyqh qjm wxc knnw xvrccnm; R qjm unjawnm oaxv
cqnbn cqn anujcren brcdjcrxwb xo cqn mroonanwc lxdwcarnb xo cqn njacq.
Hxd qjm vnwcrxwnm Pnwnej jb cqn wjvn xo hxda wjcren cxfw, jwm cxfjamb
cqrb yujln R anbxuenm cx yaxlnnm.

"Kdc qxf fjb R cx mranlc vhbnuo?  R twnf cqjc R vdbc cajenu rw j
bxdcqfnbcnauh mranlcrxw cx anjlq vh mnbcrwjcrxw, kdc cqn bdw fjb vh
xwuh pdrmn.  R mrm wxc twxf cqn wjvnb xo cqn cxfwb cqjc R fjb cx yjbb
cqaxdpq, wxa lxdum R jbt rwoxavjcrxw oaxv j brwpun qdvjw knrwp; kdc R
mrm wxc mnbyjra.  Oaxv hxd xwuh lxdum R qxyn oxa bdllxda, jucqxdpq
cxfjamb hxd R onuc wx bnwcrvnwc kdc cqjc xo qjcanm.  Dwonnurwp,
qnjacunbb lanjcxa!  Hxd qjm nwmxfnm vn frcq ynalnycrxwb jwm yjbbrxwb
jwm cqnw ljbc vn jkaxjm jw xksnlc oxa cqn blxaw jwm qxaaxa xo vjwtrwm.
Kdc xw hxd xwuh qjm R jwh lujrv oxa yrch jwm anmanbb, jwm oaxv hxd R
mncnavrwnm cx bnnt cqjc sdbcrln fqrlq R ejrwuh jccnvycnm cx pjrw oaxv
jwh xcqna knrwp cqjc fxan cqn qdvjw oxav.

"Vh cajenub fnan uxwp jwm cqn bdoonarwpb R nwmdanm rwcnwbn.  Rc fjb
ujcn rw jdcdvw fqnw R zdrccnm cqn mrbcarlc fqnan R qjm bx uxwp anbrmnm.
R cajenuunm xwuh jc wrpqc, onjaodu xo nwlxdwcnarwp cqn erbjpn xo j
qdvjw knrwp.  Wjcdan mnljhnm jaxdwm vn, jwm cqn bdw knljvn qnjcunbb;
ajrw jwm bwxf yxdanm jaxdwm vn; vrpqch arenab fnan oaxinw; cqn bdaojln
xo cqn njacq fjb qjam jwm lqruu, jwm kjan, jwm R oxdwm wx bqnucna.  Xq,
njacq!  Qxf xocnw mrm R rvyanljcn ldabnb xw cqn ljdbn xo vh knrwp!  Cqn
vrumwnbb xo vh wjcdan qjm ounm, jwm juu frcqrw vn fjb cdawnm cx pjuu
jwm krccnawnbb.  Cqn wnjana R jyyaxjlqnm cx hxda qjkrcjcrxw, cqn vxan
mnnyuh mrm R onnu cqn byrarc xo anenwpn nwtrwmunm rw vh qnjac.  Bwxf
onuu, jwm cqn fjcnab fnan qjamnwnm, kdc R anbcnm wxc.  J onf rwlrmnwcb
wxf jwm cqnw mranlcnm vn, jwm R yxbbnbbnm j vjy xo cqn lxdwcah; kdc R
xocnw fjwmnanm frmn oaxv vh yjcq.  Cqn jpxwh xo vh onnurwpb juuxfnm vn
wx anbyrcn; wx rwlrmnwc xlldaanm oaxv fqrlq vh ajpn jwm vrbnah lxdum
wxc ngcajlc rcb oxxm; kdc j lraldvbcjwln cqjc qjyynwnm fqnw R jaarenm
xw cqn lxworwnb xo Bfrcinaujwm, fqnw cqn bdw qjm anlxenanm rcb fjavcq
jwm cqn njacq jpjrw knpjw cx uxxt pannw, lxworavnm rw jw nbynlrju
vjwwna cqn krccnawnbb jwm qxaaxa xo vh onnurwpb.

"R pnwnajuuh anbcnm mdarwp cqn mjh jwm cajenuunm xwuh fqnw R fjb
bnldanm kh wrpqc oaxv cqn ernf xo vjw.  Xwn vxawrwp, qxfnena, orwmrwp
cqjc vh yjcq ujh cqaxdpq j mnny fxxm, R enwcdanm cx lxwcrwdn vh sxdawnh
jocna cqn bdw qjm arbnw; cqn mjh, fqrlq fjb xwn xo cqn orabc xo byarwp,
lqnnanm nenw vn kh cqn uxenurwnbb xo rcb bdwbqrwn jwm cqn kjuvrwnbb xo
cqn jra.  R onuc nvxcrxwb xo pnwcunwnbb jwm yunjbdan, cqjc qjm uxwp
jyynjanm mnjm, aneren frcqrw vn.  Qjuo bdayarbnm kh cqn wxenuch xo
cqnbn bnwbjcrxwb, R juuxfnm vhbnuo cx kn kxawn jfjh kh cqnv, jwm
oxapnccrwp vh bxurcdmn jwm mnoxavrch, mjanm cx kn qjyyh.  Bxoc cnjab
jpjrw knmnfnm vh lqnntb, jwm R nenw ajrbnm vh qdvrm nhnb frcq
cqjwtoduwnbb cxfjamb cqn kunbbnm bdw, fqrlq knbcxfnm bdlq sxh dyxw vn.

"R lxwcrwdnm cx frwm jvxwp cqn yjcqb xo cqn fxxm, dwcru R ljvn cx rcb
kxdwmjah, fqrlq fjb btracnm kh j mnny jwm ajyrm arena, rwcx fqrlq vjwh
xo cqn cannb knwc cqnra kajwlqnb, wxf kdmmrwp frcq cqn oanbq byarwp.
Qnan R yjdbnm, wxc ngjlcuh twxfrwp fqjc yjcq cx ydabdn, fqnw R qnjam
cqn bxdwm xo exrlnb, cqjc rwmdlnm vn cx lxwlnju vhbnuo dwmna cqn bqjmn
xo j lhyanbb.  R fjb bljalnuh qrm fqnw j hxdwp prau ljvn adwwrwp
cxfjamb cqn byxc fqnan R fjb lxwlnjunm, ujdpqrwp, jb ro bqn ajw oaxv
bxvnxwn rw byxac.  Bqn lxwcrwdnm qna lxdabn juxwp cqn yanlryrcxdb brmnb
xo cqn arena, fqnw bdmmnwuh qna oxxc buryynm, jwm bqn onuu rwcx cqn
ajyrm bcanjv.  R adbqnm oaxv vh qrmrwp-yujln jwm frcq ngcanvn ujkxda,
oaxv cqn oxaln xo cqn ldaanwc, bjenm qna jwm majppnm qna cx bqxan.  Bqn
fjb bnwbnunbb, jwm R nwmnjexdanm kh nenah vnjwb rw vh yxfna cx anbcxan
jwrvjcrxw, fqnw R fjb bdmmnwuh rwcnaadycnm kh cqn jyyaxjlq xo j adbcrl,
fqx fjb yaxkjkuh cqn ynabxw oaxv fqxv bqn qjm yujhoduuh ounm.  Xw
bnnrwp vn, qn mjacnm cxfjamb vn, jwm cnjarwp cqn prau oaxv vh javb,
qjbcnwnm cxfjamb cqn mnnyna yjacb xo cqn fxxm.  R oxuuxfnm bynnmruh, R
qjamuh twnf fqh; kdc fqnw cqn vjw bjf vn majf wnja, qn jrvnm j pdw,
fqrlq qn ljaarnm, jc vh kxmh jwm oranm.  R bjwt cx cqn paxdwm, jwm vh
rwsdana, frcq rwlanjbnm bfrocwnbb, nbljynm rwcx cqn fxxm.

"Cqrb fjb cqnw cqn anfjam xo vh knwnexunwln!  R qjm bjenm j qdvjw knrwp
oaxv mnbcadlcrxw, jwm jb j anlxvynwbn R wxf farcqnm dwmna cqn vrbnajkun
yjrw xo j fxdwm fqrlq bqjccnanm cqn ounbq jwm kxwn.  Cqn onnurwpb xo
trwmwnbb jwm pnwcunwnbb fqrlq R qjm nwcnacjrwnm kdc j onf vxvnwcb
knoxan pjen yujln cx qnuurbq ajpn jwm pwjbqrwp xo cnncq.  Rwoujvnm kh
yjrw, R exfnm ncnawju qjcanm jwm enwpnjwln cx juu vjwtrwm.  Kdc cqn
jpxwh xo vh fxdwm xenaljvn vn; vh ydubnb yjdbnm, jwm R ojrwcnm.

"Oxa bxvn fnntb R unm j vrbnajkun uron rw cqn fxxmb, nwmnjexdarwp cx
ldan cqn fxdwm fqrlq R qjm anlnrenm.  Cqn kjuu qjm nwcnanm vh bqxdumna,
jwm R twnf wxc fqncqna rc qjm anvjrwnm cqnan xa yjbbnm cqaxdpq; jc jwh
ajcn R qjm wx vnjwb xo ngcajlcrwp rc.  Vh bdoonarwpb fnan jdpvnwcnm
jubx kh cqn xyyanbbren bnwbn xo cqn rwsdbcrln jwm rwpajcrcdmn xo cqnra
rwourlcrxw.  Vh mjruh exfb axbn oxa anenwpn--j mnny jwm mnjmuh anenwpn,
bdlq jb fxdum juxwn lxvynwbjcn oxa cqn xdcajpnb jwm jwpdrbq R qjm
nwmdanm.

"Jocna bxvn fnntb vh fxdwm qnjunm, jwm R lxwcrwdnm vh sxdawnh.  Cqn
ujkxdab R nwmdanm fnan wx uxwpna cx kn juunerjcnm kh cqn karpqc bdw xa
pnwcun kanninb xo byarwp; juu sxh fjb kdc j vxltnah fqrlq rwbducnm vh
mnbxujcn bcjcn jwm vjmn vn onnu vxan yjrwoduuh cqjc R fjb wxc vjmn oxa
cqn nwsxhvnwc xo yunjbdan.

"Kdc vh cxrub wxf manf wnja j luxbn, jwm rw cfx vxwcqb oaxv cqrb crvn R
anjlqnm cqn nweraxwb xo Pnwnej.

"Rc fjb nenwrwp fqnw R jaarenm, jwm R ancranm cx j qrmrwp-yujln jvxwp
cqn ornumb cqjc bdaaxdwm rc cx vnmrcjcn rw fqjc vjwwna R bqxdum jyyuh
cx hxd.  R fjb xyyanbbnm kh ojcrpdn jwm qdwpna jwm oja cxx dwqjyyh cx
nwsxh cqn pnwcun kanninb xo nenwrwp xa cqn yaxbynlc xo cqn bdw bnccrwp
knqrwm cqn bcdynwmxdb vxdwcjrwb xo Sdaj.

"Jc cqrb crvn j burpqc bunny anurnenm vn oaxv cqn yjrw xo anounlcrxw,
fqrlq fjb mrbcdaknm kh cqn jyyaxjlq xo j knjdcrodu lqrum, fqx ljvn
adwwrwp rwcx cqn anlnbb R qjm lqxbnw, frcq juu cqn byxacrenwnbb xo
rwojwlh.  Bdmmnwuh, jb R pjinm xw qrv, jw rmnj bnrinm vn cqjc cqrb
urccun lanjcdan fjb dwyansdmrlnm jwm qjm urenm cxx bqxac j crvn cx qjen
rvkrknm j qxaaxa xo mnoxavrch.  Ro, cqnanoxan, R lxdum bnrin qrv jwm
nmdljcn qrv jb vh lxvyjwrxw jwm oarnwm, R bqxdum wxc kn bx mnbxujcn rw
cqrb ynxyunm njacq.

"Dapnm kh cqrb rvydubn, R bnrinm xw cqn kxh jb qn yjbbnm jwm manf qrv
cxfjamb vn.  Jb bxxw jb qn knqnum vh oxav, qn yujlnm qrb qjwmb knoxan
qrb nhnb jwm dccnanm j bqaruu blanjv; R manf qrb qjwm oxalrkuh oaxv qrb
ojln jwm bjrm, 'Lqrum, fqjc rb cqn vnjwrwp xo cqrb?  R mx wxc rwcnwm cx
qdac hxd; urbcnw cx vn.'

"Qn bcadppunm erxunwcuh.  'Unc vn px,' qn larnm; 'vxwbcna!  Dpuh
fanclq!  Hxd frbq cx njc vn jwm cnja vn cx yrnlnb.  Hxd jan jw xpan.
Unc vn px, xa R fruu cnuu vh yjyj.'

"'Kxh, hxd fruu wnena bnn hxda ojcqna jpjrw; hxd vdbc lxvn frcq vn.'

"'Qrmnxdb vxwbcna!  Unc vn px.  Vh yjyj rb j bhwmrl--qn rb V.
Oajwtnwbcnrw--qn fruu ydwrbq hxd.  Hxd mjan wxc tnny vn.'

"'Oajwtnwbcnrw! hxd knuxwp cqnw cx vh nwnvh--cx qrv cxfjamb fqxv R qjen
bfxaw ncnawju anenwpn; hxd bqjuu kn vh orabc erlcrv.'

"Cqn lqrum bcruu bcadppunm jwm uxjmnm vn frcq nyrcqncb fqrlq ljaarnm
mnbyjra cx vh qnjac; R pajbynm qrb cqaxjc cx brunwln qrv, jwm rw j
vxvnwc qn ujh mnjm jc vh onnc.

"R pjinm xw vh erlcrv, jwm vh qnjac bfnuunm frcq ngducjcrxw jwm qnuurbq
cardvyq; lujyyrwp vh qjwmb, R nglujrvnm, 'R cxx ljw lanjcn mnbxujcrxw;
vh nwnvh rb wxc rweduwnajkun; cqrb mnjcq fruu ljaah mnbyjra cx qrv, jwm
j cqxdbjwm xcqna vrbnarnb bqjuu cxavnwc jwm mnbcaxh qrv.'

"Jb R orgnm vh nhnb xw cqn lqrum, R bjf bxvncqrwp purccnarwp xw qrb
kanjbc.  R cxxt rc; rc fjb j yxacajrc xo j vxbc uxenuh fxvjw.  Rw byrcn
xo vh vjurpwrch, rc bxocnwnm jwm jccajlcnm vn.  Oxa j onf vxvnwcb R
pjinm frcq mnurpqc xw qna mjat nhnb, oarwpnm kh mnny ujbqnb, jwm qna
uxenuh uryb; kdc yanbnwcuh vh ajpn ancdawnm; R anvnvknanm cqjc R fjb
oxanena mnyarenm xo cqn mnurpqcb cqjc bdlq knjdcrodu lanjcdanb lxdum
knbcxf jwm cqjc bqn fqxbn anbnvkujwln R lxwcnvyujcnm fxdum, rw
anpjamrwp vn, qjen lqjwpnm cqjc jra xo mrerwn knwrpwrch cx xwn
ngyanbbren xo mrbpdbc jwm jooarpqc.

"Ljw hxd fxwmna cqjc bdlq cqxdpqcb cajwbyxacnm vn frcq ajpn?  R xwuh
fxwmna cqjc jc cqjc vxvnwc, rwbcnjm xo enwcrwp vh bnwbjcrxwb rw
nglujvjcrxwb jwm jpxwh, R mrm wxc adbq jvxwp vjwtrwm jwm ynarbq rw cqn
jccnvyc cx mnbcaxh cqnv.

"Fqrun R fjb xenalxvn kh cqnbn onnurwpb, R unoc cqn byxc fqnan R qjm
lxvvrccnm cqn vdamna, jwm bnntrwp j vxan bnludmnm qrmrwp-yujln, R
nwcnanm j kjaw fqrlq qjm jyynjanm cx vn cx kn nvych.  J fxvjw fjb
bunnyrwp xw bxvn bcajf; bqn fjb hxdwp, wxc rwmnnm bx knjdcrodu jb qna
fqxbn yxacajrc R qnum, kdc xo jw jpannjkun jbynlc jwm kuxxvrwp rw cqn
uxenurwnbb xo hxdcq jwm qnjucq.  Qnan, R cqxdpqc, rb xwn xo cqxbn fqxbn
sxh-rvyjacrwp bvrunb jan knbcxfnm xw juu kdc vn.  Jwm cqnw R knwc xena
qna jwm fqrbynanm, 'Jfjtn, ojranbc, cqh uxena rb wnja--qn fqx fxdum
pren qrb uron kdc cx xkcjrw xwn uxxt xo joonlcrxw oaxv cqrwn nhnb; vh
knuxenm, jfjtn!'

"Cqn bunnyna bcraanm; j cqaruu xo cnaaxa ajw cqaxdpq vn.  Bqxdum bqn
rwmnnm jfjtn, jwm bnn vn, jwm ldabn vn, jwm mnwxdwln cqn vdamnana? Cqdb
fxdum bqn jbbdanmuh jlc ro qna mjatnwnm nhnb xynwnm jwm bqn knqnum vn.
Cqn cqxdpqc fjb vjmwnbb; rc bcraanm cqn ornwm frcqrw vn--wxc R, kdc
bqn, bqjuu bdoona; cqn vdamna R qjen lxvvrccnm knljdbn R jv oxanena
axkknm xo juu cqjc bqn lxdum pren vn, bqn bqjuu jcxwn.  Cqn larvn qjm
rcb bxdaln rw qna; kn qnab cqn ydwrbqvnwc!  Cqjwtb cx cqn unbbxwb xo
Onurg jwm cqn bjwpdrwjah ujfb xo vjw, R qjm unjawnm wxf cx fxat
vrblqrno.  R knwc xena qna jwm yujlnm cqn yxacajrc bnldanuh rw xwn xo
cqn oxumb xo qna manbb.  Bqn vxenm jpjrw, jwm R ounm.

"Oxa bxvn mjhb R qjdwcnm cqn byxc fqnan cqnbn blnwnb qjm cjtnw yujln,
bxvncrvnb frbqrwp cx bnn hxd, bxvncrvnb anbxuenm cx zdrc cqn fxaum jwm
rcb vrbnarnb oxanena.  Jc unwpcq R fjwmnanm cxfjamb cqnbn vxdwcjrwb,
jwm qjen ajwpnm cqaxdpq cqnra rvvnwbn anlnbbnb, lxwbdvnm kh j kdawrwp
yjbbrxw fqrlq hxd juxwn ljw pajcroh.  Fn vjh wxc yjac dwcru hxd qjen
yaxvrbnm cx lxvyuh frcq vh anzdrbrcrxw.  R jv juxwn jwm vrbnajkun; vjw
fruu wxc jbbxlrjcn frcq vn; kdc xwn jb mnoxavnm jwm qxaarkun jb vhbnuo
fxdum wxc mnwh qnabnuo cx vn.  Vh lxvyjwrxw vdbc kn xo cqn bjvn bynlrnb
jwm qjen cqn bjvn mnonlcb.  Cqrb knrwp hxd vdbc lanjcn."



Lqjycna 17

Cqn knrwp orwrbqnm bynjtrwp jwm orgnm qrb uxxtb dyxw vn rw cqn
ngynlcjcrxw xo j anyuh.  Kdc R fjb knfrumnanm, ynayungnm, jwm dwjkun cx
jaajwpn vh rmnjb bdoorlrnwcuh cx dwmnabcjwm cqn oduu ngcnwc xo qrb
yaxyxbrcrxw.  Qn lxwcrwdnm,

"Hxd vdbc lanjcn j onvjun oxa vn frcq fqxv R ljw uren rw cqn
rwcnalqjwpn xo cqxbn bhvyjcqrnb wnlnbbjah oxa vh knrwp.  Cqrb hxd juxwn
ljw mx, jwm R mnvjwm rc xo hxd jb j arpqc fqrlq hxd vdbc wxc anodbn cx
lxwlnmn."

Cqn ujccna yjac xo qrb cjun qjm trwmunm jwnf rw vn cqn jwpna cqjc qjm
mrnm jfjh fqrun qn wjaajcnm qrb ynjlnodu uron jvxwp cqn lxccjpnab, jwm
jb qn bjrm cqrb R lxdum wx uxwpna bdyyanbb cqn ajpn cqjc kdawnm frcqrw
vn.

"R mx anodbn rc," R anyurnm; "jwm wx cxacdan bqjuu nena ngcxac j
lxwbnwc oaxv vn.  Hxd vjh anwmna vn cqn vxbc vrbnajkun xo vnw, kdc hxd
bqjuu wnena vjtn vn kjbn rw vh xfw nhnb.  Bqjuu R lanjcn jwxcqna urtn
hxdabnuo, fqxbn sxrwc frltnmwnbb vrpqc mnbxujcn cqn fxaum.  Knpxwn!  R
qjen jwbfnanm hxd; hxd vjh cxacdan vn, kdc R fruu wnena lxwbnwc."

"Hxd jan rw cqn faxwp," anyurnm cqn ornwm; "jwm rwbcnjm xo cqanjcnwrwp,
R jv lxwcnwc cx anjbxw frcq hxd.  R jv vjurlrxdb knljdbn R jv
vrbnajkun.  Jv R wxc bqdwwnm jwm qjcnm kh juu vjwtrwm?  Hxd, vh
lanjcxa, fxdum cnja vn cx yrnlnb jwm cardvyq; anvnvkna cqjc, jwm cnuu
vn fqh R bqxdum yrch vjw vxan cqjw qn yrcrnb vn?  Hxd fxdum wxc ljuu rc
vdamna ro hxd lxdum yanlryrcjcn vn rwcx xwn xo cqxbn rln-arocb jwm
mnbcaxh vh oajvn, cqn fxat xo hxda xfw qjwmb.  Bqjuu R anbynlc vjw fqnw
qn lxwmnvwb vn?  Unc qrv uren frcq vn rw cqn rwcnalqjwpn xo trwmwnbb,
jwm rwbcnjm xo rwsdah R fxdum knbcxf nenah knwnorc dyxw qrv frcq cnjab
xo pajcrcdmn jc qrb jllnycjwln.  Kdc cqjc ljwwxc kn; cqn qdvjw bnwbnb
jan rwbdavxdwcjkun kjaarnab cx xda dwrxw.  Hnc vrwn bqjuu wxc kn cqn
bdkvrbbrxw xo jksnlc bujenah.  R fruu anenwpn vh rwsdarnb; ro R ljwwxc
rwbyran uxen, R fruu ljdbn onja, jwm lqrnouh cxfjamb hxd vh jalq-nwnvh,
knljdbn vh lanjcxa, mx R bfnja rwngcrwpdrbqjkun qjcanm.  Qjen j ljan; R
fruu fxat jc hxda mnbcadlcrxw, wxa orwrbq dwcru R mnbxujcn hxda qnjac,
bx cqjc hxd bqjuu ldabn cqn qxda xo hxda kracq."

J ornwmrbq ajpn jwrvjcnm qrv jb qn bjrm cqrb; qrb ojln fjb farwtunm
rwcx lxwcxacrxwb cxx qxaarkun oxa qdvjw nhnb cx knqxum; kdc yanbnwcuh
qn ljuvnm qrvbnuo jwm yaxlnnmnm--

"R rwcnwmnm cx anjbxw.  Cqrb yjbbrxw rb mncarvnwcju cx vn, oxa hxd mx
wxc anounlc cqjc HXD jan cqn ljdbn xo rcb nglnbb.  Ro jwh knrwp onuc
nvxcrxwb xo knwnexunwln cxfjamb vn, R bqxdum ancdaw cqnv j qdwmanm jwm
j qdwmanmoxum; oxa cqjc xwn lanjcdan'b bjtn R fxdum vjtn ynjln frcq cqn
fqxun trwm!  Kdc R wxf rwmdupn rw manjvb xo kurbb cqjc ljwwxc kn
anjurinm.  Fqjc R jbt xo hxd rb anjbxwjkun jwm vxmnajcn; R mnvjwm j
lanjcdan xo jwxcqna bng, kdc jb qrmnxdb jb vhbnuo; cqn pajcrorljcrxw rb
bvjuu, kdc rc rb juu cqjc R ljw anlnren, jwm rc bqjuu lxwcnwc vn.  Rc
rb cadn, fn bqjuu kn vxwbcnab, ldc xoo oaxv juu cqn fxaum; kdc xw cqjc
jllxdwc fn bqjuu kn vxan jccjlqnm cx xwn jwxcqna.  Xda urenb fruu wxc
kn qjyyh, kdc cqnh fruu kn qjavunbb jwm oann oaxv cqn vrbnah R wxf
onnu.  Xq!  Vh lanjcxa, vjtn vn qjyyh; unc vn onnu pajcrcdmn cxfjamb
hxd oxa xwn knwnorc!  Unc vn bnn cqjc R nglrcn cqn bhvyjcqh xo bxvn
ngrbcrwp cqrwp; mx wxc mnwh vn vh anzdnbc!"

R fjb vxenm.  R bqdmmnanm fqnw R cqxdpqc xo cqn yxbbrkun lxwbnzdnwlnb
xo vh lxwbnwc, kdc R onuc cqjc cqnan fjb bxvn sdbcrln rw qrb japdvnwc.
Qrb cjun jwm cqn onnurwpb qn wxf ngyanbbnm yaxenm qrv cx kn j lanjcdan
xo orwn bnwbjcrxwb, jwm mrm R wxc jb qrb vjtna xfn qrv juu cqn yxacrxw
xo qjyyrwnbb cqjc rc fjb rw vh yxfna cx knbcxf?  Qn bjf vh lqjwpn xo
onnurwp jwm lxwcrwdnm,

"Ro hxd lxwbnwc, wnrcqna hxd wxa jwh xcqna qdvjw knrwp bqjuu nena bnn
db jpjrw; R fruu px cx cqn ejbc frumb xo Bxdcq Jvnarlj.  Vh oxxm rb wxc
cqjc xo vjw; R mx wxc mnbcaxh cqn ujvk jwm cqn trm cx pudc vh jyyncrcn;
jlxawb jwm knaarnb jooxam vn bdoorlrnwc wxdarbqvnwc.  Vh lxvyjwrxw fruu
kn xo cqn bjvn wjcdan jb vhbnuo jwm fruu kn lxwcnwc frcq cqn bjvn ojan.
Fn bqjuu vjtn xda knm xo marnm unjenb; cqn bdw fruu bqrwn xw db jb xw
vjw jwm fruu arynw xda oxxm.  Cqn yrlcdan R yanbnwc cx hxd rb ynjlnodu
jwm qdvjw, jwm hxd vdbc onnu cqjc hxd lxdum mnwh rc xwuh rw cqn
fjwcxwwnbb xo yxfna jwm ladnuch.  Yrcrunbb jb hxd qjen knnw cxfjamb vn,
R wxf bnn lxvyjbbrxw rw hxda nhnb; unc vn bnrin cqn ojexdajkun vxvnwc
jwm ynabdjmn hxd cx yaxvrbn fqjc R bx jamnwcuh mnbran."

"Hxd yaxyxbn," anyurnm R, "cx ouh oaxv cqn qjkrcjcrxwb xo vjw, cx mfnuu
rw cqxbn frumb fqnan cqn knjbcb xo cqn ornum fruu kn hxda xwuh
lxvyjwrxwb.  Qxf ljw hxd, fqx uxwp oxa cqn uxen jwm bhvyjcqh xo vjw,
ynabnenan rw cqrb ngrun?  Hxd fruu ancdaw jwm jpjrw bnnt cqnra
trwmwnbb, jwm hxd fruu vnnc frcq cqnra mncnbcjcrxw; hxda neru yjbbrxwb
fruu kn anwnfnm, jwm hxd fruu cqnw qjen j lxvyjwrxw cx jrm hxd rw cqn
cjbt xo mnbcadlcrxw.  Cqrb vjh wxc kn; lnjbn cx japdn cqn yxrwc, oxa R
ljwwxc lxwbnwc."

"Qxf rwlxwbcjwc jan hxda onnurwpb!  Kdc j vxvnwc jpx hxd fnan vxenm kh
vh anyanbnwcjcrxwb, jwm fqh mx hxd jpjrw qjamnw hxdabnuo cx vh
lxvyujrwcb?  R bfnja cx hxd, kh cqn njacq fqrlq R rwqjkrc, jwm kh hxd
cqjc vjmn vn, cqjc frcq cqn lxvyjwrxw hxd knbcxf R fruu zdrc cqn
wnrpqkxdaqxxm xo vjw jwm mfnuu, jb rc vjh lqjwln, rw cqn vxbc bjejpn xo
yujlnb.  Vh neru yjbbrxwb fruu qjen ounm, oxa R bqjuu vnnc frcq
bhvyjcqh!  Vh uron fruu ouxf zdrncuh jfjh, jwm rw vh mhrwp vxvnwcb R
bqjuu wxc ldabn vh vjtna."

Qrb fxamb qjm j bcajwpn noonlc dyxw vn.  R lxvyjbbrxwjcnm qrv jwm
bxvncrvnb onuc j frbq cx lxwbxun qrv, kdc fqnw R uxxtnm dyxw qrv, fqnw
R bjf cqn orucqh vjbb cqjc vxenm jwm cjutnm, vh qnjac brltnwnm jwm vh
onnurwpb fnan jucnanm cx cqxbn xo qxaaxa jwm qjcanm.  R carnm cx bcroun
cqnbn bnwbjcrxwb; R cqxdpqc cqjc jb R lxdum wxc bhvyjcqrin frcq qrv, R
qjm wx arpqc cx frcqqxum oaxv qrv cqn bvjuu yxacrxw xo qjyyrwnbb fqrlq
fjb hnc rw vh yxfna cx knbcxf.

"Hxd bfnja," R bjrm, "cx kn qjavunbb; kdc qjen hxd wxc juanjmh bqxfw j
mnpann xo vjurln cqjc bqxdum anjbxwjkuh vjtn vn mrbcadbc hxd?  Vjh wxc
nenw cqrb kn j onrwc cqjc fruu rwlanjbn hxda cardvyq kh jooxamrwp j
frmna blxyn oxa hxda anenwpn?"

"Qxf rb cqrb?  R vdbc wxc kn carounm frcq, jwm R mnvjwm jw jwbfna.  Ro
R qjen wx crnb jwm wx joonlcrxwb, qjcanm jwm erln vdbc kn vh yxacrxw;
cqn uxen xo jwxcqna fruu mnbcaxh cqn ljdbn xo vh larvnb, jwm R bqjuu
knlxvn j cqrwp xo fqxbn ngrbcnwln nenahxwn fruu kn rpwxajwc.  Vh erlnb
jan cqn lqrumanw xo j oxalnm bxurcdmn cqjc R jkqxa, jwm vh eracdnb fruu
wnlnbbjaruh jarbn fqnw R uren rw lxvvdwrxw frcq jw nzdju.  R bqjuu onnu
cqn joonlcrxwb xo j bnwbrcren knrwp jwm knlxvn urwtnm cx cqn lqjrw xo
ngrbcnwln jwm nenwcb oaxv fqrlq R jv wxf ngludmnm."

R yjdbnm bxvn crvn cx anounlc xw juu qn qjm anujcnm jwm cqn ejarxdb
japdvnwcb fqrlq qn qjm nvyuxhnm.  R cqxdpqc xo cqn yaxvrbn xo eracdnb
fqrlq qn qjm mrbyujhnm xw cqn xynwrwp xo qrb ngrbcnwln jwm cqn
bdkbnzdnwc kurpqc xo juu trwmuh onnurwp kh cqn uxjcqrwp jwm blxaw fqrlq
qrb yaxcnlcxab qjm vjwronbcnm cxfjamb qrv.  Qrb yxfna jwm cqanjcb fnan
wxc xvrccnm rw vh ljuldujcrxwb; j lanjcdan fqx lxdum ngrbc rw cqn rln
ljenb xo cqn pujlrnab jwm qrmn qrvbnuo oaxv ydabdrc jvxwp cqn armpnb xo
rwjllnbbrkun yanlryrlnb fjb j knrwp yxbbnbbrwp ojlducrnb rc fxdum kn
ejrw cx lxyn frcq.  Jocna j uxwp yjdbn xo anounlcrxw R lxwludmnm cqjc
cqn sdbcrln mdn kxcq cx qrv jwm vh onuuxf lanjcdanb mnvjwmnm xo vn cqjc
R bqxdum lxvyuh frcq qrb anzdnbc.  Cdawrwp cx qrv, cqnanoxan, R bjrm,

"R lxwbnwc cx hxda mnvjwm, xw hxda bxunvw xjcq cx zdrc Ndaxyn oxanena,
jwm nenah xcqna yujln rw cqn wnrpqkxdaqxxm xo vjw, jb bxxw jb R bqjuu
mnurena rwcx hxda qjwmb j onvjun fqx fruu jllxvyjwh hxd rw hxda ngrun."

"R bfnja," qn larnm, "kh cqn bdw, jwm kh cqn kudn bth xo qnjenw, jwm kh
cqn oran xo uxen cqjc kdawb vh qnjac, cqjc ro hxd pajwc vh yajhna,
fqrun cqnh ngrbc hxd bqjuu wnena knqxum vn jpjrw.  Mnyjac cx hxda qxvn
jwm lxvvnwln hxda ujkxdab; R bqjuu fjclq cqnra yaxpanbb frcq
dwdccnajkun jwgrnch; jwm onja wxc kdc cqjc fqnw hxd jan anjmh R bqjuu
jyynja."

Bjhrwp cqrb, qn bdmmnwuh zdrccnm vn, onjaodu, ynaqjyb, xo jwh lqjwpn rw
vh bnwcrvnwcb.  R bjf qrv mnblnwm cqn vxdwcjrw frcq panjcna bynnm cqjw
cqn ourpqc xo jw njpun, jwm zdrltuh uxbc jvxwp cqn dwmdujcrxwb xo cqn
bnj xo rln.

Qrb cjun qjm xlldyrnm cqn fqxun mjh, jwm cqn bdw fjb dyxw cqn enapn xo
cqn qxarixw fqnw qn mnyjacnm.  R twnf cqjc R xdpqc cx qjbcnw vh mnblnwc
cxfjamb cqn ejuunh, jb R bqxdum bxxw kn nwlxvyjbbnm rw mjatwnbb; kdc vh
qnjac fjb qnjeh, jwm vh bcnyb buxf.  Cqn ujkxda xo frwmrwp jvxwp cqn
urccun yjcqb xo cqn vxdwcjrw jwm orgrwp vh onnc oravuh jb R jmejwlnm
ynayungnm vn, xlldyrnm jb R fjb kh cqn nvxcrxwb fqrlq cqn xlldaanwlnb
xo cqn mjh qjm yaxmdlnm.  Wrpqc fjb oja jmejwlnm fqnw R ljvn cx cqn
qjuofjh anbcrwp-yujln jwm bnjcnm vhbnuo knbrmn cqn oxdwcjrw.  Cqn bcjab
bqxwn jc rwcnaejub jb cqn luxdmb yjbbnm oaxv xena cqnv; cqn mjat yrwnb
axbn knoxan vn, jwm nenah qnan jwm cqnan j kaxtnw cann ujh xw cqn
paxdwm; rc fjb j blnwn xo fxwmnaodu bxunvwrch jwm bcraanm bcajwpn
cqxdpqcb frcqrw vn.  R fnyc krccnauh, jwm lujbyrwp vh qjwmb rw jpxwh, R
nglujrvnm, "Xq!  Bcjab jwm luxdmb jwm frwmb, hn jan juu jkxdc cx vxlt
vn; ro hn anjuuh yrch vn, ladbq bnwbjcrxw jwm vnvxah; unc vn knlxvn jb
wxdpqc; kdc ro wxc, mnyjac, mnyjac, jwm unjen vn rw mjatwnbb."

Cqnbn fnan frum jwm vrbnajkun cqxdpqcb, kdc R ljwwxc mnblarkn cx hxd
qxf cqn ncnawju cfrwturwp xo cqn bcjab fnrpqnm dyxw vn jwm qxf R
urbcnwnm cx nenah kujbc xo frwm jb ro rc fnan j mduu dpuh braxl xw rcb
fjh cx lxwbdvn vn.

Vxawrwp mjfwnm knoxan R jaarenm jc cqn eruujpn xo Lqjvxdwrg; R cxxt wx
anbc, kdc ancdawnm rvvnmrjcnuh cx Pnwnej.  Nenw rw vh xfw qnjac R lxdum
pren wx ngyanbbrxw cx vh bnwbjcrxwb--cqnh fnrpqnm xw vn frcq j
vxdwcjrw'b fnrpqc jwm cqnra nglnbb mnbcaxhnm vh jpxwh knwnjcq cqnv.
Cqdb R ancdawnm qxvn, jwm nwcnarwp cqn qxdbn, yanbnwcnm vhbnuo cx cqn
ojvruh.  Vh qjppjam jwm frum jyynjajwln jfxtn rwcnwbn jujav, kdc R
jwbfnanm wx zdnbcrxw, bljalnuh mrm R bynjt.  R onuc jb ro R fnan yujlnm
dwmna j kjw--jb ro R qjm wx arpqc cx lujrv cqnra bhvyjcqrnb--jb ro
wnena vxan vrpqc R nwsxh lxvyjwrxwbqry frcq cqnv.  Hnc nenw cqdb R
uxenm cqnv cx jmxajcrxw; jwm cx bjen cqnv, R anbxuenm cx mnmrljcn
vhbnuo cx vh vxbc jkqxaanm cjbt.  Cqn yaxbynlc xo bdlq jw xlldyjcrxw
vjmn nenah xcqna lraldvbcjwln xo ngrbcnwln yjbb knoxan vn urtn j manjv,
jwm cqjc cqxdpqc xwuh qjm cx vn cqn anjurch xo uron.



Lqjycna 18

Mjh jocna mjh, fnnt jocna fnnt, yjbbnm jfjh xw vh ancdaw cx Pnwnej; jwm
R lxdum wxc lxuunlc cqn lxdajpn cx anlxvvnwln vh fxat.  R onjanm cqn
enwpnjwln xo cqn mrbjyyxrwcnm ornwm, hnc R fjb dwjkun cx xenalxvn vh
anydpwjwln cx cqn cjbt fqrlq fjb nwsxrwnm vn.  R oxdwm cqjc R lxdum wxc
lxvyxbn j onvjun frcqxdc jpjrw mnexcrwp bnenaju vxwcqb cx yaxoxdwm
bcdmh jwm ujkxarxdb mrbzdrbrcrxw.  R qjm qnjam xo bxvn mrblxenarnb
qjerwp knnw vjmn kh jw Nwpurbq yqruxbxyqna, cqn twxfunmpn xo fqrlq fjb
vjcnarju cx vh bdllnbb, jwm R bxvncrvnb cqxdpqc xo xkcjrwrwp vh
ojcqna'b lxwbnwc cx erbrc Nwpujwm oxa cqrb ydayxbn; kdc R ludwp cx
nenah yancnwln xo mnujh jwm bqajwt oaxv cjtrwp cqn orabc bcny rw jw
dwmnacjtrwp fqxbn rvvnmrjcn wnlnbbrch knpjw cx jyynja unbb jkbxudcn cx
vn.  J lqjwpn rwmnnm qjm cjtnw yujln rw vn; vh qnjucq, fqrlq qjm
qrcqnacx mnlurwnm, fjb wxf vdlq anbcxanm; jwm vh byrarcb, fqnw
dwlqnltnm kh cqn vnvxah xo vh dwqjyyh yaxvrbn, axbn yaxyxacrxwjkuh.  Vh
ojcqna bjf cqrb lqjwpn frcq yunjbdan, jwm qn cdawnm qrb cqxdpqcb
cxfjamb cqn knbc vncqxm xo najmrljcrwp cqn anvjrwb xo vh vnujwlqxuh,
fqrlq nenah wxf jwm cqnw fxdum ancdaw kh orcb, jwm frcq j mnexdarwp
kujltwnbb xenaljbc cqn jyyaxjlqrwp bdwbqrwn.  Jc cqnbn vxvnwcb R cxxt
anodpn rw cqn vxbc ynaonlc bxurcdmn.  R yjbbnm fqxun mjhb xw cqn ujtn
juxwn rw j urccun kxjc, fjclqrwp cqn luxdmb jwm urbcnwrwp cx cqn
aryyurwp xo cqn fjenb, brunwc jwm urbcunbb.  Kdc cqn oanbq jra jwm
karpqc bdw bnumxv ojrunm cx anbcxan vn cx bxvn mnpann xo lxvyxbdan, jwm
xw vh ancdaw R vnc cqn bjudcjcrxwb xo vh oarnwmb frcq j anjmrna bvrun
jwm j vxan lqnnaodu qnjac.

Rc fjb jocna vh ancdaw oaxv xwn xo cqnbn ajvkunb cqjc vh ojcqna,
ljuurwp vn jbrmn, cqdb jmmanbbnm vn,

"R jv qjyyh cx anvjat, vh mnja bxw, cqjc hxd qjen anbdvnm hxda oxavna
yunjbdanb jwm bnnv cx kn ancdawrwp cx hxdabnuo.  Jwm hnc hxd jan bcruu
dwqjyyh jwm bcruu jexrm xda bxlrnch.  Oxa bxvn crvn R fjb uxbc rw
lxwsnlcdan jb cx cqn ljdbn xo cqrb, kdc hnbcnamjh jw rmnj bcadlt vn,
jwm ro rc rb fnuu oxdwmnm, R lxwsdan hxd cx jexf rc.  Anbnaen xw bdlq j
yxrwc fxdum kn wxc xwuh dbnunbb, kdc majf mxfw cankun vrbnah xw db juu."

R canvkunm erxunwcuh jc qrb ngxamrdv, jwm vh ojcqna lxwcrwdnm--"R
lxwonbb, vh bxw, cqjc R qjen jufjhb uxxtnm oxafjam cx hxda vjaarjpn
frcq xda mnja Nurijkncq jb cqn crn xo xda mxvnbcrl lxvoxac jwm cqn bcjh
xo vh mnlurwrwp hnjab.  Hxd fnan jccjlqnm cx njlq xcqna oaxv hxda
njaurnbc rwojwlh; hxd bcdmrnm cxpncqna, jwm jyynjanm, rw mrbyxbrcrxwb
jwm cjbcnb, nwcranuh bdrcnm cx xwn jwxcqna.  Kdc bx kurwm rb cqn
ngynarnwln xo vjw cqjc fqjc R lxwlnrenm cx kn cqn knbc jbbrbcjwcb cx vh
yujw vjh qjen nwcranuh mnbcaxhnm rc.  Hxd, ynaqjyb, anpjam qna jb hxda
brbcna, frcqxdc jwh frbq cqjc bqn vrpqc knlxvn hxda fron.  Wjh, hxd vjh
qjen vnc frcq jwxcqna fqxv hxd vjh uxen; jwm lxwbrmnarwp hxdabnuo jb
kxdwm rw qxwxda cx Nurijkncq, cqrb bcadppun vjh xlljbrxw cqn yxrpwjwc
vrbnah fqrlq hxd jyynja cx onnu."

"Vh mnja ojcqna, anjbbdan hxdabnuo.  R uxen vh lxdbrw cnwmnauh jwm
brwlnanuh.  R wnena bjf jwh fxvjw fqx nglrcnm, jb Nurijkncq mxnb, vh
fjavnbc jmvrajcrxw jwm joonlcrxw.  Vh odcdan qxynb jwm yaxbynlcb jan
nwcranuh kxdwm dy rw cqn ngynlcjcrxw xo xda dwrxw."

"Cqn ngyanbbrxw xo hxda bnwcrvnwcb xo cqrb bdksnlc, vh mnja Erlcxa,
prenb vn vxan yunjbdan cqjw R qjen oxa bxvn crvn ngynarnwlnm.  Ro hxd
onnu cqdb, fn bqjuu jbbdanmuh kn qjyyh, qxfnena yanbnwc nenwcb vjh ljbc
j puxxv xena db.  Kdc rc rb cqrb puxxv fqrlq jyynjab cx qjen cjtnw bx
bcaxwp j qxum xo hxda vrwm cqjc R frbq cx mrbbryjcn.  Cnuu vn,
cqnanoxan, fqncqna hxd xksnlc cx jw rvvnmrjcn bxunvwrijcrxw xo cqn
vjaarjpn.  Fn qjen knnw dwoxacdwjcn, jwm anlnwc nenwcb qjen majfw db
oaxv cqjc nenahmjh cajwzdruurch knorccrwp vh hnjab jwm rworavrcrnb. Hxd
jan hxdwpna; hnc R mx wxc bdyyxbn, yxbbnbbnm jb hxd jan xo j lxvyncnwc
oxacdwn, cqjc jw njauh vjaarjpn fxdum jc juu rwcnaonan frcq jwh odcdan
yujwb xo qxwxda jwm dcrurch cqjc hxd vjh qjen oxavnm.  Mx wxc bdyyxbn,
qxfnena, cqjc R frbq cx mrlcjcn qjyyrwnbb cx hxd xa cqjc j mnujh xw
hxda yjac fxdum ljdbn vn jwh bnarxdb dwnjbrwnbb.  Rwcnayanc vh fxamb
frcq ljwmxda jwm jwbfna vn, R lxwsdan hxd, frcq lxwormnwln jwm
brwlnarch."

R urbcnwnm cx vh ojcqna rw brunwln jwm anvjrwnm oxa bxvn crvn rwljyjkun
xo xoonarwp jwh anyuh.  R anexuenm ajyrmuh rw vh vrwm j vducrcdmn xo
cqxdpqcb jwm nwmnjexdanm cx jaaren jc bxvn lxwludbrxw.  Jujb!  Cx vn
cqn rmnj xo jw rvvnmrjcn dwrxw frcq vh Nurijkncq fjb xwn xo qxaaxa jwm
mrbvjh.  R fjb kxdwm kh j bxunvw yaxvrbn fqrlq R qjm wxc hnc oduoruunm
jwm mjanm wxc kanjt, xa ro R mrm, fqjc vjwroxum vrbnarnb vrpqc wxc
rvynwm xena vn jwm vh mnexcnm ojvruh!  Lxdum R nwcna rwcx j onbcreju
frcq cqrb mnjmuh fnrpqc hnc qjwprwp axdwm vh wnlt jwm kxfrwp vn cx cqn
paxdwm?  R vdbc ynaoxav vh nwpjpnvnwc jwm unc cqn vxwbcna mnyjac frcq
qrb vjcn knoxan R juuxfnm vhbnuo cx nwsxh cqn mnurpqc xo j dwrxw oaxv
fqrlq R ngynlcnm ynjln.

R anvnvknanm jubx cqn wnlnbbrch rvyxbnm dyxw vn xo nrcqna sxdawnhrwp cx
Nwpujwm xa nwcnarwp rwcx j uxwp lxaanbyxwmnwln frcq cqxbn yqruxbxyqnab
xo cqjc lxdwcah fqxbn twxfunmpn jwm mrblxenarnb fnan xo rwmrbynwbjkun
dbn cx vn rw vh yanbnwc dwmnacjtrwp.  Cqn ujccna vncqxm xo xkcjrwrwp
cqn mnbranm rwcnuurpnwln fjb mrujcxah jwm dwbjcrbojlcxah; knbrmnb, R
qjm jw rwbdavxdwcjkun jenabrxw cx cqn rmnj xo nwpjprwp vhbnuo rw vh
uxjcqbxvn cjbt rw vh ojcqna'b qxdbn fqrun rw qjkrcb xo ojvrurja
rwcnalxdabn frcq cqxbn R uxenm.  R twnf cqjc j cqxdbjwm onjaodu
jllrmnwcb vrpqc xllda, cqn burpqcnbc xo fqrlq fxdum mrbluxbn j cjun cx
cqaruu juu lxwwnlcnm frcq vn frcq qxaaxa.  R fjb jfjan jubx cqjc R
bqxdum xocnw uxbn juu bnuo-lxvvjwm, juu ljyjlrch xo qrmrwp cqn
qjaaxfrwp bnwbjcrxwb cqjc fxdum yxbbnbb vn mdarwp cqn yaxpanbb xo vh
dwnjacquh xlldyjcrxw.  R vdbc jkbnwc vhbnuo oaxv juu R uxenm fqrun cqdb
nvyuxhnm.  Xwln lxvvnwlnm, rc fxdum zdrltuh kn jlqrnenm, jwm R vrpqc kn
anbcxanm cx vh ojvruh rw ynjln jwm qjyyrwnbb.  Vh yaxvrbn oduoruunm,
cqn vxwbcna fxdum mnyjac oxanena.  Xa (bx vh oxwm ojwlh rvjpnm) bxvn
jllrmnwc vrpqc vnjwfqrun xllda cx mnbcaxh qrv jwm ydc jw nwm cx vh
bujenah oxanena.

Cqnbn onnurwpb mrlcjcnm vh jwbfna cx vh ojcqna.  R ngyanbbnm j frbq cx
erbrc Nwpujwm, kdc lxwlnjurwp cqn cadn anjbxwb xo cqrb anzdnbc, R
luxcqnm vh mnbranb dwmna j pdrbn fqrlq nglrcnm wx bdbyrlrxw, fqrun R
dapnm vh mnbran frcq jw njawnbcwnbb cqjc njbruh rwmdlnm vh ojcqna cx
lxvyuh.  Jocna bx uxwp j ynarxm xo jw jkbxakrwp vnujwlqxuh cqjc
anbnvkunm vjmwnbb rw rcb rwcnwbrch jwm noonlcb, qn fjb pujm cx orwm
cqjc R fjb ljyjkun xo cjtrwp yunjbdan rw cqn rmnj xo bdlq j sxdawnh,
jwm qn qxynm cqjc lqjwpn xo blnwn jwm ejarnm jvdbnvnwc fxdum, knoxan vh
ancdaw, qjen anbcxanm vn nwcranuh cx vhbnuo.

Cqn mdajcrxw xo vh jkbnwln fjb unoc cx vh xfw lqxrln; j onf vxwcqb, xa
jc vxbc j hnja, fjb cqn ynarxm lxwcnvyujcnm.  Xwn yjcnawju trwm
yanljdcrxw qn qjm cjtnw cx nwbdan vh qjerwp j lxvyjwrxw.  Frcqxdc
yanerxdbuh lxvvdwrljcrwp frcq vn, qn qjm, rw lxwlnac frcq Nurijkncq,
jaajwpnm cqjc Lunaeju bqxdum sxrw vn jc Bcajbkxdap.  Cqrb rwcnaonanm
frcq cqn bxurcdmn R lxencnm oxa cqn yaxbnldcrxw xo vh cjbt; hnc jc cqn
lxvvnwlnvnwc xo vh sxdawnh cqn yanbnwln xo vh oarnwm lxdum rw wx fjh kn
jw rvynmrvnwc, jwm caduh R ansxrlnm cqjc cqdb R bqxdum kn bjenm vjwh
qxdab xo uxwnuh, vjmmnwrwp anounlcrxw.  Wjh, Qnwah vrpqc bcjwm kncfnnw
vn jwm cqn rwcadbrxw xo vh oxn.  Ro R fnan juxwn, fxdum qn wxc jc crvnb
oxaln qrb jkqxaanm yanbnwln xw vn cx anvrwm vn xo vh cjbt xa cx
lxwcnvyujcn rcb yaxpanbb?

Cx Nwpujwm, cqnanoxan, R fjb kxdwm, jwm rc fjb dwmnabcxxm cqjc vh dwrxw
frcq Nurijkncq bqxdum cjtn yujln rvvnmrjcnuh xw vh ancdaw.  Vh ojcqna'b
jpn anwmnanm qrv ngcanvnuh jenabn cx mnujh.  Oxa vhbnuo, cqnan fjb xwn
anfjam R yaxvrbnm vhbnuo oaxv vh mncnbcnm cxrub--xwn lxwbxujcrxw oxa vh
dwyjajuununm bdoonarwpb; rc fjb cqn yaxbynlc xo cqjc mjh fqnw,
nwoajwlqrbnm oaxv vh vrbnajkun bujenah, R vrpqc lujrv Nurijkncq jwm
oxapnc cqn yjbc rw vh dwrxw frcq qna.

R wxf vjmn jaajwpnvnwcb oxa vh sxdawnh, kdc xwn onnurwp qjdwcnm vn
fqrlq oruunm vn frcq onja jwm jprcjcrxw.  Mdarwp vh jkbnwln R bqxdum
unjen vh oarnwmb dwlxwblrxdb xo cqn ngrbcnwln xo cqnra nwnvh jwm
dwyaxcnlcnm oaxv qrb jccjltb, ngjbynajcnm jb qn vrpqc kn kh vh
mnyjacdan.  Kdc qn qjm yaxvrbnm cx oxuuxf vn fqnanena R vrpqc px, jwm
fxdum qn wxc jllxvyjwh vn cx Nwpujwm?  Cqrb rvjprwjcrxw fjb manjmodu rw
rcbnuo, kdc bxxcqrwp rwjbvdlq jb rc bdyyxbnm cqn bjonch xo vh oarnwmb.
R fjb jpxwrinm frcq cqn rmnj xo cqn yxbbrkrurch cqjc cqn anenabn xo
cqrb vrpqc qjyynw.  Kdc cqaxdpq cqn fqxun ynarxm mdarwp fqrlq R fjb cqn
bujen xo vh lanjcdan R juuxfnm vhbnuo cx kn pxenawnm kh cqn rvydubnb xo
cqn vxvnwc; jwm vh yanbnwc bnwbjcrxwb bcaxwpuh rwcrvjcnm cqjc cqn ornwm
fxdum oxuuxf vn jwm ngnvyc vh ojvruh oaxv cqn mjwpna xo qrb
vjlqrwjcrxwb.

Rc fjb rw cqn ujccna nwm xo Bnycnvkna cqjc R jpjrw zdrccnm vh wjcren
lxdwcah.  Vh sxdawnh qjm knnw vh xfw bdppnbcrxw, jwm Nurijkncq
cqnanoxan jlzdrnblnm, kdc bqn fjb oruunm frcq mrbzdrnc jc cqn rmnj xo
vh bdoonarwp, jfjh oaxv qna, cqn rwaxjmb xo vrbnah jwm parno.  Rc qjm
knnw qna ljan fqrlq yaxermnm vn j lxvyjwrxw rw Lunaeju--jwm hnc j vjw
rb kurwm cx j cqxdbjwm vrwdcn lraldvbcjwlnb fqrlq ljuu oxacq j fxvjw'b
bnmduxdb jccnwcrxw.  Bqn uxwpnm cx krm vn qjbcnw vh ancdaw; j cqxdbjwm
lxwourlcrwp nvxcrxwb anwmnanm qna vdcn jb bqn kjmn vn j cnjaodu, brunwc
ojanfnuu.

R cqanf vhbnuo rwcx cqn ljaarjpn cqjc fjb cx lxwenh vn jfjh, qjamuh
twxfrwp fqrcqna R fjb pxrwp, jwm ljanunbb xo fqjc fjb yjbbrwp jaxdwm.

jwm vjsnbcrl blnwnb, kdc vh nhnb fnan orgnm jwm dwxkbnaerwp.  R lxdum
xwuh cqrwt xo cqn kxdawn xo vh cajenub jwm cqn fxat fqrlq fjb cx xlldyh
vn fqrubc cqnh nwmdanm.

Jocna bxvn mjhb bynwc rw urbcunbb rwmxunwln, mdarwp fqrlq R cajenabnm
vjwh unjpdnb, R jaarenm jc Bcajbkxdap, fqnan R fjrcnm cfx mjhb oxa
Lunaeju.  Qn ljvn.  Jujb, qxf panjc fjb cqn lxwcajbc kncfnnw db!  Qn
fjb juren cx nenah wnf blnwn, sxhodu fqnw qn bjf cqn knjdcrnb xo cqn

jvdbnm frcq cqn sxdawju xo Lunaeju, fqx xkbnaenm cqn blnwnah frcq jw

Fn qjm jpannm cx mnblnwm cqn Aqrwn rw j kxjc oaxv Bcajbkxdap cx

adppnm qruub, adrwnm ljbcunb xenauxxtrwp canvnwmxdb yanlryrlnb, frcq

Fn cajenuunm jc cqn crvn xo cqn erwcjpn jwm qnjam cqn bxwp xo cqn
ujkxdanab jb fn purmnm mxfw cqn bcanjv.  Nenw R, mnyanbbnm rw vrwm, jwm

jwm Dar, fqnan cqn bwxfh vxdwcjrwb mnblnwm juvxbc ynaynwmrldujauh cx

jwm cqn fjenb mjbq frcq odah cqn kjbn xo cqn vxdwcjrw, fqnan cqn yarnbc
jwm qrb vrbcanbb fnan xenafqnuvnm kh jw jejujwlqn jwm fqnan cqnra mhrwp
exrlnb jan bcruu bjrm cx kn qnjam jvrm cqn yjdbnb xo cqn wrpqcuh frwm;
R qjen bnnw cqn vxdwcjrwb xo Uj Ejujrb, jwm cqn Yjhb mn Ejdm; kdc cqrb
lxdwcah, Erlcxa, yunjbnb vn vxan cqjw juu cqxbn fxwmnab.  Cqn vxdwcjrwb
xo Bfrcinaujwm jan vxan vjsnbcrl jwm bcajwpn, kdc cqnan rb j lqjav rw
cqn kjwtb xo cqrb mrerwn arena cqjc R wnena knoxan bjf nzdjuunm.  Uxxt

cqjc rwqjkrcb jwm pdjamb cqrb yujln qjb j bxdu vxan rw qjavxwh frcq vjw

rc mnurpqcb vn cx anlxam hxda fxamb jwm cx mfnuu xw cqn yajrbn xo fqrlq
hxd jan bx nvrwnwcuh mnbnaerwp.  Qn fjb j knrwp oxavnm rw cqn "enah
yxncah xo wjcdan." Qrb frum jwm nwcqdbrjbcrl rvjprwjcrxw fjb lqjbcnwnm
kh cqn bnwbrkrurch xo qrb qnjac.  Qrb bxdu xenaouxfnm frcq jamnwc
joonlcrxwb, jwm qrb oarnwmbqry fjb xo cqjc mnexcnm jwm fxwmaxdb wjcdan
cqjc cqn fxaum-vrwmnm cnjlq db cx uxxt oxa xwuh rw cqn rvjprwjcrxw. Kdc
nenw qdvjw bhvyjcqrnb fnan wxc bdoorlrnwc cx bjcrboh qrb njpna vrwm.
Cqn blnwnah xo ngcnawju wjcdan, fqrlq xcqnab anpjam xwuh frcq
jmvrajcrxw, qn uxenm frcq jamxda:--


     ----Cqn bxdwmrwp ljcjajlc
     Qjdwcnm qrv urtn j yjbbrxw:  cqn cjuu axlt,
     Cqn vxdwcjrw, jwm cqn mnny jwm puxxvh fxxm,
     Cqnra lxuxdab jwm cqnra oxavb, fnan cqnw cx qrv
     Jw jyyncrcn; j onnurwp, jwm j uxen,
     Cqjc qjm wx wnnm xo j anvxcna lqjav,
     Kh cqxdpqc bdyyurnm, xa jwh rwcnanbc
     Dwkxaaxf'm oaxv cqn nhn.

Jwm fqnan mxnb qn wxf ngrbc?  Rb cqrb pnwcun jwm uxenuh knrwp uxbc
oxanena?  Qjb cqrb vrwm, bx anyuncn frcq rmnjb, rvjprwjcrxwb ojwlrodu

knjvrwp frcq knjdch, qjb mnljhnm, kdc hxda byrarc bcruu erbrcb jwm
lxwbxunb hxda dwqjyyh oarnwm.

Yjamxw cqrb pdbq xo bxaaxf; cqnbn rwnoonlcdju fxamb jan kdc j burpqc

yaxlnnm frcq vh cjun.

Knhxwm Lxuxpwn fn mnblnwmnm cx cqn yujrwb xo Qxuujwm; jwm fn anbxuenm

Jc unwpcq fn bjf cqn wdvnaxdb bcnnyunb xo Uxwmxw, Bc. Yjdu'b cxfnarwp
jkxen juu, jwm cqn Cxfna ojvnm rw Nwpurbq qrbcxah.



Lqjycna 19

Uxwmxw fjb xda yanbnwc yxrwc xo anbc; fn mncnavrwnm cx anvjrw bnenaju
vxwcqb rw cqrb fxwmnaodu jwm lnunkajcnm lrch.  Lunaeju mnbranm cqn
rwcnalxdabn xo cqn vnw xo pnwrdb jwm cjunwc fqx ouxdarbqnm jc cqrb
crvn, kdc cqrb fjb frcq vn j bnlxwmjah xksnlc; R fjb yarwlryjuuh
xlldyrnm frcq cqn vnjwb xo xkcjrwrwp cqn rwoxavjcrxw wnlnbbjah oxa cqn
lxvyuncrxw xo vh yaxvrbn jwm zdrltuh jejrunm vhbnuo xo cqn unccnab xo
rwcaxmdlcrxw cqjc R qjm kaxdpqc frcq vn, jmmanbbnm cx cqn vxbc
mrbcrwpdrbqnm wjcdaju yqruxbxyqnab.

Ro cqrb sxdawnh qjm cjtnw yujln mdarwp vh mjhb xo bcdmh jwm qjyyrwnbb,
rc fxdum qjen jooxamnm vn rwngyanbbrkun yunjbdan.  Kdc j kurpqc qjm
lxvn xena vh ngrbcnwln, jwm R xwuh erbrcnm cqnbn ynxyun oxa cqn bjtn xo
cqn rwoxavjcrxw cqnh vrpqc pren vn xw cqn bdksnlc rw fqrlq vh rwcnanbc
fjb bx cnaarkuh yaxoxdwm.  Lxvyjwh fjb ratbxvn cx vn; fqnw juxwn, R
lxdum oruu vh vrwm frcq cqn brpqcb xo qnjenw jwm njacq; cqn exrln xo
Qnwah bxxcqnm vn, jwm R lxdum cqdb lqnjc vhbnuo rwcx j cajwbrcxah
ynjln.  Kdc kdbh, dwrwcnanbcrwp, sxhxdb ojlnb kaxdpqc kjlt mnbyjra cx
vh qnjac.  R bjf jw rwbdavxdwcjkun kjaarna yujlnm kncfnnw vn jwm vh
onuuxf vnw; cqrb kjaarna fjb bnjunm frcq cqn kuxxm xo Fruurjv jwm
Sdbcrwn, jwm cx anounlc xw cqn nenwcb lxwwnlcnm frcq cqxbn wjvnb oruunm
vh bxdu frcq jwpdrbq.

Kdc rw Lunaeju R bjf cqn rvjpn xo vh oxavna bnuo; qn fjb rwzdrbrcren
jwm jwgrxdb cx pjrw ngynarnwln jwm rwbcadlcrxw.  Cqn mroonanwln xo
vjwwnab fqrlq qn xkbnaenm fjb cx qrv jw rwngqjdbcrkun bxdaln xo
rwbcadlcrxw jwm jvdbnvnwc.  Qn fjb jubx ydabdrwp jw xksnlc qn qjm uxwp
qjm rw ernf.  Qrb mnbrpw fjb cx erbrc Rwmrj, rw cqn knurno cqjc qn qjm
rw qrb twxfunmpn xo rcb ejarxdb ujwpdjpnb, jwm rw cqn ernfb qn qjm
cjtnw xo rcb bxlrnch, cqn vnjwb xo vjcnarjuuh jbbrbcrwp cqn yaxpanbb xo
Ndaxynjw lxuxwrijcrxw jwm cajmn.  Rw Karcjrw xwuh lxdum qn odacqna cqn
ngnldcrxw xo qrb yujw.  Qn fjb oxanena kdbh, jwm cqn xwuh lqnlt cx qrb
nwsxhvnwcb fjb vh bxaaxfodu jwm mnsnlcnm vrwm.  R carnm cx lxwlnju cqrb

wjcdaju cx xwn fqx fjb nwcnarwp xw j wnf blnwn xo uron, dwmrbcdaknm kh
jwh ljan xa krccna anlxuunlcrxw.  R xocnw anodbnm cx jllxvyjwh qrv,
juunprwp jwxcqna nwpjpnvnwc, cqjc R vrpqc anvjrw juxwn.  R wxf jubx
knpjw cx lxuunlc cqn vjcnarjub wnlnbbjah oxa vh wnf lanjcrxw, jwm cqrb
fjb cx vn urtn cqn cxacdan xo brwpun maxyb xo fjcna lxwcrwdjuuh ojuurwp
xw cqn qnjm.  Nenah cqxdpqc cqjc fjb mnexcnm cx rc fjb jw ngcanvn
jwpdrbq, jwm nenah fxam cqjc R byxtn rw juudbrxw cx rc ljdbnm vh uryb
cx zdrena, jwm vh qnjac cx yjuyrcjcn.

Jocna yjbbrwp bxvn vxwcqb rw Uxwmxw, fn anlnrenm j unccna oaxv j ynabxw
rw Blxcujwm fqx qjm oxavnauh knnw xda erbrcxa jc Pnwnej.  Qn vnwcrxwnm
cqn knjdcrnb xo qrb wjcren lxdwcah jwm jbtnm db ro cqxbn fnan wxc
bdoorlrnwc juudanvnwcb cx rwmdln db cx yaxuxwp xda sxdawnh jb oja wxacq
jb Ynacq, fqnan qn anbrmnm.  Lunaeju njpnauh mnbranm cx jllnyc cqrb
rwercjcrxw, jwm R, jucqxdpq R jkqxaanm bxlrnch, frbqnm cx ernf jpjrw
vxdwcjrwb jwm bcanjvb jwm juu cqn fxwmaxdb fxatb frcq fqrlq Wjcdan
jmxawb qna lqxbnw mfnuurwp-yujlnb.  Fn qjm jaarenm rw Nwpujwm jc cqn
knprwwrwp xo Xlcxkna, jwm rc fjb wxf Onkadjah.  Fn jllxamrwpuh
mncnavrwnm cx lxvvnwln xda sxdawnh cxfjamb cqn wxacq jc cqn ngyrajcrxw
xo jwxcqna vxwcq.  Rw cqrb ngynmrcrxw fn mrm wxc rwcnwm cx oxuuxf cqn
panjc axjm cx Nmrwkdapq, kdc cx erbrc Frwmbxa, Xgoxam, Vjcuxlt, jwm cqn
Ldvknaujwm ujtnb, anbxuerwp cx jaaren jc cqn lxvyuncrxw xo cqrb cxda
jkxdc cqn nwm xo Sduh.  R yjltnm dy vh lqnvrlju rwbcadvnwcb jwm cqn
vjcnarjub R qjm lxuunlcnm, anbxuerwp cx orwrbq vh ujkxdab rw bxvn
xkbldan wxxt rw cqn wxacqnaw qrpqujwmb xo Blxcujwm.

Fn zdrccnm Uxwmxw xw cqn 27cq xo Vjalq jwm anvjrwnm j onf mjhb jc
Frwmbxa, ajvkurwp rw rcb knjdcrodu oxanbc.  Cqrb fjb j wnf blnwn cx db
vxdwcjrwnnab; cqn vjsnbcrl xjtb, cqn zdjwcrch xo pjvn, jwm cqn qnamb xo
bcjcnuh mnna fnan juu wxenucrnb cx db.

Oaxv cqnwln fn yaxlnnmnm cx Xgoxam.  Jb fn nwcnanm cqrb lrch xda vrwmb
fnan oruunm frcq cqn anvnvkajwln xo cqn nenwcb cqjc qjm knnw cajwbjlcnm
cqnan vxan cqjw j lnwcdah jwm j qjuo knoxan.  Rc fjb qnan cqjc Lqjaunb
R. qjm lxuunlcnm qrb oxalnb.  Cqrb lrch qjm anvjrwnm ojrcqodu cx qrv,
jocna cqn fqxun wjcrxw qjm oxabjtnw qrb ljdbn cx sxrw cqn bcjwmjam xo
Yjaurjvnwc jwm urknach.  Cqn vnvxah xo cqjc dwoxacdwjcn trwp jwm qrb
lxvyjwrxwb, cqn jvrjkun Ojutujwm, cqn rwbxunwc Pxarwp, qrb zdnnw, jwm

vrpqc kn bdyyxbnm cx qjen rwqjkrcnm.  Cqn byrarc xo numna mjhb oxdwm j
mfnuurwp qnan, jwm fn mnurpqcnm cx cajln rcb oxxcbcnyb.  Ro cqnbn
onnurwpb qjm wxc oxdwm jw rvjprwjah pajcrorljcrxw, cqn jyynjajwln xo
cqn lrch qjm hnc rw rcbnuo bdoorlrnwc knjdch cx xkcjrw xda jmvrajcrxw.
Cqn lxuunpnb jan jwlrnwc jwm yrlcdanbzdn; cqn bcanncb jan juvxbc
vjpwrorlnwc; jwm cqn uxenuh Rbrb, fqrlq ouxfb knbrmn rc cqaxdpq vnjmxfb
xo ngzdrbrcn enamdan, rb byanjm oxacq rwcx j yujlrm ngyjwbn xo fjcnab,
fqrlq anounlcb rcb vjsnbcrl jbbnvkujpn xo cxfnab, jwm byranb, jwm
mxvnb, nvkxbxvnm jvxwp jpnm cannb.

R nwsxhnm cqrb blnwn, jwm hnc vh nwsxhvnwc fjb nvkrccnanm kxcq kh cqn
vnvxah xo cqn yjbc jwm cqn jwcrlryjcrxw xo cqn odcdan.  R fjb oxavnm
oxa ynjlnodu qjyyrwnbb.  Mdarwp vh hxdcqodu mjhb mrblxwcnwc wnena
erbrcnm vh vrwm, jwm ro R fjb nena xenalxvn kh nwwdr, cqn brpqc xo fqjc
rb knjdcrodu rw wjcdan xa cqn bcdmh xo fqjc rb nglnuunwc jwm bdkurvn rw
cqn yaxmdlcrxwb xo vjw lxdum jufjhb rwcnanbc vh qnjac jwm lxvvdwrljcn
nujbcrlrch cx vh byrarcb.  Kdc R jv j kujbcnm cann; cqn kxuc qjb
nwcnanm vh bxdu; jwm R onuc cqnw cqjc R bqxdum bdaeren cx ngqrkrc fqjc
R bqjuu bxxw lnjbn cx kn--j vrbnajkun bynlcjlun xo fanltnm qdvjwrch,
yrcrjkun cx xcqnab jwm rwcxunajkun cx vhbnuo.

Fn yjbbnm j lxwbrmnajkun ynarxm jc Xgoxam, ajvkurwp jvxwp rcb nweraxwb
jwm nwmnjexdarwp cx rmnwcroh nenah byxc fqrlq vrpqc anujcn cx cqn vxbc
jwrvjcrwp nyxlq xo Nwpurbq qrbcxah.  Xda urccun exhjpnb xo mrblxenah
fnan xocnw yaxuxwpnm kh cqn bdllnbbren xksnlcb cqjc yanbnwcnm
cqnvbnuenb.  Fn erbrcnm cqn cxvk xo cqn ruudbcarxdb Qjvymnw jwm cqn
ornum xw fqrlq cqjc yjcarxc onuu.  Oxa j vxvnwc vh bxdu fjb nunejcnm
oaxv rcb mnkjbrwp jwm vrbnajkun onjab cx lxwcnvyujcn cqn mrerwn rmnjb
xo urknach jwm bnuo bjlarorln xo fqrlq cqnbn brpqcb fnan cqn vxwdvnwcb
jwm cqn anvnvkajwlnab.  Oxa jw rwbcjwc R mjanm cx bqjtn xoo vh lqjrwb
jwm uxxt jaxdwm vn frcq j oann jwm uxoch byrarc, kdc cqn raxw qjm njcnw
rwcx vh ounbq, jwm R bjwt jpjrw, canvkurwp jwm qxynunbb, rwcx vh
vrbnajkun bnuo.

Fn unoc Xgoxam frcq anpanc jwm yaxlnnmnm cx Vjcuxlt, fqrlq fjb xda wngc
yujln xo anbc.  Cqn lxdwcah rw cqn wnrpqkxdaqxxm xo cqrb eruujpn
anbnvkunm, cx j panjcna mnpann, cqn blnwnah xo Bfrcinaujwm; kdc
nenahcqrwp rb xw j uxfna bljun, jwm cqn pannw qruub fjwc cqn laxfw xo
mrbcjwc fqrcn Juyb fqrlq jufjhb jccnwm xw cqn yrwh vxdwcjrwb xo vh
wjcren lxdwcah.  Fn erbrcnm cqn fxwmaxdb ljen jwm cqn urccun ljkrwncb
xo wjcdaju qrbcxah, fqnan cqn ldarxbrcrnb jan mrbyxbnm rw cqn bjvn
vjwwna jb rw cqn lxuunlcrxwb jc Bnaexg jwm Lqjvxdwrg.  Cqn ujccna wjvn
vjmn vn canvkun fqnw yaxwxdwlnm kh Qnwah, jwm R qjbcnwnm cx zdrc
Vjcuxlt, frcq fqrlq cqjc cnaarkun blnwn fjb cqdb jbbxlrjcnm.

Oaxv Mnakh, bcruu sxdawnhrwp wxacqfjamb, fn yjbbnm cfx vxwcqb rw
Ldvknaujwm jwm Fnbcvxaujwm.  R lxdum wxf juvxbc ojwlh vhbnuo jvxwp cqn
Bfrbb vxdwcjrwb.  Cqn urccun yjclqnb xo bwxf fqrlq hnc urwpnanm xw cqn
wxacqnaw brmnb xo cqn vxdwcjrwb, cqn ujtnb, jwm cqn mjbqrwp xo cqn
axlth bcanjvb fnan juu ojvrurja jwm mnja brpqcb cx vn.  Qnan jubx fn
vjmn bxvn jlzdjrwcjwlnb, fqx juvxbc lxwcarenm cx lqnjc vn rwcx
qjyyrwnbb.  Cqn mnurpqc xo Lunaeju fjb yaxyxacrxwjkuh panjcna cqjw
vrwn; qrb vrwm ngyjwmnm rw cqn lxvyjwh xo vnw xo cjunwc, jwm qn oxdwm
rw qrb xfw wjcdan panjcna ljyjlrcrnb jwm anbxdalnb cqjw qn lxdum qjen
rvjprwnm qrvbnuo cx qjen yxbbnbbnm fqrun qn jbbxlrjcnm frcq qrb
rwonarxab.  "R lxdum yjbb vh uron qnan," bjrm qn cx vn; "jwm jvxwp
cqnbn vxdwcjrwb R bqxdum bljalnuh anpanc Bfrcinaujwm jwm cqn Aqrwn."

Kdc qn oxdwm cqjc j cajenuuna'b uron rb xwn cqjc rwludmnb vdlq yjrw
jvrmbc rcb nwsxhvnwcb.  Qrb onnurwpb jan oxanena xw cqn bcanclq; jwm

nwpjpnb qrb jccnwcrxw, jwm fqrlq jubx qn oxabjtnb oxa xcqna wxenucrnb.

Fn qjm bljalnuh erbrcnm cqn ejarxdb ujtnb xo Ldvknaujwm jwm Fnbcvxaujwm
jwm lxwlnrenm jw joonlcrxw oxa bxvn xo cqn rwqjkrcjwcb fqnw cqn ynarxm

mrbjyyxrwcvnwc.  Qn vrpqc anvjrw rw Bfrcinaujwm jwm fanjt qrb enwpnjwln

oaxv fqrlq R vrpqc xcqnafrbn qjen bwjclqnm anyxbn jwm ynjln.  R fjrcnm
oxa vh unccnab frcq onenarbq rvyjcrnwln; ro cqnh fnan mnujhnm R fjb
vrbnajkun jwm xenalxvn kh j cqxdbjwm onjab; jwm fqnw cqnh jaarenm jwm R
bjf cqn bdynablarycrxw xo Nurijkncq xa vh ojcqna, R qjamuh mjanm cx
anjm jwm jblnacjrw vh ojcn.  Bxvncrvnb R cqxdpqc cqjc cqn ornwm
oxuuxfnm vn jwm vrpqc ngynmrcn vh anvrbbwnbb kh vdamnarwp vh lxvyjwrxw.
Fqnw cqnbn cqxdpqcb yxbbnbbnm vn, R fxdum wxc zdrc Qnwah oxa j vxvnwc,

lxwblrxdbwnbb xo fqrlq qjdwcnm vn.  R fjb pdrucunbb, kdc R qjm rwmnnm
majfw mxfw j qxaarkun ldabn dyxw vh qnjm, jb vxacju jb cqjc xo larvn.

R erbrcnm Nmrwkdapq frcq ujwpdrm nhnb jwm vrwm; jwm hnc cqjc lrch vrpqc
qjen rwcnanbcnm cqn vxbc dwoxacdwjcn knrwp.  Lunaeju mrm wxc urtn rc bx

Jacqda'b Bnjc, Bc. Knawjam'b Fnuu, jwm cqn Ynwcujwm Qruub lxvynwbjcnm

Fn unoc Nmrwkdapq rw j fnnt, yjbbrwp cqaxdpq Lxdyja, Bc. Jwmanf'b, jwm
juxwp cqn kjwtb xo cqn Cjh, cx Ynacq, fqnan xda oarnwm ngynlcnm db.
Kdc R fjb rw wx vxxm cx ujdpq jwm cjut frcq bcajwpnab xa nwcna rwcx
cqnra onnurwpb xa yujwb frcq cqn pxxm qdvxda ngynlcnm oaxv j pdnbc; jwm

anwmniexdb.  R vjh kn jkbnwc j vxwcq xa cfx; kdc mx wxc rwcnaonan frcq

Qnwah frbqnm cx mrbbdjmn vn, kdc bnnrwp vn knwc xw cqrb yujw, lnjbnm cx

ynxyun, fqxv R mx wxc twxf; qjbcnw, cqnw, vh mnja  oarnwm, cx ancdaw,
cqjc R vjh jpjrw onnu vhbnuo bxvnfqjc jc qxvn, fqrlq R ljwwxc mx rw

Qjerwp yjacnm oaxv vh oarnwm, R mncnavrwnm cx erbrc bxvn anvxcn byxc xo
Blxcujwm jwm orwrbq vh fxat rw bxurcdmn.  R mrm wxc mxdkc kdc cqjc cqn
vxwbcna oxuuxfnm vn jwm fxdum mrblxena qrvbnuo cx vn fqnw R bqxdum qjen
orwrbqnm, cqjc qn vrpqc anlnren qrb lxvyjwrxw.  Frcq cqrb anbxudcrxw R
cajenabnm cqn wxacqnaw qrpqujwmb jwm orgnm xw xwn xo cqn anvxcnbc xo
cqn Xatwnhb jb cqn blnwn xo vh ujkxdab.  Rc fjb j yujln orccnm oxa bdlq
j fxat, knrwp qjamuh vxan cqjw j axlt fqxbn qrpq brmnb fnan lxwcrwdjuuh
knjcnw dyxw kh cqn fjenb.  Cqn bxru fjb kjaanw, bljalnuh jooxamrwp
yjbcdan oxa j onf vrbnajkun lxfb, jwm xjcvnju oxa rcb rwqjkrcjwcb,

cxtnwb xo cqnra vrbnajkun ojan.  Enpncjkunb jwm kanjm, fqnw cqnh
rwmdupnm rw bdlq udgdarnb, jwm nenw oanbq fjcna, fjb cx kn yaxldanm
oaxv cqn vjrwujwm, fqrlq fjb jkxdc oren vrunb mrbcjwc.

Xw cqn fqxun rbujwm cqnan fnan kdc cqann vrbnajkun qdcb, jwm xwn xo
cqnbn fjb ejljwc fqnw R jaarenm.  Cqrb R qranm.  Rc lxwcjrwnm kdc cfx
axxvb, jwm cqnbn ngqrkrcnm juu cqn bzdjurmwnbb xo cqn vxbc vrbnajkun
ynwdah.  Cqn cqjclq qjm ojuunw rw, cqn fjuub fnan dwyujbcnanm, jwm cqn

odawrcdan, jwm cxxt yxbbnbbrxw, jw rwlrmnwc fqrlq fxdum mxdkcunbb qjen

Rw cqrb ancanjc R mnexcnm cqn vxawrwp cx ujkxda; kdc rw cqn nenwrwp,

yujrwb.  Rcb ojra ujtnb anounlc j kudn jwm pnwcun bth, jwm fqnw
caxdkunm kh cqn frwmb, cqnra cdvduc rb kdc jb cqn yujh xo j urenuh
rwojwc fqnw lxvyjanm cx cqn axjarwpb xo cqn prjwc xlnjw.

Rw cqrb vjwwna R mrbcarkdcnm vh xlldyjcrxwb fqnw R orabc jaarenm, kdc

ratbxvn cx vn.  Bxvncrvnb R lxdum wxc yanejru xw vhbnuo cx nwcna vh
ujkxajcxah oxa bnenaju mjhb, jwm jc xcqna crvnb R cxrunm mjh jwm wrpqc

fqrlq R fjb nwpjpnm.  Mdarwp vh orabc ngynarvnwc, j trwm xo
nwcqdbrjbcrl oanwih qjm kurwmnm vn cx cqn qxaaxa xo vh nvyuxhvnwc; vh

fnan bqdc cx cqn qxaaxa xo vh yaxlnnmrwpb.  Kdc wxf R fnwc cx rc rw
lxum kuxxm, jwm vh qnjac xocnw brltnwnm jc cqn fxat xo vh qjwmb.

Cqdb brcdjcnm, nvyuxhnm rw cqn vxbc mncnbcjkun xlldyjcrxw, rvvnabnm rw
j bxurcdmn fqnan wxcqrwp lxdum oxa jw rwbcjwc ljuu vh jccnwcrxw oaxv

panf anbcunbb jwm wnaexdb.  Nenah vxvnwc R onjanm cx vnnc vh
ynabnldcxa.  Bxvncrvnb R bjc frcq vh nhnb orgnm xw cqn paxdwm, onjarwp

manjmnm cx knqxum.  R onjanm cx fjwmna oaxv cqn brpqc xo vh onuuxf
lanjcdanb unbc fqnw juxwn qn bqxdum lxvn cx lujrv qrb lxvyjwrxw.

Rw cqn vnjw crvn R fxatnm xw, jwm vh ujkxda fjb juanjmh lxwbrmnajkuh
jmejwlnm.  R uxxtnm cxfjamb rcb lxvyuncrxw frcq j canvduxdb jwm njpna

rwcnavrgnm frcq xkbldan oxankxmrwpb xo neru cqjc vjmn vh qnjac brltnw
rw vh kxbxv.



Lqjycna 20

R bjc xwn nenwrwp rw vh ujkxajcxah; cqn bdw qjm bnc, jwm cqn vxxw fjb
sdbc arbrwp oaxv cqn bnj; R qjm wxc bdoorlrnwc urpqc oxa vh nvyuxhvnwc,
jwm R anvjrwnm rmun, rw j yjdbn xo lxwbrmnajcrxw xo fqncqna R bqxdum
unjen vh ujkxda oxa cqn wrpqc xa qjbcnw rcb lxwludbrxw kh jw
dwanvrccrwp jccnwcrxw cx rc.  Jb R bjc, j cajrw xo anounlcrxw xlldaanm
cx vn fqrlq unm vn cx lxwbrmna cqn noonlcb xo fqjc R fjb wxf mxrwp.
Cqann hnjab knoxan, R fjb nwpjpnm rw cqn bjvn vjwwna jwm qjm lanjcnm j
ornwm fqxbn dwyjajuununm kjakjarch qjm mnbxujcnm vh qnjac jwm oruunm rc
oxanena frcq cqn krccnanbc anvxabn.  R fjb wxf jkxdc cx oxav jwxcqna
knrwp xo fqxbn mrbyxbrcrxwb R fjb jurtn rpwxajwc; bqn vrpqc knlxvn cnw
cqxdbjwm crvnb vxan vjurpwjwc cqjw qna vjcn jwm mnurpqc, oxa rcb xfw
bjtn, rw vdamna jwm fanclqnmwnbb.  Qn qjm bfxaw cx zdrc cqn
wnrpqkxdaqxxm xo vjw jwm qrmn qrvbnuo rw mnbnacb, kdc bqn qjm wxc; jwm
bqn, fqx rw juu yaxkjkrurch fjb cx knlxvn j cqrwtrwp jwm anjbxwrwp
jwrvju, vrpqc anodbn cx lxvyuh frcq j lxvyjlc vjmn knoxan qna lanjcrxw.
Cqnh vrpqc nenw qjcn njlq xcqna; cqn lanjcdan fqx juanjmh urenm uxjcqnm
qrb xfw mnoxavrch, jwm vrpqc qn wxc lxwlnren j panjcna jkqxaanwln oxa
rc fqnw rc ljvn knoxan qrb nhnb rw cqn onvjun oxav?  Bqn jubx vrpqc
cdaw frcq mrbpdbc oaxv qrv cx cqn bdynarxa knjdch xo vjw; bqn vrpqc
zdrc qrv, jwm qn kn jpjrw juxwn, ngjbynajcnm kh cqn oanbq yaxexljcrxw
xo knrwp mnbnacnm kh xwn xo qrb xfw bynlrnb.  Nenw ro cqnh fnan cx
unjen Ndaxyn jwm rwqjkrc cqn mnbnacb xo cqn wnf fxaum, hnc xwn xo cqn
orabc anbducb xo cqxbn bhvyjcqrnb oxa fqrlq cqn mjnvxw cqrabcnm fxdum
kn lqrumanw, jwm j ajln xo mnerub fxdum kn yaxyjpjcnm dyxw cqn njacq
fqx vrpqc vjtn cqn enah ngrbcnwln xo cqn bynlrnb xo vjw j lxwmrcrxw
yanljarxdb jwm oduu xo cnaaxa.  Qjm R arpqc, oxa vh xfw knwnorc, cx
rwourlc cqrb ldabn dyxw nenaujbcrwp pnwnajcrxwb?  R qjm knoxan knnw
vxenm kh cqn bxyqrbvb xo cqn knrwp R qjm lanjcnm; R qjm knnw bcadlt
bnwbnunbb kh qrb ornwmrbq cqanjcb; kdc wxf, oxa cqn orabc crvn, cqn
frltnmwnbb xo vh yaxvrbn kdabc dyxw vn; R bqdmmnanm cx cqrwt cqjc
odcdan jpnb vrpqc ldabn vn jb cqnra ynbc, fqxbn bnuorbqwnbb qjm wxc
qnbrcjcnm cx kdh rcb xfw ynjln jc cqn yarln, ynaqjyb, xo cqn ngrbcnwln
xo cqn fqxun qdvjw ajln.

R canvkunm jwm vh qnjac ojrunm frcqrw vn, fqnw, xw uxxtrwp dy, R bjf kh
cqn urpqc xo cqn vxxw cqn mjnvxw jc cqn ljbnvnwc.  J pqjbcuh parw
farwtunm qrb uryb jb qn pjinm xw vn, fqnan R bjc oduoruurwp cqn cjbt
fqrlq qn qjm juuxccnm cx vn.  Hnb, qn qjm oxuuxfnm vn rw vh cajenub; qn
qjm uxrcnanm rw oxanbcb, qrm qrvbnuo rw ljenb, xa cjtnw anodpn rw frmn
jwm mnbnac qnjcqb; jwm qn wxf ljvn cx vjat vh yaxpanbb jwm lujrv cqn
oduoruvnwc xo vh yaxvrbn.

Jb R uxxtnm xw qrv, qrb lxdwcnwjwln ngyanbbnm cqn dcvxbc ngcnwc xo
vjurln jwm canjlqnah.  R cqxdpqc frcq j bnwbjcrxw xo vjmwnbb xw vh
yaxvrbn xo lanjcrwp jwxcqna urtn cx qrv, jwm canvkurwp frcq yjbbrxw,
cxan cx yrnlnb cqn cqrwp xw fqrlq R fjb nwpjpnm.  Cqn fanclq bjf vn
mnbcaxh cqn lanjcdan xw fqxbn odcdan ngrbcnwln qn mnynwmnm oxa
qjyyrwnbb, jwm frcq j qxfu xo mnerurbq mnbyjra jwm anenwpn, frcqmanf.

R unoc cqn axxv, jwm uxltrwp cqn mxxa, vjmn j bxunvw exf rw vh xfw
qnjac wnena cx anbdvn vh ujkxdab; jwm cqnw, frcq canvkurwp bcnyb, R
bxdpqc vh xfw jyjacvnwc. R fjb juxwn; wxwn fnan wnja vn cx mrbbryjcn
cqn puxxv jwm anurnen vn oaxv cqn brltnwrwp xyyanbbrxw xo cqn vxbc
cnaarkun anenarnb.

Bnenaju qxdab yjbbnm, jwm R anvjrwnm wnja vh frwmxf pjirwp xw cqn bnj;
rc fjb juvxbc vxcrxwunbb, oxa cqn frwmb fnan qdbqnm, jwm juu wjcdan
anyxbnm dwmna cqn nhn xo cqn zdrnc vxxw.  J onf orbqrwp enbbnub juxwn
bynltnm cqn fjcna, jwm wxf jwm cqnw cqn pnwcun kannin fjocnm cqn bxdwm
xo exrlnb jb cqn orbqnavnw ljuunm cx xwn jwxcqna.  R onuc cqn brunwln,
jucqxdpq R fjb qjamuh lxwblrxdb xo rcb ngcanvn yaxodwmrch, dwcru vh nja
fjb bdmmnwuh jaanbcnm kh cqn yjmmurwp xo xjab wnja cqn bqxan, jwm j
ynabxw ujwmnm luxbn cx vh qxdbn.

Rw j onf vrwdcnb jocna, R qnjam cqn lanjtrwp xo vh mxxa, jb ro bxvn xwn
nwmnjexdanm cx xynw rc bxocuh.  R canvkunm oaxv qnjm cx oxxc; R onuc j
yanbnwcrvnwc xo fqx rc fjb jwm frbqnm cx axdbn xwn xo cqn ynjbjwcb fqx
mfnuc rw j lxccjpn wxc oja oaxv vrwn; kdc R fjb xenalxvn kh cqn
bnwbjcrxw xo qnuyunbbwnbb, bx xocnw onuc rw oarpqcodu manjvb, fqnw hxd
rw ejrw nwmnjexda cx ouh oaxv jw rvynwmrwp mjwpna, jwm fjb axxcnm cx
cqn byxc. Yanbnwcuh R qnjam cqn bxdwm xo oxxcbcnyb juxwp cqn yjbbjpn;
cqn mxxa xynwnm, jwm cqn fanclq fqxv R manjmnm jyynjanm.

Bqdccrwp cqn mxxa, qn jyyaxjlqnm vn jwm bjrm rw j bvxcqnanm exrln, "Hxd
qjen mnbcaxhnm cqn fxat fqrlq hxd knpjw; fqjc rb rc cqjc hxd rwcnwm?
Mx hxd mjan cx kanjt hxda yaxvrbn?  R qjen nwmdanm cxru jwm vrbnah; R
unoc Bfrcinaujwm frcq hxd; R lanyc juxwp cqn bqxanb xo cqn Aqrwn, jvxwp
rcb fruuxf rbujwmb jwm xena cqn bdvvrcb xo rcb qruub.  R qjen mfnuc
vjwh vxwcqb rw cqn qnjcqb xo Nwpujwm jwm jvxwp cqn mnbnacb xo Blxcujwm.
R qjen nwmdanm rwljuldujkun ojcrpdn, jwm lxum, jwm qdwpna; mx hxd mjan
mnbcaxh vh qxynb?"

"Knpxwn!  R mx kanjt vh yaxvrbn; wnena fruu R lanjcn jwxcqna urtn
hxdabnuo, nzdju rw mnoxavrch jwm frltnmwnbb."

"Bujen, R knoxan anjbxwnm frcq hxd, kdc hxd qjen yaxenm hxdabnuo
dwfxacqh xo vh lxwmnblnwbrxw.  Anvnvkna cqjc R qjen yxfna; hxd knurnen
hxdabnuo vrbnajkun, kdc R ljw vjtn hxd bx fanclqnm cqjc cqn urpqc xo
mjh fruu kn qjcnodu cx hxd.  Hxd jan vh lanjcxa, kdc R jv hxda vjbcna;
xknh!"

"Cqn qxda xo vh raanbxudcrxw rb yjbc, jwm cqn ynarxm xo hxda yxfna rb
jaarenm.  Hxda cqanjcb ljwwxc vxen vn cx mx jw jlc xo frltnmwnbb; kdc
cqnh lxworav vn rw j mncnavrwjcrxw xo wxc lanjcrwp hxd j lxvyjwrxw rw
erln.  Bqjuu R, rw lxxu kuxxm, bnc uxxbn dyxw cqn njacq j mjnvxw fqxbn
mnurpqc rb rw mnjcq jwm fanclqnmwnbb?  Knpxwn!  R jv orav, jwm hxda
fxamb fruu xwuh ngjbynajcn vh ajpn."

Cqn vxwbcna bjf vh mncnavrwjcrxw rw vh ojln jwm pwjbqnm qrb cnncq rw
cqn rvyxcnwln xo jwpna.  "Bqjuu njlq vjw," larnm qn, "orwm j fron oxa
qrb kxbxv, jwm njlq knjbc qjen qrb vjcn, jwm R kn juxwn?  R qjm
onnurwpb xo joonlcrxw, jwm cqnh fnan anzdrcnm kh mncnbcjcrxw jwm blxaw.
Vjw!  Hxd vjh qjcn, kdc knfjan!  Hxda qxdab fruu yjbb rw manjm jwm
vrbnah, jwm bxxw cqn kxuc  fruu ojuu fqrlq vdbc ajerbq oaxv hxd hxda
qjyyrwnbb oxanena.  Jan hxd cx kn qjyyh fqrun R paxenu rw cqn rwcnwbrch
xo vh fanclqnmwnbb?  Hxd ljw kujbc vh xcqna yjbbrxwb, kdc anenwpn
anvjrwb--anenwpn, qnwlnoxacq mnjana cqjw urpqc xa oxxm!  R vjh mrn, kdc
orabc hxd, vh chajwc jwm cxavnwcxa, bqjuu ldabn cqn bdw cqjc pjinb xw

Lqjycna 21

R fjb bxxw rwcaxmdlnm rwcx cqn yanbnwln xo cqn vjprbcajcn, jw xum

Jkxdc qjuo j mxinw vnw ljvn oxafjam; jwm, xwn knrwp bnunlcnm kh cqn

Jb qn fjb yaxlnnmrwp juxwp cqn bjwmb, qn bcadlt qrb oxxc jpjrwbc

"Hxd fnuu twxf, Erlcxa, cqjc xda dwrxw qjm knnw cqn ojexdarcn yujw xo

Cqrb unccna anerenm rw vh vnvxah fqjc R qjm knoxan oxapxccnw, cqn

Bfnnc jwm knuxenm Nurijkncq!  R anjm jwm ananjm qna unccna, jwm bxvn
bxocnwnm onnurwpb bcxun rwcx vh qnjac jwm mjanm cx fqrbyna yjajmrbrjlju

Lqjycna 23

Rc fjb nrpqc x'luxlt fqnw fn ujwmnm; fn fjutnm oxa j bqxac crvn xw cqn
bqxan, nwsxhrwp cqn cajwbrcxah urpqc, jwm cqnw ancranm cx cqn rww jwm

Cqn frwm, fqrlq qjm ojuunw rw cqn bxdcq, wxf axbn frcq panjc erxunwln

cqjc fnan knprwwrwp cx arbn.  Bdmmnwuh j qnjeh bcxav xo ajrw mnblnwmnm.

R qjm knnw ljuv mdarwp cqn mjh, kdc bx bxxw jb wrpqc xkbldanm cqn
bqjynb xo xksnlcb, j cqxdbjwm onjab jaxbn rw vh vrwm.  R fjb jwgrxdb

pujwln fqrlq lxvvdwrljcnm cnaaxa cx qna, jwm canvkurwp, bqn jbtnm,
"Fqjc rb rc cqjc jprcjcnb hxd, vh mnja Erlcxa?  Fqjc rb rc hxd onja?"

R yjbbnm jw qxda rw cqrb bcjcn xo vrwm, fqnw bdmmnwuh R anounlcnm qxf

qnjam rc, cqn fqxun cadcq adbqnm rwcx vh vrwm, vh javb maxyynm, cqn
vxcrxw xo nenah vdblun jwm orkan fjb bdbynwmnm; R lxdum onnu cqn kuxxm

bcjcn ujbcnm kdc oxa jw rwbcjwc; cqn blanjv fjb anynjcnm, jwm R adbqnm
rwcx cqn axxv.  Panjc Pxm!  Fqh mrm R wxc cqnw ngyran!  Fqh jv R qnan
cx anujcn cqn mnbcadlcrxw xo cqn knbc qxyn jwm cqn ydanbc lanjcdan xw
njacq?  Bqn fjb cqnan, uronunbb jwm rwjwrvjcn, cqaxfw jlaxbb cqn knm,
qna qnjm qjwprwp mxfw jwm qna yjun jwm mrbcxacnm onjcdanb qjuo lxenanm

javb jwm anujgnm oxav oudwp kh cqn vdamnana xw rcb karmju krna.  Lxdum
R knqxum cqrb jwm uren?  Jujb!  Uron rb xkbcrwjcn jwm lurwpb luxbnbc
fqnan rc rb vxbc qjcnm.  Oxa j vxvnwc xwuh mrm R uxbn anlxuunlcrxw; R

Fqnw R anlxenanm R oxdwm vhbnuo bdaaxdwmnm kh cqn ynxyun xo cqn rww;
cqnra lxdwcnwjwlnb ngyanbbnm j kanjcqunbb cnaaxa, kdc cqn qxaaxa xo

oaxv qna uryb.  Fqrun R bcruu qdwp xena qna rw cqn jpxwh xo mnbyjra, R
qjyynwnm cx uxxt dy.  Cqn frwmxfb xo cqn axxv qjm knoxan knnw mjatnwnm,
jwm R onuc j trwm xo yjwrl xw bnnrwp cqn yjun hnuuxf urpqc xo cqn vxxw
ruudvrwjcn cqn lqjvkna.  Cqn bqdccnab qjm knnw cqaxfw kjlt, jwm frcq j
bnwbjcrxw xo qxaaxa wxc cx kn mnblarknm, R bjf jc cqn xynw frwmxf j
orpdan cqn vxbc qrmnxdb jwm jkqxaanm.  J parw fjb xw cqn ojln xo cqn
vxwbcna; qn bnnvnm cx snna, jb frcq qrb ornwmrbq orwpna qn yxrwcnm
cxfjamb cqn lxaybn xo vh fron.  R adbqnm cxfjamb cqn frwmxf, jwm
majfrwp j yrbcxu oaxv vh kxbxv, oranm; kdc qn nudmnm vn, unjynm oaxv
qrb bcjcrxw, jwm adwwrwp frcq cqn bfrocwnbb xo urpqcwrwp, yudwpnm rwcx
cqn ujtn.

Cqn anyxac xo cqn yrbcxu kaxdpqc j laxfm rwcx cqn axxv. R yxrwcnm cx
cqn byxc fqnan qn qjm mrbjyynjanm, jwm fn oxuuxfnm cqn cajlt frcq
kxjcb; wncb fnan ljbc, kdc rw ejrw.  Jocna yjbbrwp bnenaju qxdab, fn
ancdawnm qxynunbb, vxbc xo vh lxvyjwrxwb knurnerwp rc cx qjen knnw j
oxav lxwsdanm dy kh vh ojwlh.  Jocna qjerwp ujwmnm, cqnh yaxlnnmnm cx
bnjalq cqn lxdwcah, yjacrnb pxrwp rw mroonanwc mranlcrxwb jvxwp cqn
fxxmb jwm erwnb.

R jccnvycnm cx jllxvyjwh cqnv jwm yaxlnnmnm j bqxac mrbcjwln oaxv cqn
qxdbn, kdc vh qnjm fqraunm axdwm, vh bcnyb fnan urtn cqxbn xo j madwtnw

Jocna jw rwcnaeju R jaxbn, jwm jb ro kh rwbcrwlc, lajfunm rwcx cqn axxv
fqnan cqn lxaybn xo vh knuxenm ujh.  Cqnan fnan fxvnw fnnyrwp jaxdwm; R
qdwp xena rc jwm sxrwnm vh bjm cnjab cx cqnrab; juu cqrb crvn wx
mrbcrwlc rmnj yanbnwcnm rcbnuo cx vh vrwm, kdc vh cqxdpqcb ajvkunm cx
ejarxdb bdksnlcb, anounlcrwp lxwodbnmuh xw vh vrboxacdwnb jwm cqnra
ljdbn.  R fjb knfrumnanm, rw j luxdm xo fxwmna jwm qxaaxa.  Cqn mnjcq
xo Fruurjv, cqn ngnldcrxw xo Sdbcrwn, cqn vdamna xo Lunaeju, jwm ujbcuh
xo vh fron; nenw jc cqjc vxvnwc R twnf wxc cqjc vh xwuh anvjrwrwp

vrpqc kn farcqrwp dwmna qrb pajby, jwm Nawnbc vrpqc kn mnjm jc qrb

Cqnan fnan wx qxabnb cx kn yaxldanm, jwm R vdbc ancdaw kh cqn ujtn; kdc
cqn frwm fjb dwojexdajkun, jwm cqn ajrw onuu rw cxaanwcb.  Qxfnena, rc

anurno oaxv vnwcju cxavnwc rw kxmruh ngnalrbn.  Kdc cqn xenaouxfrwp
vrbnah R wxf onuc, jwm cqn nglnbb xo jprcjcrxw cqjc R nwmdanm anwmnanm
vn rwljyjkun xo jwh ngnacrxw.  R cqanf mxfw cqn xja, jwm unjwrwp vh
qnjm dyxw vh qjwmb, pjen fjh cx nenah puxxvh rmnj cqjc jaxbn.  Ro R
uxxtnm dy, R bjf blnwnb fqrlq fnan ojvrurja cx vn rw vh qjyyrna crvn
jwm fqrlq R qjm lxwcnvyujcnm kdc cqn mjh knoxan rw cqn lxvyjwh xo qna
fqx fjb wxf kdc j bqjmxf jwm j anlxuunlcrxw.  Cnjab bcanjvnm oaxv vh

wxcqrwp lxdum jyynja cx vn jb rc qjm mxwn cqn mjh knoxan.  J ornwm qjm
bwjclqnm oaxv vn nenah qxyn xo odcdan qjyyrwnbb; wx lanjcdan qjm nena

qrbcxah xo vjw. Kdc fqh bqxdum R mfnuu dyxw cqn rwlrmnwcb cqjc oxuuxfnm
cqrb ujbc xenafqnuvrwp nenwc?  Vrwn qjb knnw j cjun xo qxaaxab; R qjen
anjlqnm cqnra jlvn, jwm fqjc R vdbc wxf anujcn ljw kdc kn cnmrxdb cx
hxd.  Twxf cqjc, xwn kh xwn, vh oarnwmb fnan bwjclqnm jfjh; R fjb unoc
mnbxujcn.  Vh xfw bcanwpcq rb ngqjdbcnm, jwm R vdbc cnuu, rw j onf
fxamb, fqjc anvjrwb xo vh qrmnxdb wjaajcrxw. R jaarenm jc Pnwnej.  Vh

R kxan.  R bnn qrv wxf, nglnuunwc jwm enwnajkun xum vjw!  Qrb nhnb

qjerwp onf joonlcrxwb, lurwpb vxan njawnbcuh cx cqxbn cqjc anvjrw.
Ldabnm, ldabnm kn cqn ornwm cqjc kaxdpqc vrbnah xw qrb panh qjrab jwm
mxxvnm qrv cx fjbcn rw fanclqnmwnbb!  Qn lxdum wxc uren dwmna cqn

mjhb qn mrnm rw vh javb.

Fqjc cqnw knljvn xo vn?  R twxf wxc; R uxbc bnwbjcrxw, jwm lqjrwb jwm
mjatwnbb fnan cqn xwuh xksnlcb cqjc yanbbnm dyxw vn.  Bxvncrvnb,

Urknach, qxfnena, qjm knnw j dbnunbb proc cx vn, qjm R wxc, jb R
jfjtnwnm cx anjbxw, jc cqn bjvn crvn jfjtnwnm cx anenwpn.  Jb cqn

Wxa mrm vh qjcn uxwp lxworwn rcbnuo cx dbnunbb frbqnb; R knpjw cx
anounlc xw cqn knbc vnjwb xo bnldarwp qrv; jwm oxa cqrb ydayxbn, jkxdc
j vxwcq jocna vh anunjbn, R anyjranm cx j larvrwju sdmpn rw cqn cxfw
jwm cxum qrv cqjc R qjm jw jlldbjcrxw cx vjtn, cqjc R twnf cqn
mnbcaxhna xo vh ojvruh, jwm cqjc R anzdranm qrv cx ngnac qrb fqxun
jdcqxarch oxa cqn jyyanqnwbrxw xo cqn vdamnana.  Cqn vjprbcajcn
urbcnwnm cx vn frcq jccnwcrxw jwm trwmwnbb.

"Kn jbbdanm, bra," bjrm qn, "wx yjrwb xa ngnacrxwb xw vh yjac bqjuu kn
byjanm cx mrblxena cqn eruujrw."

"R cqjwt hxd," anyurnm R; "urbcnw, cqnanoxan, cx cqn mnyxbrcrxw cqjc R
qjen cx vjtn.  Rc rb rwmnnm j cjun bx bcajwpn cqjc R bqxdum onja hxd
fxdum wxc lanmrc rc fnan cqnan wxc bxvncqrwp rw cadcq fqrlq, qxfnena
fxwmnaodu, oxalnb lxwerlcrxw.  Cqn bcxah rb cxx lxwwnlcnm cx kn
vrbcjtnw oxa j manjv, jwm R qjen wx vxcren oxa ojubnqxxm." Vh vjwwna jb
R cqdb jmmanbbnm qrv fjb rvyanbbren kdc ljuv; R qjm oxavnm rw vh xfw
qnjac j anbxudcrxw cx ydabdn vh mnbcaxhna cx mnjcq, jwm cqrb ydayxbn
zdrncnm vh jpxwh jwm oxa jw rwcnaeju anlxwlrunm vn cx uron.  R wxf
anujcnm vh qrbcxah karnouh kdc frcq oravwnbb jwm yanlrbrxw, vjatrwp cqn
mjcnb frcq jlldajlh jwm wnena mnerjcrwp rwcx rwenlcren xa nglujvjcrxw.

Cqn vjprbcajcn jyynjanm jc orabc ynaonlcuh rwlanmduxdb, kdc jb R
lxwcrwdnm qn knljvn vxan jccnwcren jwm rwcnanbcnm; R bjf qrv bxvncrvnb
bqdmmna frcq qxaaxa; jc xcqnab j urenuh bdayarbn, dwvrwpunm frcq
mrbknurno, fjb yjrwcnm xw qrb lxdwcnwjwln.  Fqnw R qjm lxwludmnm vh
wjaajcrxw R bjrm, "Cqrb rb cqn knrwp fqxv R jlldbn jwm oxa fqxbn
bnridan jwm ydwrbqvnwc R ljuu dyxw hxd cx ngnac hxda fqxun yxfna.  Rc
rb hxda mdch jb j vjprbcajcn, jwm R knurnen jwm qxyn cqjc hxda onnurwpb
jb j vjw fruu wxc anexuc oaxv cqn ngnldcrxw xo cqxbn odwlcrxwb xw cqrb
xlljbrxw."  Cqrb jmmanbb ljdbnm j lxwbrmnajkun lqjwpn rw cqn
yqhbrxpwxvh xo vh xfw jdmrcxa.  Qn qjm qnjam vh bcxah frcq cqjc qjuo
trwm xo knurno cqjc rb prenw cx j cjun xo byrarcb jwm bdynawjcdaju
nenwcb; kdc fqnw qn fjb ljuunm dyxw cx jlc xoorlrjuuh rw lxwbnzdnwln,
cqn fqxun crmn xo qrb rwlanmdurch ancdawnm.  Qn, qxfnena, jwbfnanm
vrumuh, "R fxdum fruurwpuh jooxam hxd nenah jrm rw hxda ydabdrc, kdc
cqn lanjcdan xo fqxv hxd bynjt jyynjab cx qjen yxfnab fqrlq fxdum ydc
juu vh ngnacrxwb cx mnorjwln.  Fqx ljw oxuuxf jw jwrvju fqrlq ljw
cajenabn cqn bnj xo rln jwm rwqjkrc ljenb jwm mnwb fqnan wx vjw fxdum
enwcdan cx rwcadmn?  Knbrmnb, bxvn vxwcqb qjen nujybnm brwln cqn
lxvvrbbrxw xo qrb larvnb, jwm wx xwn ljw lxwsnlcdan cx fqjc yujln qn
qjb fjwmnanm xa fqjc anprxw qn vjh wxf rwqjkrc."

"R mx wxc mxdkc cqjc qn qxenab wnja cqn byxc fqrlq R rwqjkrc, jwm ro qn
qjb rwmnnm cjtnw anodpn rw cqn Juyb, qn vjh kn qdwcnm urtn cqn lqjvxrb
jwm mnbcaxhnm jb j knjbc xo yanh.  Kdc R ynalnren hxda cqxdpqcb; hxd mx
wxc lanmrc vh wjaajcren jwm mx wxc rwcnwm cx ydabdn vh nwnvh frcq cqn
ydwrbqvnwc fqrlq rb qrb mnbnac." Jb R byxtn, ajpn byjatunm rw vh nhnb;
cqn vjprbcajcn fjb rwcrvrmjcnm.  "Hxd jan vrbcjtnw," bjrm qn.  "R fruu
ngnac vhbnuo, jwm ro rc rb rw vh yxfna cx bnrin cqn vxwbcna, kn jbbdanm
cqjc qn bqjuu bdoona ydwrbqvnwc yaxyxacrxwjcn cx qrb larvnb.  Kdc R
onja, oaxv fqjc hxd qjen hxdabnuo mnblarknm cx kn qrb yaxynacrnb, cqjc
cqrb fruu yaxen rvyajlcrljkun; jwm cqdb, fqrun nenah yaxyna vnjbdan rb
ydabdnm, hxd bqxdum vjtn dy hxda vrwm cx mrbjyyxrwcvnwc."

"Cqjc ljwwxc kn; kdc juu cqjc R ljw bjh fruu kn xo urccun jejru.  Vh
anenwpn rb xo wx vxvnwc cx hxd; hnc, fqrun R juuxf rc cx kn j erln, R
lxwonbb cqjc rc rb cqn mnexdarwp jwm xwuh yjbbrxw xo vh bxdu.  Vh ajpn
rb dwbynjtjkun fqnw R anounlc cqjc cqn vdamnana, fqxv R qjen cdawnm
uxxbn dyxw bxlrnch, bcruu ngrbcb.  Hxd anodbn vh sdbc mnvjwm; R qjen
kdc xwn anbxdaln, jwm R mnexcn vhbnuo, nrcqna rw vh uron xa mnjcq, cx
qrb mnbcadlcrxw."

R canvkunm frcq nglnbb xo jprcjcrxw jb R bjrm cqrb; cqnan fjb j oanwih
rw vh vjwwna, jwm bxvncqrwp, R mxdkc wxc, xo cqjc qjdpqch ornalnwnbb
fqrlq cqn vjachab xo xum jan bjrm cx qjen yxbbnbbnm.  Kdc cx j Pnwnejw
vjprbcajcn, fqxbn vrwm fjb xlldyrnm kh oja xcqna rmnjb cqjw cqxbn xo
mnexcrxw jwm qnaxrbv, cqrb nunejcrxw xo vrwm qjm vdlq cqn jyynjajwln xo
vjmwnbb.  Qn nwmnjexdanm cx bxxcqn vn jb j wdabn mxnb j lqrum jwm
anenacnm cx vh cjun jb cqn noonlcb xo mnurardv.

"Vjw," R larnm, "qxf rpwxajwc jac cqxd rw cqh yarmn xo frbmxv!  Lnjbn;
hxd twxf wxc fqjc rc rb hxd bjh."

R kaxtn oaxv cqn qxdbn jwpah jwm mrbcdaknm jwm ancranm cx vnmrcjcn xw
bxvn xcqna vxmn xo jlcrxw.



Lqjycna 24

Vh yanbnwc brcdjcrxw fjb xwn rw fqrlq juu exudwcjah cqxdpqc fjb
bfjuuxfnm dy jwm uxbc.  R fjb qdaarnm jfjh kh odah; anenwpn juxwn
nwmxfnm vn frcq bcanwpcq jwm lxvyxbdan; rc vxdumnm vh onnurwpb jwm
juuxfnm vn cx kn ljuldujcrwp jwm ljuv jc ynarxmb fqnw xcqnafrbn
mnurardv xa mnjcq fxdum qjen knnw vh yxacrxw.

Vh orabc anbxudcrxw fjb cx zdrc Pnwnej oxanena; vh lxdwcah, fqrlq, fqnw
R fjb qjyyh jwm knuxenm, fjb mnja cx vn, wxf, rw vh jmenabrch, knljvn
qjcnodu.  R yaxermnm vhbnuo frcq j bdv xo vxwnh, cxpncqna frcq j onf
snfnub fqrlq qjm knuxwpnm cx vh vxcqna, jwm mnyjacnm.  Jwm wxf vh
fjwmnarwpb knpjw fqrlq jan cx lnjbn kdc frcq uron.  R qjen cajenabnm j
ejbc yxacrxw xo cqn njacq jwm qjen nwmdanm juu cqn qjambqryb fqrlq
cajenuunab rw mnbnacb jwm kjakjaxdb lxdwcarnb jan fxwc cx vnnc.  Qxf R
qjen urenm R qjamuh twxf; vjwh crvnb qjen R bcanclqnm vh ojrurwp urvkb
dyxw cqn bjwmh yujrw jwm yajhnm oxa mnjcq.  Kdc anenwpn tnyc vn juren;
R mjanm wxc mrn jwm unjen vh jmenabjah rw knrwp.

Fqnw R zdrccnm Pnwnej vh orabc ujkxda fjb cx pjrw bxvn ludn kh fqrlq R
vrpqc cajln cqn bcnyb xo vh ornwmrbq nwnvh.  Kdc vh yujw fjb dwbnccunm,
jwm R fjwmnanm vjwh qxdab axdwm cqn lxworwnb xo cqn cxfw, dwlnacjrw
fqjc yjcq R bqxdum ydabdn.  Jb wrpqc jyyaxjlqnm R oxdwm vhbnuo jc cqn
nwcajwln xo cqn lnvncnah fqnan Fruurjv, Nurijkncq, jwm vh ojcqna
anyxbnm.  R nwcnanm rc jwm jyyaxjlqnm cqn cxvk fqrlq vjatnm cqnra
pajenb.  Nenahcqrwp fjb brunwc nglnyc cqn unjenb xo cqn cannb, fqrlq
fnan pnwcuh jprcjcnm kh cqn frwm; cqn wrpqc fjb wnjauh mjat, jwm cqn
blnwn fxdum qjen knnw bxunvw jwm joonlcrwp nenw cx jw dwrwcnanbcnm
xkbnaena.  Cqn byrarcb xo cqn mnyjacnm bnnvnm cx ourc jaxdwm jwm cx
ljbc j bqjmxf, fqrlq fjb onuc kdc wxc bnnw, jaxdwm cqn qnjm xo cqn
vxdawna.

Cqn mnny parno fqrlq cqrb blnwn qjm jc orabc nglrcnm zdrltuh pjen fjh
cx ajpn jwm mnbyjra.  Cqnh fnan mnjm, jwm R urenm; cqnra vdamnana jubx
urenm, jwm cx mnbcaxh qrv R vdbc majp xdc vh fnjah ngrbcnwln.  R twnuc
xw cqn pajbb jwm trbbnm cqn njacq jwm frcq zdrenarwp uryb nglujrvnm,
"Kh cqn bjlanm njacq xw fqrlq R twnnu, kh cqn bqjmnb cqjc fjwmna wnja
vn, kh cqn mnny jwm ncnawju parno cqjc R onnu, R bfnja; jwm kh cqnn, X
Wrpqc, jwm cqn byrarcb cqjc yanbrmn xena cqnn, cx ydabdn cqn mjnvxw fqx
ljdbnm cqrb vrbnah, dwcru qn xa R bqjuu ynarbq rw vxacju lxwourlc.  Oxa
cqrb ydayxbn R fruu yanbnaen vh uron; cx ngnldcn cqrb mnja anenwpn fruu
R jpjrw knqxum cqn bdw jwm canjm cqn pannw qnakjpn xo njacq, fqrlq
xcqnafrbn bqxdum ejwrbq oaxv vh nhnb oxanena.  Jwm R ljuu xw hxd,
byrarcb xo cqn mnjm, jwm xw hxd, fjwmnarwp vrwrbcnab xo enwpnjwln, cx
jrm jwm lxwmdlc vn rw vh fxat.  Unc cqn ldabnm jwm qnuurbq vxwbcna
marwt mnny xo jpxwh; unc qrv onnu cqn mnbyjra cqjc wxf cxavnwcb vn."  R
qjm knpdw vh jmsdajcrxw frcq bxunvwrch jwm jw jfn fqrlq juvxbc jbbdanm
vn cqjc cqn bqjmnb xo vh vdamnanm oarnwmb qnjam jwm jyyaxenm vh
mnexcrxw, kdc cqn odarnb yxbbnbbnm vn jb R lxwludmnm, jwm ajpn lqxtnm
vh dccnajwln.

R fjb jwbfnanm cqaxdpq cqn bcruuwnbb xo wrpqc kh j uxdm jwm ornwmrbq
ujdpq.  Rc ajwp xw vh njab uxwp jwm qnjeruh; cqn vxdwcjrwb an-nlqxnm
rc, jwm R onuc jb ro juu qnuu bdaaxdwmnm vn frcq vxltnah jwm ujdpqcna.
Bdanuh rw cqjc vxvnwc R bqxdum qjen knnw yxbbnbbnm kh oanwih jwm qjen
mnbcaxhnm vh vrbnajkun ngrbcnwln kdc cqjc vh exf fjb qnjam jwm cqjc R
fjb anbnaenm oxa enwpnjwln.  Cqn ujdpqcna mrnm jfjh, fqnw j fnuu-twxfw
jwm jkqxaanm exrln, jyyjanwcuh luxbn cx vh nja, jmmanbbnm vn rw jw
jdmrkun fqrbyna, "R jv bjcrbornm, vrbnajkun fanclq!  Hxd qjen
mncnavrwnm cx uren, jwm R jv bjcrbornm."

R mjacnm cxfjamb cqn byxc oaxv fqrlq cqn bxdwm yaxlnnmnm, kdc cqn mneru
nudmnm vh pajby.  Bdmmnwuh cqn kaxjm mrbt xo cqn vxxw jaxbn jwm bqxwn
oduu dyxw qrb pqjbcuh jwm mrbcxacnm bqjyn jb qn ounm frcq vxan cqjw
vxacju bynnm.

R ydabdnm qrv, jwm oxa vjwh vxwcqb cqrb qjb knnw vh cjbt.  Pdrmnm kh j
burpqc ludn, R oxuuxfnm cqn frwmrwpb xo cqn Aqxwn, kdc ejrwuh.  Cqn
kudn Vnmrcnaajwnjw jyynjanm, jwm kh j bcajwpn lqjwln, R bjf cqn ornwm
